### [140] [REFACT: Adaptive Fact Restatement for Compact and Faithful Chain-of-Thought Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20833)
*Zhensheng Jin,Xin Dai,Zhenghao Liu,Chaojun Xiao,Huiyuan Xie,Yu Gu,Ge Yu,Maosong Sun*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: REFACT提出一种自适应的事实重述引用框架，通过训练模型判断推理步骤是否需要上下文支持以及以何种粒度重述源事实，从而避免推理失误和无差别复制事实。采用两阶段SFT-to-RL优化策略，引入引用效用奖励机制，确保引用事实完整、可追溯且足以支撑答案。在LongBench、LV-Eval和ConFiQA上的实验表明，REFACT显著提升长上下文问答与反事实忠实性，同时减少令牌消耗。分析显示，该方法以更少的重述事实保留更多答案相关证据，使推理轨迹更密集而非更冗长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于大语言模型的推理方法在证据稀疏、噪声或与参数知识冲突时，容易导致推理偏离上下文。现有的接地方法要么在生成后附加引用，要么鼓励在推理过程中检索证据，但无法保证引用内容对局部推理和最终答案的充分性。因此需要一种能动态决定何时及如何引用事实的机制，以提高推理的准确性和可信度。

Method: 提出REFACT框架，通过两阶段训练（SFT到强化学习）实现自适应的事实重述。模型学习判断每个推理步骤是否需要上下文支持，并决定引用事实的粒度。引入引用效用奖励，激励模型生成格式良好、可追溯且能充分支持答案的引用内容。

Result: 在LongBench、LV-Eval和ConFiQA数据集上，REFACT显著提升了长上下文问答性能和反事实忠实性，同时大幅降低令牌使用量。分析表明，其推理轨迹具有更高的信息密度，即用更少的事实重述保留了更多关键证据。

Conclusion: REFACT通过将引用转化为支撑答案的中间状态，有效解决了长推理中因证据不足或冲突导致的漂移问题，实现了更准确、高效且可解释的推理过程，为大语言模型的可信推理提供了新范式。

Abstract: Large language models increasingly rely on long-form reasoning for complex tasks, yet their reasoning traces may drift away from the supplied context when evidence is sparse, noisy, or in conflict with parametric knowledge. Existing grounding methods either attach citations after generation or encourage evidence retrieval inside the trace, but they often do not ensure that cited content is sufficient for the local inference and final answer. We propose REFACT, an adaptive fact-restatement citation framework that trains models to decide when a reasoning step needs contextual grounding and at what granularity source facts should be restated. This design avoids both unsupported inference and indiscriminate fact copying by turning citations into answer-supporting intermediate states. REFACT is optimized with a two-stage SFT-to-RL pipeline in which a citation-utility reward encourages cited facts to be well-formed, source-traceable, and answer-sufficient. Experiments on LongBench, LV-Eval, and ConFiQA show that REFACT improves long-context QA and counterfactual faithfulness while substantially reducing token consumption. Further analysis shows that REFACT preserves more answer-bearing evidence with fewer restated facts, yielding reasoning traces that are denser rather than longer. All code and data are available at https://github.com/NEUIR/REFACT.

</details>


### [141] [CSPF: A Constrained Shared-Private Fusion Method for Non-Verifiable Preference Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20862)
*Hehao Zhang,Danli Wang,Xinyuan Wang,Xuange Gao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出CSPF方法，通过融合不同冻结奖励模型的隐藏状态表示，在人类偏好监督下实现对非可验证任务的可靠评估。该方法将专家信号分解为共享与私有表示，促进跨专家对齐并保留互补观点，在多个基准测试中表现优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以充分捕捉非可验证任务中人类偏好的多样化评价标准，亟需更有效的融合机制来提升评估可靠性。

Method: CSPF将多个异构冻结奖励模型视为互补评估者，通过学习其隐藏状态表示，在成对人类偏好监督下进行融合；采用共享-私有分解结构，平衡一致性与多样性。

Result: 在LM-Arena目标域适应和PPE分布外偏好评估任务中，CSPF在主要指标上均优于单专家奖励模型、标量得分多专家及评分卡裁判等基线方法。

Conclusion: 融合隐藏状态表示能提供更丰富的偏好评估基础，为非可验证偏好任务构建集成评估信号提供了可行路径。

Abstract: At present, reliable evaluation of non-verifiable tasks remains challenging. Existing approaches often fail to adequately capture the diverse evaluative criteria underlying human preferences in such tasks. To this end, we propose Constrained Shared-Private Fusion (CSPF), a fusion method that treats heterogeneous frozen reward models as complementary evaluators and learns to integrate their hidden-state representations under pairwise human-preference supervision. CSPF decomposes each expert signal into shared and expert-private representations, encouraging cross-expert alignment while preserving complementary viewpoints. Across experiments on LM-Arena target-domain adaptation and PPE out-of-distribution preference evaluation, CSPF achieves the best performance on the primary metrics among the evaluated single-expert reward-model, scalar-score multi-expert, and rubric-judge baselines. Overall, CSPF suggests that fusing hidden-state representations provides a more expressive basis for preference assessment, offering a practical route toward integrated evaluative signals for non-verifiable preference tasks.

### [142] [LegalCiteTrust: Benchmarking Citation Trustworthiness in Chinese Long-Form Legal Research Reports](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20872)
*Yunhan Li,Mingjie Xie,Zeyang Shi,Gengshen Wu,Min Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LegalCiteTrust 是一个用于评估中文长篇法律研究报告中引用可信度的基准，涵盖72个密集标注的任务，从覆盖范围、支持力度和引用可信度三个维度进行评估。引用可信度通过存在性、忠实性和适用性（E/F/A）三个层面量化。实验表明，尽管检索工具能提升证据支持，但未必提高可信度评分；而基于E/F/A的修订能更显著提升可信度与最终评分。研究强调，生成可靠法律报告需在检索后实施以引用为中心的证据治理，确保法律依据被准确选择、描述和应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前长篇法律研究报告依赖大语言模型和智能研究系统，但其可靠性不仅取决于任务完成情况，还取决于引用的法律权威是否可信。即使引用了真实来源，也可能因遗漏限制条件、错误描述或过度引申而产生风险。因此需要一个专门评估引用可信度的基准，以推动更可靠的法律研究自动化。

Method: 提出LegalCiteTrust基准，包含72个报告级任务，从覆盖范围、支持力度和引用可信度三方面评估。引用可信度通过存在性（Existence）、忠实性（Fidelity）和适用性（Applicability）三个子维度进行操作化定义，并对不同系统（通用LLM、深度研究系统、法律专用系统）进行实验比较。

Result: 实验发现：任务完成度、证据丰富度、引用密度与引用可靠性反映出系统行为差异；检索工具虽可增强证据支持，但无法稳定提升可信度；而基于E/F/A的修订策略比仅检查存在性的过滤更能有效提升可信度与最终得分。

Conclusion: 可信法律研究生成不仅需要获取法律依据，还需在检索后实施以引用为中心的证据治理，确保引用的法律权威被准确选择、描述和应用，才能真正实现高可信度输出。

Abstract: Long-form legal research reports increasingly rely on LLMs and agentic research systems, but their reliability depends not only on answering the task, but also on whether cited legal authorities are trustworthy. A citation can be risky even when it points to a real source: the report may omit limiting conditions, misdescribe the authority, or use it to support a stronger claim than the source allows. We introduce LegalCiteTrust, a benchmark for evaluating citation trustworthiness in Chinese long-form legal research reports. It contains 72 densely annotated report-level tasks and evaluates reports along three dimensions: Coverage, Support, and Citation Trustworthiness. Citation Trustworthiness is operationalized through citation-level Existence, Fidelity, and Applicability (E/F/A). Experiments on general-purpose LLMs, deep-research systems, and legal-specific systems show that task completion, evidence richness, citation density, and citation reliability expose different system behaviors. Retrieval tools can improve evidence support without reliably improving the Trust score, while E/F/A-based revision improves Trust and Final score more clearly than existence-only filtering. These results suggest that trustworthy legal research generation requires citation-aware evidence governance after retrieval: systems must not only retrieve legal authorities, but also select, describe, and apply them reliably.

Result: 构建了涵盖四类工作领域的评估基准，任务具备防搜索污染特性，支持跨模型公平比较，提供可复现、可审计的评估环境，报告了多个模型在不同子集上的表现榜单。

Rather than adapting public issue text, every task is reverse-engineered from a real commit, pull request, or business scenario and rewritten as a short, colloquial, role-played request, so that a task's prompt is not recoverable by web-searching the underlying issue, pull request, or commit thread. Because the dataset is released openly - task directories, environment images, evaluation harness, tests, and reference solutions - contamination resistance rests on this construction together with dataset versioning rather than on secrecy. The four subsets - repository-level engineering, front-end development, office and business workflows, and red-/blue-team security - probe complementary facets of real work, each with its own verification style. All are packaged in a uniform task-directory format and run, under a uniform and reproducible protocol, on two agent harnesses (CodeBuddy Code and Claude Code); the full open release makes the benchmark reproducible end to end and directly auditable, since any third party can re-run each task and inspect its content. Because each subset uses a different scoring instrument, scores are not comparable across subsets and the suite reports no suite-wide average. We report a cross-model leaderboard across several model families.

TL;DR: 本文探讨了现有基于词典的仇恨言论检测方法在测量怨恨情绪时的局限性，提出使用上下文理解模型替代简单的词项匹配，并在多语言非循环基准上验证其有效性。结果显示，上下文阅读模型显著提升了对隐含、引用和跨句怨恨的识别精度，尤其在词典未覆盖的情况下表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有词典法（如Grievance Dictionary）依赖词项匹配，无法处理语义复杂情况（如否定、引用、谴责），且评估数据常被词典自身选择规则污染，导致结果虚高。需要更准确、更诚实的测量方式。

Method: 保留原词典22个构念分类体系，但用上下文感知的语言模型取代词项匹配；构建一个五语言、2000项的非循环评估集，包含无条件随机、词典正向与负向三类文本，以避免评估偏差。

Result: 上下文阅读模型在词典负向文本上的平均精度从0.14提升至0.20，尤其在隐含、引用和跨句表达中提升显著；原词典的宏AUROC 0.686因评估偏差实际仅为0.500。

Conclusion: 怨恨情绪应通过理解上下文而非简单词项匹配来更准确、更公正地测量，建议采用上下文模型并使用独立于词典选择的数据进行评估。代码与数据已开源。

Abstract: Grievance is one of the warning signs analysts look for when assessing threats of violence. It is increasingly measured at scale from online text, most often with word-level lexicons like the Grievance Dictionary that score by matching weighted terms. Such matching is a fast and transparent proxy, but it cannot resolve whether a term is asserted, quoted, negated, or condemned. These lexicons are also often evaluated on pools enriched with the very examples they retrieve, so a high score partly reflects agreement with the lexicon's own selection rule. Examining a five-language, 2{,}000-item evaluation pool, we find its halves separated almost perfectly by the lexicon itself: every item labeled ``random'' is in fact lexicon-negative, so the lexicon's apparent macro-AUROC of 0.686 collapses to a 0.500 floor fixed by construction. We keep the dictionary's 22-construct ontology but replace term matching with context-reading models, evaluated on a non-circular benchmark that separates unconditional-random, lexicon-positive, and lexicon-negative strata across five languages. Reading the full post rather than the target sentence alone helps most where the lexicon is silent, raising average precision on lexicon-negative text from 0.14 to 0.20, with the largest gains on quoted, implicit, and cross-sentence grievance. Together, these results show that grievance is measured more faithfully by reading the surrounding context, and more honestly when tested on text the lexicon did not select. We release our code and benchmark at https://github.com/behavioral-ds/multilingual_grievance.

Yet, current large language models (LLMs) appear to be capable of doing it. We investigate whether this animacy-sensitive behavior of LLMs can be traced to a localized set of causally relevant components and connections. To do so, we construct a controlled dataset of minimal pairs and perform circuit discovery on four open-weight models. Through in-depth experiments and ablations, we show that a causal mechanism responsible for handling animacy in these models does exist, thus discovering an animacy circuit. ### [147] [Sample-Efficient Learning from Agent Experience](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21051)
*Chenhui Gou,Haoqin Tu,Yunhao Fang,Jianfei Cai,Hamid Rezatofighi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为经验蒸馏（Experience Distillation）的新方法，旨在解决智能体在真实世界中因环境交互成本高而受限的问题。该方法通过将智能体自身交互历史中的信息内化到模型权重中，实现了无需额外环境交互即可保留大部分基于上下文学习的性能增益。实验表明，在749个软件工程任务和6个文本冒险游戏中，该方法可保留至少64.8%的上下文学习收益，远超直接监督微调（仅3.8%）和传统强化学习基线（需至少9.6倍更少样本）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界中的智能体学习受限于昂贵的环境交互（如耗时实验或人工反馈）。虽然上下文学习能高效利用历史经验，但其效果依赖于上下文存在；而现有知识蒸馏方法难以在不牺牲样本效率的前提下应用于交互历史。因此，亟需一种能将上下文信息永久内化且无需额外交互的方法。

Method: 提出经验蒸馏框架，通过将智能体的历史交互数据作为输入，训练模型将上下文信息压缩并固化到参数中，实现无须再依赖原始上下文即可保持高性能。该过程完全基于已有经验，不需进一步环境交互。

Result: 在软件工程任务和文本冒险游戏上，经验蒸馏保留了至少64.8%的上下文学习性能增益；相比之下，监督微调仅恢复3.8%；与经典强化学习相比，该方法以至少9.6倍更少的环境样本达到相当性能。

Conclusion: 经验蒸馏成功实现了对上下文学习优势的持久化，显著降低对环境交互的依赖，为高效、低成本的真实世界智能体学习提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Real-world agent learning is often constrained by costly environment interactions, such as running time-consuming experiments or obtaining human feedback. In-context learning offers a highly sample-efficient way for agents to learn from their own interaction histories, but its gains disappear once that experience is removed from the context. Separately, context distillation provides a mechanism for internalizing contextual information into model weights. However, applying it to agents' interaction histories without sacrificing environment sample efficiency remains underexplored. We term this problem Experience Distillation and develop an implementation that requires no further environment interaction beyond the collected experience. Experiments on 749 curated software-engineering tasks and six text-adventure games show that it retains at least 64.8\% of the gains from in-context learning across both domains, whereas direct supervised fine-tuning on the collected experience recovers only 3.8\%. Compared with classical reinforcement-learning baselines, in-context learning from trial-and-error experience followed by Experience Distillation matches their performance with at least \(9.6\times\) fewer environment samples.

### [148] [QuantiBias: Benchmarking Quantization-Induced Bias in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21063)
*Emilio Ferrara*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 量化虽提升效率，但显著增加模型在开放式生成中的偏见，且标准安全评估无法捕捉此问题。提出QuantiBias基准，通过多语言、生成式探针与控制实验，发现量化后模型在开放问答中约24%-27%的回答包含刻板印象，且不同模型家族对推理前后的敏感性不一，需重新评估量化模型的开放生成偏见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型普遍经过量化以提升效率，但其安全性常被假设为无损；然而本文发现量化会引入未被标准评估检测到的开放式生成偏见，亟需新方法识别和衡量该风险。

Method: 提出QuantiBias基准，结合多语言生成式刻板印象探测任务，对比量化前后模型在拒绝、多选与开放生成中的表现，引入推理前后条件控制，并由独立评判者评估内容严重性。

Result: 量化模型在开放式回答中表现出显著偏见（24%-27%含刻板印象），尽管在拒绝和多选任务中表现正常；不同模型家族对推理前后的敏感性差异明显，部分家族经推理可减半偏见，另一些则无改善。

Conclusion: 量化过程虽不影响传统安全指标，但会加剧开放生成中的偏见，因此量化后的模型必须重新评估其开放生成偏差，不能仅依赖现有短形式安全测试。

Abstract: Almost every large language model that reaches a broad audience is quantized: trained in full precision, then compressed for efficiency. This step is assumed harmless and its safety is rarely re-checked. We find its principal side effect is increased bias that standard safety evaluation misses. Holding the model, its training, and the prompts fixed, a quantized model still refuses harmful requests, still avoids over-refusing benign prompts, and still selects the unbiased multiple-choice answer. Yet asked an open-ended question, the same model volunteers stereotypes in all eight languages we probe, in roughly one in four open-ended answers under an independent judge (~24% to ~27% across the compression ladder): it passes every standard check and still reaches users measurably more biased. The selective gap is a robust finding; whether open-ended bias further increases with compression is less certain, sensitive to the judge that scores it. We address both with \textbf{QuantiBias}, a benchmark that pairs a generative, multilingual stereotype probe with the refusal and multiple-choice controls that isolate open-ended generation, contrasts each build with and without reasoning, and rates the content severity of what it generates. Across two backbone models (Qwen and Gemma), a five-family screen, and eight benchmarks, quantizers allocate their extra precision by capability data that carries no bias-prevention signal, and reasoning before answering roughly halves the effect on some families while doing nothing on others. A quantized build must be re-evaluated for open-ended bias, not only on the short-form safeguards it already passes.

</details>


### [149] [PrefReward: Learning User Preference Matrix for Personalized Text Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21067)
*Yue Wu,Chengbing Wang,Yimeng Bai,Xiaoyan Zhao,Yang Zhang,Fuli Feng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出PrefReward框架，通过显式建模用户偏好矩阵并将其作为解码过程中的奖励信号，提升生成内容的个性化质量与可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有个性化方法依赖模型参数中的隐式表示，难以解释用户偏好且处理长上下文依赖能力弱。

Method: 分两阶段：(1) 提取用户特定的偏好矩阵以总结个人风格倾向；(2) 使用基于KL散度的奖励函数引导生成过程。

Result: 在LongLaMP数据集上的实验表明，PrefReward在生成质量与个性化可解释性方面均优于非个性化及基于检索的基线方法。

Conclusion: PrefReward通过显式建模用户偏好，有效提升了生成内容的个性化表现与可解释性，为长文本生成中的个性化问题提供了新思路。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable ability in generating personalized content by leveraging user histories and contextual cues. However, most existing personalization approaches rely on implicit representations within model parameters, making it difficult to interpret user-specific preferences or effectively handle long-context dependencies. To address these challenges, we propose PrefReward, a novel preference-aware generative framework that explicitly models user styles through a structured preference matrix and integrates it into the decoding process as a reward signal. PrefReward consists of two stages: (1) extracting a user-specific preference matrix that summarizes individual stylistic tendencies, and (2) using the matrix to guide generation via a KL-divergence-based reward function. Experiments on the LongLaMP dataset show that PrefReward outperforms non-personalized and retrieval-based baselines in both generation quality and personalization interpretability.

</details>


### [150] [One More Turn, Less Regret: A Regret-Based Multi-Turn Benchmark for LLMs' Clarification Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21143)
*Minh Ngoc Ta,My Anh Tran Nguyen,Duong D. Nguyen,Yuxia Wang,Preslav Nakov*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: RegretBench 是一个用于评估对话式大模型澄清行为的多轮基准测试，将澄清视为策略性决策过程，而非孤立的问题质量评估。它通过隐藏意图设定模糊性，支持基于语义状态跟踪的自由交互，并引入基于遗憾度的评估目标，衡量模型相对于参考澄清策略所损失的价值。实验表明，仅关注最终成功率不足，模型在效率、鲁棒性和停止决策上差异显著。该基准从意图解析、交互成本、无效澄清和遗憾度等多维度揭示模型是否高效且有意义地进行澄清。有效澄清不仅需要合理问题，更需适时提问并及时停止。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将澄清视为孤立问题质量评估，忽略了其作为序列决策的本质。用户请求的模糊性常隐含真实意图，模型需在多轮交互中判断何时提问、问什么、何时停止，因此需要一种能衡量澄清策略整体表现的新评估框架。

Method: 提出 RegretBench 基准，采用隐藏意图设定模糊性，支持自由形式交互与语义状态追踪，并设计基于遗憾度的目标函数，量化模型在澄清过程中相对于理想策略所损失的价值。

Result: 实验显示，即使模型在准确率上相近，其交互效率、对用户行为的鲁棒性及停止决策能力差异显著。RegretBench 能有效识别出哪些模型真正实现了高效、有意义的澄清。

Conclusion: 有效的澄清不仅是提出合理问题，更要求在正确时机提问并在意图明确后及时停止。仅靠最终成功无法全面评价模型的澄清能力，必须结合交互成本与遗憾度等综合指标。

Abstract: Ambiguous user requests make clarification a sequential decision problem for conversational LLM assistants: they must decide whether to ask, what to ask, when to stop, and when to answer. We introduce RegretBench, a multi-turn benchmark that evaluates clarification as policy behavior rather than isolated question quality. RegretBench provides a hidden-intent formulation of ambiguity, supports free-form interaction grounded in semantic-state tracking, and introduces a regret-based objective that measures how much value a model loses relative to a reference clarification policy. Experiments on open-domain QA and product recommendation scenarios show that final success alone is insufficient, as models with similar accuracy can differ substantially in efficiency, robustness to user behaviors, and stopping decisions. By jointly measuring intent resolution, interaction cost, ineffective clarification, and regret, RegretBench reveals whether models clarify usefully and efficiently. Our results show that effective clarification requires more than plausible questions: models must ask the right question at the right time and stop once the user's intended meaning is clear.

</details>


### [151] [Progressive Cramming: Reliable Token Compression and What It Reveals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21231)
*Dmitrii Tarasov,Timofei Lashukov,Elizaveta Goncharova,Andrey Kuznetsov*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出渐进式压缩（progressive cramming），通过逐令牌增长目标前缀，直到在固定优化预算内无法实现重建为止。结果发现压缩轨迹在嵌入空间中呈现低维结构；即使保留原始前缀，预加压缩嵌入也会导致多项选择基准上的准确率轻微但稳定下降，并在生成评估中几乎完全丧失能力。因果注意力剔除干预表明，这种退化源于模型早期层中嵌入的交互作用。研究认为，完美重建虽可通过脆弱的操控实现，但不足以代表有意义的压缩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究序列压缩中的极限问题，特别是现有方法在固定令牌预算和高精度阈值下，残差误差是否源于优化不足或根本性限制。

Method: 提出渐进式压缩方法，逐步增加目标前缀长度，直至无法在给定优化预算内完成重建。结合嵌入空间分析、多任务基准测试与因果注意力干预，研究压缩过程对模型性能的影响。

Result: 压缩轨迹具有低维结构；预加压缩嵌入导致多项选择任务准确率下降，生成任务能力几乎完全崩溃；退化主要源于模型早期层的嵌入交互。

Conclusion: 完美重建仅依赖于脆弱的控制机制，而非可迁移的语义，因此不足以构成有意义的压缩。渐进式压缩为研究压缩极限提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Token cramming compresses sequences into learned embeddings with near-perfect reconstruction, but fixed token budgets and 99\% accuracy thresholds leave it unclear whether residual errors reflect optimization failures or fundamental limits. We introduce progressive cramming, which grows the target prefix token-by-token, stopping only when reconstruction is no longer achievable within a fixed optimization budget. Progressive trajectories occupy low-dimensional structure in embedding space. Prepending a crammed embedding causes a moderate but consistent accuracy drop on multiple-choice benchmarks even with the original prefix in context, and collapses capability almost entirely under generative evaluation. Causal attention-knockout interventions trace this degradation to the embedding's interactions in the model's early layers. These results position progressive cramming as a tool for studying compression limits and show that perfect reconstruction - achievable through brittle steering rather than transferable semantics - is insufficient for meaningful compression.

</details>


### [152] [slang.gr as a Large-Scale Crowdsourced Resource for Non-Standard Greek](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21255)
*Panagiotis Papadakos,Katerina Papantoniou,Dimitris Plexousakis*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究首次对希腊语非标准语言（slang.gr）进行了大规模计算分析，构建了一个结合词汇、用户标签和互动数据的众包词典，并通过多层结构化分类体系对非规范标签进行映射。研究发现希腊语俚语以人物相关和评价性语言为核心，具有高度形态创造力，且参与者分布极不均衡，生命周期短且社区重叠严重。基于此，提出一种融合用户角色、互动模式和审核信号的社区置信度评分机制，显著提升定义可信度评估能力。结果表明，基于分类体系的表示方法在保持行为结构的同时增强了可解释性，为非标准语言的计算研究、社会语言学自然语言处理、偏见分析及大模型中非正式语言研究提供了重要资源与基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 俚语是日常语言的核心组成部分，体现语言创造力、社会身份和文化变迁，但其动态性和非标准化特征使其难以进行计算建模。现有研究缺乏对非标准语言的大规模系统性分析工具，尤其在希腊语等非主流语言中更为匮乏。因此，亟需建立一个结构化的计算资源来支持对俚语的语言学和社会行为特征的深入研究。

Method: 1. 构建slang.gr：一个众包的希腊语非标准语言词典，包含词汇条目、用户生成标签和互动数据；2. 设计多层结构化分类体系，将嘈杂的标签映射到包含语义类别和社会语言学元数据的层级分类中；3. 采用统计与网络分析方法，探索俚语的语言结构与贡献者社区的行为模式；4. 提出社区置信度评分机制，整合用户角色、互动频率、参与时间及内容审核信号，量化定义的可信度；5. 对比不同表示方式在可解释性与行为结构保留方面的表现。

Result: 1. 希腊语俚语高度集中于人物相关与评价性表达，表现出强烈的形态创新性；2. 贡献者社区呈现显著的长尾分布，多数用户活跃期短，但存在大量重叠的子社区；3. 社区置信度评分能有效区分高质量与低质量定义，优于传统基于频率的方法；4. 结构化分类体系在提升可解释性的同时，仍能捕捉关键行为特征，适用于后续分析。

Conclusion: 本研究成功建立了slang.gr作为首个面向非标准希腊语的计算资源，揭示了俚语的语言与社会动态特征。通过引入结构化分类与社区置信度机制，不仅提升了分析的可解释性，也为未来社会语言学自然语言处理、偏见检测以及大语言模型中非正式语言的理解奠定了坚实基础。

Abstract: Slang is a central component of everyday language, reflecting linguistic creativity, social identity, and cultural change, yet its dy- namic and non-standard nature makes it difficult to model computationally. We present the first large-scale computational study of slang.gr, a crowdsourced lexicon of Greek non-standard language, combining lexical content, user-generated tags, and interaction data. To enable the systematic analysis, we map noisy folksonomic tags to a structured multi-layer taxonomy capturing both semantic categories and sociolinguistic metadata. Using this representation, we analyze the linguistic structure of Greek slang and the behavior of its contributor community. We find that slang is strongly centered on person-related and evaluative language, exhibits high morphological creativity, and is shaped by highly skewed participation with short user lifespans and overlapping communities. Building on these signals, we introduce a community-based confidence score for definitions that integrates user roles, interaction patterns, and moderation signals. Our results show that taxonomy-based representations improve interpretability while retaining meaningful aspects of behavioral structure, enabling a more structured and interpretable analysis of confidence signals. Overall, this work establishes slang.gr as a computational resource for non-standard Greek and provides a foundation for sociolinguistic NLP, bias analysis, and the study of informal language in LLMs.

### [153] [A Comparative Evaluation of Embeddings and LLMs in a Greek Book Publisher Setting - The CUP Dataset](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21274)
*Katerina Papantoniou,Panagiotis Papadakos,Theodore Patkos,Dimitris Garefalakis,Nikos Vardakis,Dimitris Plexousakis*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CUP 是一个希腊语书籍检索基准，包含 868 条目录记录和 104 个专家标注的查询，涵盖分级相关性判断。评估了稀疏（BM25）、密集（sentence-transformers）、混合及基于大模型的方法。多语言嵌入优于希腊语专用模型，混合检索表现最佳。分析显示，BM25 在命名实体查询中表现优异，而密集与混合方法在自然语言、噪声、跨语言和概念查询中更优。字段感知提示对不同模型效果各异，LLM 的目录摘要提升仅基于目录的检索，而 LLM 后过滤虽提升早期检索但成本高昂。整体上，CUP 支持对希腊语检索在词汇、语义、噪声及跨语言查询中的真实世界评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为希腊语书籍检索提供一个全面、真实世界的评估基准，涵盖多种查询类型（如命名实体、自然语言、跨语言、概念查询），以评估不同检索方法的性能，填补现有资源在多语言和复杂查询场景下的空白。

Method: 构建包含 868 条目录记录和 104 个专家标注查询的 CUP 基准；采用 BM25、sentence-transformers、混合检索及基于大模型的检索方法进行实验；通过查询级分析比较各方法在不同查询类型下的表现；引入字段感知提示、目录摘要和后过滤等技术优化检索效果。

Result: 多语言嵌入优于希腊语专用模型；混合检索在整体表现上最优；BM25 在命名实体查询中表现突出；密集与混合方法在自然语言、噪声、跨语言和概念查询中更具优势；字段感知提示效果因模型而异；LLM 目录摘要提升仅基于目录的检索；LLM 后过滤显著提升早期检索但代价高。

Conclusion: CUP 为希腊语书籍检索提供了有效的评估框架，支持对多种查询类型的系统性测试，揭示了不同检索方法的适用场景，推动了多语言信息检索的发展。

Abstract: We present CUP, a Greek book retrieval benchmark consisting of 868 catalog records and 104 expert-annotated queries with graded relevance judgments. We evaluate sparse (BM25), dense (sentence-transformers), hybrid, and LLM-assisted retrieval methods in this book-search setting. Multilingual embeddings outperform Greek-specific models, while hybrid retrieval performs best overall. A query-level analysis shows that BM25 excels at named-entity queries, while dense and hybrid methods improve natural-language, noisy, cross-lingual, and concept queries. Field-aware prompting has model-specific effects, while LLM TOC summarization improves TOC-only retrieval and LLM post-filtering improves early-stage retrieval at a high cost. Overall, CUP enables real-world evaluation of Greek retrieval across lexical, semantic, noisy, and cross-lingual queries.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have developed rapidly and become valuable tools in everyday life. However, how to align LLMs to a particular set of human values is still an open problem. Recent studies show that instruction tuning has strong potential for zero-shot tasks and may serve as an effective approach to addressing value alignment. Nevertheless, although many datasets for instruction tuning already exist, they are not specifically designed around moral scenarios and behaviors. We construct a unified moral-value dataset that can be directly used for instruction tuning. This dataset is built upon existing moral-value datasets by merging them into a unified corpus and converting them into an instruction-response format. We show that training on a mixed dataset combining general task datasets with our dataset preserves general-task performance, and we report preliminary observations on how the mixing ratio affects value-oriented task performance. Our work provides a moral-value dataset for instruction tuning and offers a useful resource for further alignment research. ### [155] [news-crawler-LM: A Small Long-Context Model For High-Quality News Crawling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21284)
*Pascal Stolzenburg,Jonas Golde,Max Dallabetta,Alan Akbik*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为news-crawler-LM的小型长上下文语言模型，专门用于从新闻网页中提取结构化内容。该模型在高质量、人工验证的Fundus新闻爬取库上进行微调，能够将原始HTML转换为纯文本和结构化JSON（如标题、作者、发布日期、正文等）。实验表明，在HTML到Markdown和HTML到JSON的提取任务中，news-crawler-LM显著优于现有基线方法，分别在BLEU和METEOR指标上提升4.8/6.1和2.2/4.1；但在未见过的出版商上的纯文本提取任务中，性能仅略优于规则解析工具。所有模型与资源均已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Fundus新闻爬取库中的高质量人工标注数据，对小型长上下文语言模型进行微调，使其能将原始HTML直接转化为结构化文本与JSON格式输出。

Abstract: Extracting structured content from news pages remains challenging due to heterogeneous HTML layouts, inconsistent markup, and substantial boilerplate such as navigation elements and advertisements. Rule-based news crawlers can achieve high extraction accuracy by encoding site-specific structure, but require manual configuration in order to generalize to new publishers. Large language models provide a more flexible alternative by reducing the need for handcrafted rules, but their high computational cost limits practical deployment. In this paper, we introduce news-crawler-LM, a small long-context language model fine-tuned on high-quality, human-validated extractions from the Fundus news-crawling library. Our model converts raw HTML into plaintext and structured JSON, including fields such as headline, author, publication date, and article body. In our experiments, news-crawler-LM outperforms strong baselines in HTML-to-Markdown and HTML-to-JSON extraction, improving performance by +4.8 BLEU and +6.1 METEOR in the HTML-to-Markdown task, and by +2.2 BLEU and +4.1 METEOR in the HTML-to-JSON task. However, we also observe that our model only slightly better compared to other rule-based parsing libraries on the HTML-to-plaintext task in evaluations on previously unseen publishers. We release all models and artifacts to the research community.

</details>


### [156] [Adaptive Depth Sparse Framework: Similarity-Driven Resource Allocation for Pre-Trained LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21291)
*Yidu Wu,Xiang Wang,Kejie Zhao,Zhangchi Wang,Qinghai Guo,Xiaoying Tang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需重新训练即可将预训练大语言模型转换为稀疏深度模型的自适应深度稀疏框架（AdaDSF）。该方法基于各层输入与输出隐藏状态之间的余弦相似度，动态分配每层的令牌保留率，并通过轻量级路由器选择关键信息令牌，同时引入特征保持对齐目标以保证稀疏模型与密集模型在中间层和最终表示上的一致性。在GPT-NeoX和Qwen2.5上的实验表明，AdaDSF显著降低推理计算量（FLOPs），同时保持接近密集模型的性能，在相同稀疏度下优于MoD、D-LLM和DLO等强基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有加速方法通常依赖任务特定的微调或从头训练，导致适配成本高且跨任务通用性差。需要一种无需重新训练即可高效加速大语言模型的方法。

Method: 基于层间输入输出隐藏状态的余弦相似度，动态计算每层的令牌保留比例；设计轻量级路由机制选择重要令牌；引入特征保持对齐损失，使稀疏模型的中间和最终表示逼近密集模型。

Result: 在语言建模和常识推理任务上，AdaDSF在大幅降低推理FLOPs的同时，保持了接近密集模型的性能，在相同稀疏度下相比MoD、D-LLM和DLO等基线方法表现出更小的精度下降。

Conclusion: AdaDSF是一种高效、通用的无重训练稀疏化框架，可有效降低大语言模型的推理开销，同时保持高性能，具备良好的跨任务适用性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) achieve strong generation and reasoning performance, but the Transformer architecture incurs high inference cost. Existing acceleration methods often rely on task-specific fine-tuning or training from scratch, increasing adaptation cost and limiting cross-task usability. We present an Adaptive Depth Sparse Framework (AdaDSF) that converts off-the-shelf pre-trained LLMs into depth-sparse models without full retraining. Our key insight is that layers contribute unequally to representation transformation, characterized by the cosine similarity between layer input and output hidden states. Based on this, AdaDSF assigns layer-wise token retention ratios from similarity statistics, uses a lightweight router to select informative tokens at each layer, and introduces a feature-preserving alignment objective to match intermediate and final representations between sparse and dense models. On GPT-NeoX and Qwen2.5 over language modeling and commonsense reasoning, AdaDSF substantially reduces inference FLOPs while preserving performance close to dense counterparts. Under comparable sparsity, AdaDSF consistently yields smaller accuracy degradation than strong baselines including MoD, D-LLM, and DLO.

### [157] [GRADRAG: Cross-Component Prompt Adaptation for Coordinated Multi-Agent RAG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21324)
*Paolo Pedinotti,Enrico Santus*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: GRADRAG 是一个用于多智能体检索增强生成（RAG）系统的跨组件提示优化框架，通过将 RAG 管道建模为计算图，利用结构化评估反馈迭代更新上游组件。其核心包括评估器（Evaluator）与提示优化器（Prompt Optimizer），前者对答案和证据进行批判性评价并生成可操作反馈，后者据此优化检索器、图构造器和回答器等智能体。评估器还支持早期停止机制。在 SQUALITY 与 QMSUM 基准上，无论采用扁平块检索还是基于图的检索，GRADRAG 均显著优于仅优化生成器的一次性优化基线，提升达 12-15 个百分点，在两次迭代内即实现大部分性能增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 RAG 系统中多智能体的优化通常孤立进行，缺乏端到端的协同改进机制。为解决这一问题，本文提出 GRADRAG 框架，旨在通过统一反馈机制实现跨组件的协同优化，提升整体系统性能。

Method: 将 RAG 管道建模为计算图，设计评估器（Evaluator）对下游输出进行结构化评价，生成可操作反馈；由提示优化器（Prompt Optimizer）利用该反馈迭代更新上游各智能体（如检索器、图构造器、回答器）。同时引入早期停止策略，当输出质量达标时终止优化流程。

Result: 在 SQUALITY 与 QMSUM 基准上，无论使用扁平块检索或图结构检索，GRADRAG 均显著优于仅优化生成器的一次性优化方法，在 LLM 判定的成对比较中取得 12-15 个百分点的净偏好优势，且多数性能提升可在两轮迭代内达成。

Conclusion: GRADRAG 通过跨组件反馈与迭代优化，有效提升了多智能体 RAG 系统的整体表现，证明了协同优化机制在复杂生成管道中的关键作用。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems increasingly employ multiple LLM agents. Yet, most prior work optimizes components in isolation rather than coordinating improvements across the pipeline. We introduce GRADRAG, a framework for cross-component prompt adaptation that models the RAG pipeline as a computational graph and propagates structured evaluation feedback to update upstream agents. An Evaluator critiques downstream answers and supporting evidence, producing actionable feedback that a Prompt Optimizer uses to iteratively update adaptive agents, such as retrievers, graph constructors, and answerers. The Evaluator also triggers early stopping when the output is deemed satisfactory. We evaluate GRADRAG on the SQUALITY and QMSUM benchmarks under two retrieval paradigms: flat chunk-based retrieval using IRCoT-style query refinement (Trivedi et al., 2023), and graph-based retrieval that constructs and iteratively enriches an entity-relation graph from the document. Across both settings, GRADRAG consistently outperforms one-step refinement baselines that update only the final generator, achieving a 12-15 percentage point net preference margin in LLM-judged pairwise comparisons, with most gains realized within two refinement iterations.

Second, that gap concentrates on retrieval (2.23) and synthesis (2.15), not extraction (0.84). Third, Decision Usefulness shows the widest cross-model dispersion of any dimension (4.0 points on issuer profiling) and top-tier inter-judge agreement (mean r = 0.52).
  Plausibility is cheap. Bankability is the bar.

### [162] [Anti-Periodic Positional Encoding: Möbius Boundary Conditions Make In-Context Retrieval Reliable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21405)
*Ji Ho Bae*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Möbius RoPE introduces an anti-periodic positional encoding using odd multiples of π in frequency ladder, creating deterministic coupling between sequence ends via a Dirichlet dipole. It achieves superior needle-in-a-haystack retrieval (90.3% vs. 63.3%) with low variance (p=0.013–0.029), outperforming periodic and aperiodic baselines. Hybrid models maintain baseline perplexity while improving reliability; swapping back to standard RoPE collapses retrieval, confirming dependence on long-range geometry. Only anti-periodic hybrid offers both low perplexity and high retrieval robustness.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To improve long-range dependency modeling and retrieval reliability in Transformers by introducing a novel anti-periodic boundary condition in positional encoding, addressing the unreliability of standard RoPE in needle-in-a-haystack tasks.

Method: Propose Möbius RoPE with anti-periodic frequency ladder θ_i = π(2i+1)/N, enabling holonomy -1 and closed-form Dirichlet dipole coupling. Evaluate via numerical verification, pretraining 48 models across 160M/410M classes, comparing hybrid, standard, NoPE, and swapped variants.

Result: Hybrid Möbius RoPE maintains perplexity (29.66 vs. 29.72) but boosts retrieval accuracy to 90.3±5.7% at context 512 (vs. 63.3±31.4%), with robust statistical significance (p=0.013–0.040). Aperiodic and periodic baselines fail to replicate the effect. Swapping to standard RoPE collapses retrieval, especially for far needles. Anti-periodic hybrid uniquely balances low perplexity and high retrieval reliability.

Conclusion: Möbius RoPE provides a zero-cost enhancement to Transformer performance: it preserves training stability while drastically improving retrieval reliability through anti-periodic positional geometry, offering a robust solution to the 'needle-in-a-haystack' problem without increasing model complexity.

Abstract: Möbius RoPE is a rotary positional encoding built on the anti-periodic frequency ladder $θ_i=π(2i+1)/N$: every rotation plane advances by an odd multiple of $π$ across the training context, so the positional holonomy is $-1$ and the two ends of the sequence are deterministically coupled through a closed-form Dirichlet "dipole"; to our knowledge this is the first anti-periodic boundary condition in positional encoding. We verify the theory numerically to $\sim 10^{-6}$ and pretrain 48 models spanning six 160M-class and three 410M-class arms (2B FineWeb-Edu tokens each; the hybrid arm puts Möbius frequencies on 25% of heads). Hybrid perplexity is unchanged (29.66 vs. 29.72), but needle-in-a-haystack retrieval becomes reliable: $90.3\pm5.7\%$ versus $63.3\pm31.4\%$ at context 512 ($n=6$ seeds), observed worst seed 86% versus 14%, robust variance tests $p=0.013$-$0.029$ (unadjusted), recurring at 410M (Levene $p=0.040$). Matched controls isolate the mechanism: an aperiodic ladder in the same frequency band reproduces none of the effect, and a periodic (holonomy $+1$) ladder only a fraction. Swapping trained models' frequency table back to standard RoPE (weights frozen) collapses retrieval, with damage concentrated on far needles: trained models depend on this long-range geometry. A NoPE arm is even more reliable at short context but pays a 13% perplexity tax and extrapolates worst; only the anti-periodic hybrid pairs baseline perplexity with a high reliability floor. The effect is scoped to single-needle retrieval within the training window; a one-line frequency swap thus provides zero-cost insurance against the retrieval seed lottery.

</details>

Abstract: Recent advancements in automated audio captioning (AAC) have shifted from monolithic sentence generation toward structured formats that explicitly disentangle distinct acoustic and semantic properties. However, evaluating this heterogeneous data remains a significant challenge. Existing caption metrics focus on flat textual outputs and fail to reliably assess multimodal attributes. To bridge this gap, we propose a multi-axis evaluation framework tailored for structured audio descriptions. Our approach combines Large Language Model (LLM) judges to capture semantic nuance with deterministic computational metrics to precisely measure acoustic deviations. ### [164] [Token Budget Saturation and Mechanistic Early Detection of Reasoning Non-Convergence in Chain-of-Thought Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21433)
*Renuka Oladri,Niveda Jawahar,Abdirisak Mohamed*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究发现，链式思维模型在推理时存在二元收敛模式：要么在有限的词元预算内完成推理（收敛），要么耗尽预算仍未得出结论（非收敛）。实验表明，收敛生成的准确率高达90.3%（AIME 1983-2024），而非收敛仅为6.6%，整体收敛率为62.0%。研究进一步探索是否能在思考链早期通过模型内部表示预测收敛结果。通过在第50至300个词元位置训练线性探测器，发现第20层在第150个词元处的激活值可达到AUC 0.608（±0.080，五折交叉验证），显著高于随机水平，且在第50个词元已具备一定预测能力。相比基于词元熵和重复统计的行为基线，激活探测器表现更优。全范围置换检验得到p=0.063（10万次置换），表明存在微弱但可能有意义的信号，尽管样本量不足以在传统阈值下确认。研究暗示，收敛命运在生成结束前就已部分编码于中间表示中，为早期退出推断与自适应计算分配提供了路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究链式思维模型在推理过程中出现的二元收敛现象是否可在生成早期通过内部模型状态进行预测，以实现更高效的推理机制。

Method: 通过在隐藏状态激活值（第50-300个词元）上训练线性探测器，评估不同层和位置的预测能力；对比基于词元熵和重复统计的行为基线；使用置换检验评估信号显著性。

Result: 第20层在第150个词元处的激活值可实现AUC 0.608，显著优于随机水平；激活探测器优于行为基线；置换检验显示p=0.063，提示存在微弱但可能有效的信号。

Conclusion: 收敛命运在生成过程早期即被部分编码于模型中间表示中，为实现早期退出和动态计算分配提供了可行性基础。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought reasoning models such as DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-7B exhibit a bimodal convergence pattern: generations either terminate within a token budget (converged) or exhaust it without reaching a conclusion (non-converged). We characterize this phenomenon empirically, showing that converged generations achieve 90.3% accuracy on AIME 1983-2024 while non-converged ones achieve only 6.6%, with an overall convergence rate of 62.0%. We then ask whether this outcome is detectable early in the thinking chain using internal model representations. Training linear probes on hidden-state activations at token positions 50-300, we find that layer-20 activations at token 150 achieve AUC 0.608 (+-0.080, 5-fold CV), reliably above chance even at token 50. Activation probes consistently outperform behavioral baselines derived from token entropy and repetition statistics. A sweep-level permutation test yields p=0.063 (100,000 permutations), consistent with a modest signal that our sample size cannot confirm at conventional thresholds. These findings suggest that convergence fate is partially encoded in intermediate representations well before the generation ends, opening a path toward early-exit inference and adaptive compute allocation.

</details>


### [165] [When Trivia Is Not Trivial: Everyday Knowledge Failures in Multilingual LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21445)
*Anna Mosolova,Djamé Seddah*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究引入了TriviaRoomQA，一个涵盖288个主题的多语言基准，用于评估大语言模型在日常、文化相关及长尾知识方面的能力。测试覆盖六种欧洲语言和额外的法语题目，共3,300个平行多选题及5,340个法语文本。评估了来自欧、亚、北美30个开源大模型（参数量7B至70B），发现模型在历史、地理、数学等知识密集型任务表现良好，但在名人、音乐、电影、新闻等流行文化领域明显较弱，且跨语言性能存在差异，表明事实知识获取并非完全语言独立。研究揭示了现有学术基准未覆盖的重要知识差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有学术基准多聚焦于饱和的知识领域，难以反映真实世界中关于日常文化和长尾知识的挑战，而这类知识在问答竞赛中至关重要。因此，亟需一个能评估模型在广泛、现实情境下知识掌握能力的新基准。

Method: 构建TriviaRoomQA多语言基准，包含3,300个跨语言多选题和5,340个法语文本；选取30个不同来源与规模的开源大模型进行评估；通过对比模型在各类主题上的表现，分析其在知识密集型与流行文化任务中的差异，并考察语言对性能的影响。

Result: 模型在历史、地理、数学等知识密集型任务中表现优异，但在明星、音乐、电影、新闻等流行文化任务中显著落后；跨语言表现不一致，说明知识获取受语言影响，存在语言依赖性；现有基准未能充分捕捉这些现实知识差距。

Conclusion: TriviaroomQA揭示了当前大语言模型在日常文化与长尾知识方面的显著短板，表明现有学术基准不足以全面评估模型的真实世界知识水平，亟需更贴近实际应用的评测体系。

Abstract: Quiz rooms, trivia nights, and quiz shows challenge human knowledge across a wide range of topics, from canonical facts to everyday culture. In this paper, we examine whether large language models (LLMs) can perform competitively in such settings, using quiz-style questions to test them on both common and niche topics. We introduce TriviaRoomQA, a multilingual benchmark designed to evaluate everyday, culturally grounded, and long-tail knowledge across 288 topics. The benchmark contains 3,300 parallel multiple-choice questions in six European languages and additional 5,340 French-only questions for a more fine-grained case study. We evaluate 30 open-weight LLMs from European, Asian, and North American providers, covering models from 7 to 70B parameters. We find that models are strong on knowledge-intensive topics such as history, geography, and mathematics, but substantially weaker on everyday popular-culture topics such as celebrities, music, movies, and news. Moreover, model performance varies across languages even for the same underlying questions, suggesting that access to factual knowledge is not always language-independent. In sum, our dataset and experiments demonstrate an important knowledge gap which is not captured by existing academic-based saturated benchmarks.

Abstract: The ability to handle long-term memory in LLMs is becoming increasingly critical, yet existing benchmarks remain English-centric and rely on aggregate retrieval metrics, failing to capture interactions between long-range context, temporal information, and reasoning. To address this, we introduce RUMBA (Russian User Memory BenchmArk) - a new benchmark for long-term conversational memory that provides a fine-grained taxonomy of memory-centric question types and a unified methodology accounting for semantic type, session scope, temporal reasoning, and the explicitness of temporal expressions. RUMBA consists of timestamped user-assistant dialogues with QA pairs requiring retrieval, combination, and reasoning across sessions. While designed for Russian, we also provide an aligned English subset under the same methodology. ### [167] [What, Where, and How: Disentangling the Roles of Task, Language, and Model in Code Model Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21491)
*Piotr Wilam*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过2x2实验设计（Python/Rust与Qwen2.5-Coder-7B/DeepSeek-Coder-V1-6.7B组合），首次系统评估独立训练的语言模型在代码理解中是否以相同方式表征概念。结果表明：任务决定哪些概念获得专用电路（模型间一致性高，Spearman ρ ≈ 0.65），模型决定电路的层位置（Qwen在深层，DeepSeek在浅层）和演化方式（Qwen早期激活原子概念）。电路结构非通用，存在“内容统一但组织异构”的现象。此外，模型间共享神经元，且对Rust类型系统有更强的语义聚类能力，验证了功能有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究独立训练的语言模型在代码理解任务中是否存在共同的表征机制，尤其是概念电路是否具有普遍性。传统观点假设模型应趋同，但其背后的决定因素（任务、语言、模型自身）尚不明确。本研究旨在通过控制变量的2x2设计分离这些影响因素。

Method: 采用新提出的概念电路提取方法，构建包含4个模型-语言组合的2x2实验设计（Python/Qwen, Python/DeepSeek, Rust/Qwen, Rust/DeepSeek），对58个Python和57个Rust语法概念进行统一测量。通过层间分析、神经元聚类、Jaccard相似度、消融实验和线性探针等手段，量化概念电路的分布、位置、动态及功能。

Result: 1. 模型在概念选择上高度一致（ρ ≈ 0.65，p < 1e-7），说明任务驱动表示内容；2. 电路在模型中的位置不同（Qwen在L17-19，DeepSeek在L6-7）；3. 电路演化模式不同（Qwen早期激增，DeepSeek无此特征）；4. Rust比Python多出2-3倍的概念特异性电路；5. 模型间共享神经元，且DeepSeek比Qwen更显著；6. Qwen将Rust关键字绑定为单一语义簇（Jaccard=0.535），揭示表面语法之外的语义维度。

Conclusion: ‘电路是否通用’的答案取决于问题维度：‘什么’（What）是通用的，‘在哪’（Where）和‘如何’（How）则依赖于模型。这表明表征内容可统一，但计算组织不具普遍性。模型行为并非预先设定，而是由训练过程自发形成，且存在未被预测的跨语言协同与语义压缩现象。未来需验证该模型特征是否可外推至其他模型。

Abstract: Do independently trained language models come to represent the same thing in the same way? We answer for code, extending a recently introduced concept-circuit extraction method to a 2x2 design -- Python and Rust crossed with Qwen2.5-Coder-7B and DeepSeek-Coder-V1-6.7B -- and measuring a complete inventory of grammatical concepts (58 Python, 57 Rust) identically in all four cells: the smallest design that separates what depends on the task, the language, and the model.
  The answer splits into three parts. What earns dedicated circuitry is set by the task: the models agree on which concepts receive circuits (Spearman $ρ$ = 0.638 for Python, 0.673 for Rust, both p < $10^{-7}$). Where those circuits sit is set by the model: Qwen processes concepts in a late band (~L17-19), DeepSeek at L6-7, for both languages. How circuits grow across layers is also set by the model: Qwen gives its atomic concepts an early spike that DeepSeek does not. "Are circuits universal?" thus has no single answer: yes for What, no for Where and How -- universality is a property of representational content, not of computational organisation.
  None of this structure was fixed in advance. The agreement could have landed anywhere between independence and identity; it lands at $ρ\approx 0.65$. Rust constructs receive 2-3x more concept-specific circuitry than their Python equivalents, in both models. Both models share neurons between the languages (6/7 and 7/7 paired constructs), DeepSeek 1.94x more than Qwen -- a direction no prior result predicts. And Qwen binds nine keywords of Rust's type-and-trait machinery into one tight neuron cluster (Jaccard 0.535 vs null 0.112, p < 0.001), a semantic dimension invisible in surface syntax. Ablation and linear probes confirm the circuits are functional.
  All claims are scoped to this 2x2; whether the per-model profile predicts a third model is the designed next test.

</details>


### [168] [Artificial Epanorthosis: Why large language models overuse a classical rhetorical figure, and how to mitigate it](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21498)
*Federico Boggia*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨大语言模型中频繁出现的修辞手法'epanorthosis'（自我修正）现象，指出其根源在于训练数据中的宣传性文本和偏好调优（RLHF）对自信、强调性表达的奖励，而非生成顺序本身。通过构建'epanorthosis指数'，对比模型与人类在不同语体中的表现，发现模型在演说类文本中过度使用该修辞，在非正式问答中则不足，而在论证、新闻和百科类文本中与人类接近。研究提出以轻量级LoRA适配器进行缓解，并证明通过一句指令或监督微调可显著降低该现象，目标应是使模型在各语体中校准至人类水平，而非完全消除。最终警示：真正的风险是我们开始像机器一样写作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示大语言模型中过度使用eponorthosis这一修辞现象的成因及其潜在危害，强调模型输出风格与人类差异的重要性，防止人类语言风格被机器主导。

Method: 基于人类修辞学分类（Fontanier）构建epanorthosis指数，评估模型在不同语体中的密度；采用LoRA适配器、指令微调与监督微调等技术进行干预；通过跨语言（意大利语）实验验证效果。

Result: 模型在演说类文本中eponorthosis密度约为人类的2-3倍，尤其在大模型中更明显；在非正式问答中则显著低于人类；通过轻量级干预手段可有效调控该现象，实现与人类水平的校准。

Conclusion: 大语言模型的修辞风格偏差源于训练数据与优化目标，而非生成机制本身。应以校准至各语体下的人类基准为目标，而非彻底消除特定修辞。若不加控制，人类语言将逐渐趋同于机器写作风格，带来深远影响。

Abstract: A rhetorical figure that Cicero and Quintilian catalogued two thousand years ago reappears, systematically, in the text of large language models: epanorthosis, the self-correction of the specimen «This is not a course. It is a journey of transformation». This essay argues that the overuse is a trained disposition, driven mainly by a training distribution rich in promotional prose and by preference tuning (RLHF) that rewards confident, emphatic phrasing; the left-to-right nature of generation is an amplifier rather than the root cause. Building on evidence that models diverge from human rhetorical style, and on Fontanier's classification of epanorthosis as a figure of thought, it sets out a programme that scores the figure against genre-specific human baselines through an Epanorthosis Index (density relative to the human rate). A first measurement, on three sizes of one instruction-tuned model family, finds mis-calibration by register in both directions: the models overshoot in oratory (about twofold, near threefold in Italian, concentrated in the larger tiers) and undershoot in informal question-and-answer writing, while matching humans in argument, journalism, and encyclopedic prose. Three constructive contributions follow: a survey of mitigation techniques centred on lightweight LoRA adapters; a demonstration, in Italian, that a one-line instruction cuts the figure by half to nearly three-quarters and that a supervised-fine-tuning adapter removes it almost entirely, with a scaling coefficient that dials the reduction back onto the human rate; and the argument that the target is calibration to the human rate for each genre, not elimination. It closes on the stakes: the real risk is that we begin to write like the machines.

</details>


### [169] [DONDO: Open w2v-BERT Speech-Recognition Base Models for African Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21540)
*Paul Azunre*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: DONDO 是一个针对非洲语言的开源、宽松许可的自动语音识别（ASR）基础模型系列，基于 w2v-BERT 2.0 自监督语音编码器。包含21个单语模型和5个多语模型，覆盖加纳、塞拉利昂、尼日利亚、塞内加尔、肯尼亚和津巴布韦的27种语言变体。模型主要在宗教文本的朗读语音上进行微调，以获得广泛、无版权问题且拼写一致的数据。采用两步（或三步）学习率退火的微调方法，先以高学习率适应共享多语模型，再逐步降低学习率以恢复甚至超越单语基线性能。引入轻量级语言条件机制，在输入特征前添加一热语言标识作为前缀帧，实现单一多语检查点在推理时定向至目标语言。五个多语家族平均词错误率（WER）达10-13%，显著缩小与单语模型的差距，同时用一个检查点覆盖多种语言。所有模型均在 Hugging Face KhayaAI 组织下以 Apache-2.0 许可证（仅需署名）发布，支持自由微调及商业用途。所覆盖语言估计有约一亿母语使用者，若计入第二语言使用者则人数更多。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多非洲语言缺乏高质量、可公开使用的转录语音数据，限制了其自动语音识别系统的发展。现有解决方案常依赖于有限或受版权约束的数据集，导致模型覆盖范围小、可扩展性差。为解决这一问题，本文提出 DONDO，旨在构建一个开放、可扩展、高质量的 ASR 基础模型体系，覆盖多个非洲语言，推动低资源语言的语音技术发展。

Method: 基于 w2v-BERT 2.0 自监督语音编码器，构建单语与多语 ASR 模型。使用宗教文本中的朗读语音进行数据收集，确保数据广度与拼写一致性。采用两步（或三步）学习率退火的微调策略：第一步以高学习率快速适应共享多语模型；第二步逐步降低学习率以优化性能。引入轻量级语言条件机制，通过在输入前添加一热语言标识前缀帧，实现多语模型在推理阶段的语言定向。

Result: 五个多语模型家族平均词错误率（WER）达到10-13%，显著缩小与单语模型的差距，且能在一个检查点中覆盖多种语言。所有模型在 Hugging Face 上以 Apache-2.0 许可证发布，支持自由微调和商业应用。所覆盖语言估计有约一亿母语使用者，涵盖更广泛的人群。

Conclusion: DONDO 成功构建了一个开放、高效、可扩展的非洲语言 ASR 模型体系，通过创新的微调策略与语言条件机制，在保证多语言覆盖的同时实现了接近单语模型的性能。该工作为非洲低资源语言的语音技术发展提供了重要基础设施，具有广泛的社会与技术价值。

Abstract: We present DONDO, a family of open, permissively licensed automatic speech recognition (ASR) base models for African languages, built on the w2v-BERT 2.0 self-supervised speech encoder. DONDO comprises twenty-one monolingual models and five multilingual models spanning twenty-seven language varieties across Ghana, Sierra Leone, Nigeria, Senegal, Kenya and Zimbabwe. Models are fine-tuned primarily on read speech drawn from religious texts, which offer broad, license-clear and orthographically consistent coverage for languages that otherwise lack transcribed audio. We describe a two-step (and, for one family, three-step) learning-rate-annealed fine-tuning procedure that first adapts a shared multilingual model at a high learning rate and then anneals it to recover, and in several cases surpass, strong monolingual baselines. We further describe a lightweight language-conditioning mechanism that injects a one-hot language identity as a sequence of prefix frames prepended to the acoustic features, allowing a single multilingual checkpoint to be steered to a target language at inference. Across the five multilingual families the annealed models reach average word error rates (WER) of 10-13%, closing most of the gap to monolingual models while covering many languages in a single checkpoint. All models are released on the Hugging Face KhayaAI organisation under the Apache-2.0 license (attribution only) so that others may fine-tune them freely, including for commercial use. We provide a conservative estimate that the languages covered are spoken by on the order of one hundred million first-language speakers, and by substantially more when second-language use is included.

</details>


### [170] [MedGame: Storytelling Gamification Empowered by Large Language Models for Medical Education](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21570)
*Qian Wu,Xinrong Zhou,Zizhan Ma,Kai Chen,Zheyao Gao,Xun Lin,Hongqiu Wu,Longfei Gou,Yixiao Liu,Ann Sin Nga Lau,Qi Dou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MedGame 是一个将静态临床案例转化为结构化、可执行叙事游戏的框架，通过双引擎设计（医学叙事设计师和故事导演）实现决策导向的学习轨迹。构建了包含5000个案例的MedGame Bench基准测试集，实验表明任务特定微调能显著提升开源大模型表现，缩小与商用模型差距；初步学生研究显示，学习者认为MedGame比纯文本更吸引人且实用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有医疗教育系统多局限于问答或单轮反馈等局部交互，缺乏对完整临床案例进行决策中心学习轨迹的组织，因此需要一种能够将临床案例转化为动态、互动式学习体验的框架。

Method: MedGame采用双引擎架构：医学叙事设计师生成基于病例的临床故事情节、状态和决策节点；故事导演将其转化为依赖感知的多模态编排计划，并在自研交互平台上实现渲染。

Result: 任务特定微调显著提升了开源LLMs在MedGame Bench上的表现，缩小了与商业模型的性能差距；用户研究证实，学习者认为MedGame比传统文本形式更具吸引力和实用性。

Conclusion: MedGame成功将静态临床案例转变为可执行的互动叙事游戏，为医学教育提供了新型、高参与度的学习范式，具有广泛应用潜力。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) show promise for medical education, but most existing systems focus on localized interactions such as question answering or single-turn feedback, rather than organizing an entire clinical case into a decision-centered learning trajectory. We introduce \textit{MedGame}, a framework that transforms static clinical cases into structured, executable storytelling games. MedGame uses a dual-engine design: a Medical Narrative Designer synthesizes case-grounded clinical storylines with states and decision nodes, while a Story Director converts them into dependency-aware multimodal orchestration plans rendered by our released interactive platform. We construct MedGame Bench, a 5,000-case benchmark and evaluation protocol for Medical Narrative Generation and Story Direction. Experiments show that task-specific fine-tuning substantially improves open-source LLMs on MedGame Bench and narrows the gap with commercial models. A pilot student study further shows that learners perceive MedGame as more engaging and useful than text-only alternatives.

</details>


### [171] [Surprisal Theory is Tautological (without Rational Grounding)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21574)
*Ryan Cotterell*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Surprisal theory is shown to be a tautology unless the language model is constrained by cognitive principles, not just corpus fit. Without such constraints, it cannot make falsifiable predictions. Recent evidence shows better corpus models don't always predict human processing better, undermining the assumption that corpus-based models suffice. A rationalist approach—grounded in cognitive mechanisms like memory or processing goals—is needed to break the tautology.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To challenge the validity of surprisal theory as a predictive framework in psycholinguistics by demonstrating that, without additional cognitive constraints on the language model, it becomes a tautology with no falsifiable content.

Method: Logical analysis and critique of the assumptions underlying surprisal theory, combined with review of empirical findings showing poor correlation between corpus-fitted models and human processing difficulty.

Result: Surprisal theory lacks predictive power unless the language model is derived from non-empirical cognitive principles (e.g., memory constraints, processing goals), not just statistical fit to training data.

Conclusion: To be scientifically meaningful, surprisal theory must incorporate a rationalist, cognitively motivated language model rather than relying solely on empirical corpus statistics.

Abstract: Surprisal theory holds that the human processing difficulty of a linguistic unit in context is an affine function of its surprisal under some language model. I argue this claim is a tautology without further constraint: for any non-negative difficulty measure over units in context, there exists a language model whose surprisal is an affine function of it under mild technical conditions. Therefore, because any pattern of difficulty is consistent with some language model, without an additional constraint on the language model, surprisal theory makes no falsifiable predictions. The tautology was long obscured by an assumption implicit in two decades of psycholinguistic work---that the relevant language model is the distribution that generated the training corpus, so that improving corpus fit improves predictions of human behavior. Recent empirical work has undermined this assumption, demonstrating that better corpus models can be worse predictors of processing difficulty. I conclude that breaking the tautology requires a rationalist intervention, i.e., the relevant language model must be derived from a non-empirically motivated model of the comprehender, which could be based on, for instance, memory constraints or processing goals, and that, thus, does not depend on the behavioral data surprisal theory is meant to explain.

</details>

### [172] [DataPrep-Bench: Benchmarking LLMs as Training Data Preparators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20465)
*Hao Liang,Qifeng Cai,Yibo Lin,Jianzhuo Du,Qifeng Xia,Sizhe Qiu,Linzhuang Sun,Meiyi Qiang,Zhaoyang Han,Xiaochen Ma,Bohan Zeng,Ruichuan An,Conghui He,Wentao Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了DataPrep-Bench，首个统一基准，用于联合评估大语言模型在数据构建和数据质量评估两方面的能力。数据构建任务中，方法基于相同原始数据生成监督训练数据，并通过微调基线模型进行评分；同时发布技能引导代理Data-Construction-Skill，显著提升金融领域表现。在数据质量评估方面，引入基于分布对齐的DAS评分方法，其在四个领域中表现出最强跨模型相关性，且在数学、科学、医学三个领域同时达到r > 0.70，优于现有各类评价指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前缺乏统一基准来衡量大语言模型、智能体及数据工作流在端到端数据准备中的实际效果。尤其在数据质量和下游训练效用之间缺乏可靠评估体系，亟需一个以最终下游性能为导向的综合性评估框架。

Method: 提出DataPrep-Bench，涵盖六大数据领域，采用共享下游评估协议。数据构建部分通过微调基线模型（如Dolly-15k）评估输出数据质量；数据质量评估部分使用皮尔逊相关系数衡量评分函数与下游性能之间的关系，并引入基于最大均值差异（MMD）的分布对齐评分（DAS）。

Result: Data-Construction-Skill在Llama-3.1-8B金融任务中比基线提升近20分；DAS在四个领域中取得最强跨模型相关性，在数学、科学、医学三领域同时实现r > 0.70，显著优于现有质量、多样性及启发式评估方法。

Conclusion: DataPrep-Bench为大语言模型驱动的数据准备提供了统一、以下游性能为导向的评估框架，将数据构建与数据质量评估视为同等重要的目标，推动该领域系统化发展。

Abstract: The quality of training data fundamentally determines the capabilities of large language models (LLMs), yet no unified benchmark exists to measure how well LLMs, agents, and data-centric workflows actually prepare training data end to end. We view LLM-driven data preparation as comprising two complementary capabilities: data construction, which transforms raw sources into supervised training data, and data quality evaluation, which predicts the training value of candidate datasets before downstream training; throughout, "quality" refers to downstream training utility rather than surface-level textual properties. We introduce DataPrep-Bench, the first unified benchmark that jointly evaluates both capabilities under a shared downstream-grounded protocol over six domains and multiple base models. For data construction, methods consume identical raw sources and are scored by fine-tuning a base model on their outputs jointly with Dolly-15k; alongside this track we release Data-Construction-Skill, a skill-guided agent that lifts the Dolly-only baseline by nearly 20 points absolute on Llama-3.1-8B Finance and is competitive with the strongest agent- and DataFlow-based methods in knowledge-extraction-dense domains. For data quality evaluation, scoring functions are scored by Pearson correlation with downstream performance on a shared candidate pool; we release the Distributional Alignment Score (DAS), a distribution-based evaluator that uses MMD between a candidate dataset and a domain proxy. DAS attains the strongest cross-model correlation in four of six domains and is the only metric clearing r > 0.70 simultaneously in Math, Science, and Medical, outperforming existing quality-, diversity-, and heuristic-based evaluators. DataPrep-Bench provides a unified, downstream-grounded framework for measuring progress on both capabilities as co-equal targets of LLM-driven data preparation.

</details>


### [173] [PhantomFill: When the Form Demands an Answer, Language Models Invent One](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20492)
*Rana Muhammad Usman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了语言模型在生产环境中因格式要求而产生幻觉的现象。当模型被强制以特定格式（如JSON字段）回答时，即使输入信息不足，也会虚构答案，且这种现象在多数模型中普遍存在。实验显示，要求结构化输出会显著提升虚假生成率，甚至在部分模型中达到100%。尽管提供‘证据不足’选项或直接指令禁止推断，仍无法有效阻止幻觉。研究提出新基准 PhantomFill，用于量化‘被迫虚构率’和‘逃逸利用率’，并验证了一行代码级别的修复方案。核心结论是：格式压力导致的幻觉是训练中未被测量的关键问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型在实际应用中常被要求以结构化格式（如JSON）输出，但这种格式约束会导致模型在缺乏足够信息时仍强行生成内容，从而引发严重幻觉。作者旨在揭示这一现象的根本原因——格式本身即是诱因，并推动对模型诚实性与格式依赖关系的系统评估。

Method: 通过设计不可回答的输入场景（如无回复的高赞帖子、未转录的客服通话），对比同一模型在自由文本与结构化格式下的输出行为；测试不同指令、提示、模型规模及开放权重情况下的反应；引入 PhantomFill 基准，量化‘被迫虚构率’与‘逃逸利用率’，并验证简单模式修复的有效性。

Result: 在自由文本中，GPT-5.5 98% 次数诚实表示无数据可答；但在强制要求 JSON 格式时，40次中有40次虚构情感分析结果。十种模型中，格式压力导致幻觉率达100%。所有九个开源模型忽略‘证据不足’选项，六种模型中四者无视明确指令。最小与最大模型表现更诚实，中间尺寸最易伪造。一行为的模式修复可有效降低幻觉。

Conclusion: 语言模型的幻觉不仅源于能力缺陷，更深层原因是格式要求带来的强制生成压力。结构化输出中的必填字段（如枚举、最小数量数组）成为幻觉温床，而当前评估体系未捕捉此问题。必须建立新基准（如 PhantomFill）来监测和缓解格式驱动的虚构行为，诚实性应作为模型设计的核心指标。

Abstract: Language models in production do not write prose. They fill forms: JSON fields, function arguments, extraction templates. We show that the form itself causes hallucination.
  We ask thirteen models the same question about the same input and change only the answer format. The inputs are built so the question cannot be answered: a viral post showing 12,400 likes but no visible replies, a support ticket whose call was never transcribed. In free text, GPT-5.5 answers honestly. It says there is no reply data, 98% of the time. Given a required JSON field for sentiment, the same model invents an answer 40 times out of 40. It fabricates the mood of crowds it never saw and quotes customers it never heard.
  The pattern holds with force. Required fields drive fabrication to 100% in ten of thirteen models. An explicit "insufficient evidence" option rescues only the frontier: all nine open-weight models ignore it. A direct instruction, do not infer sentiment, is overridden by the schema in four of six models. Resistance does not come with scale: within a single model family, the smallest model refuses, the mid-sized model fabricates, the largest refuses again. Honesty under format pressure is a training outcome that no one is measuring.
  The fabrication hides exactly where hedging is impossible: in required enums and minimum-count arrays, fields where no disclaimer fits. We release PhantomFill, a benchmark with deterministic scoring and two reportable numbers: the Coerced Fabrication Rate and the Escape Utilization Rate. The fix we test is one line of schema. The failure we measure is everywhere.

</details>


### [174] [The Active Ingredient in Muon's Grokking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20512)
*Yufeng Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Muon优化器在模运算任务上比AdamW更快达到grokking阈值，关键优势来自正交化（通过Newton-Schulz迭代实现），而非仅谱范数约束。消融实验表明，仅谱范数约束无加速效果且不稳定，而正交化单独即可实现与完整Muon相当的性能。机制分析显示，正交化优化器以约1/3的谱范数完成泛化，收敛至更低范数解，而非简单减少参数扰动。减少Newton-Schulz迭代次数可加快到达阈值，但导致解脆弱，尤其在高学习率下易崩溃；单次迭代仅在小学习率下稳定，五次迭代为学习率鲁棒的最佳选择。此外，谱缩放可被移除而无性能损失。研究强调需同时关注首次跨越和持续稳定的时间，以准确评估‘更快’的含义。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Muon优化器为何在模运算任务中比AdamW更快实现grokking，特别是分离并验证其核心机制（谱范数约束与正交化动量）的实际贡献，避免归因偏差，并提升对优化器行为的理解与可复现性。

Method: 通过多种子、多学习率的消融实验与机制分析，系统测试不同组件（正交化、谱范数约束、迭代次数、谱缩放）的影响；结合稳定性指标，对比首次达到阈值时间与持续稳定时间，评估优化器性能。

Result: 正交化是速度提升的关键因素，谱范数约束单独无效；正交化优化器在更低谱范数下达成泛化；减少迭代次数虽快但不稳定，五次迭代在不同学习率下表现最稳健；谱缩放可被移除而不影响性能。在稳定性度量下，‘更快’的结论可能反转，需综合考量多种指标。

Conclusion: Muon优化器的加速源于正交化机制，而非谱范数约束。最优配置为五次Newton-Schulz迭代，兼具速度与鲁棒性。研究强调在评估优化器时应兼顾首次突破与持续稳定，避免片面判断。代码已公开以支持复现。

Abstract: The Muon optimizer reaches the grokking threshold on modular arithmetic faster than AdamW. Prior work attributes this to "spectral-norm constraints plus orthogonalized momentum" but does not isolate which mechanism matters. To better understand Moun's behavior, we run multi-seed and multi-learning-rate sweeps to decompose and stress-test the effect. First, an ablation shows the speedup comes from orthogonalization (the Newton-Schulz iteration): orthogonalize-only matches full Muon, whereas spectral-only is no faster than AdamW and is unreliable, and this verdict holds across learning rates. Second, a mechanistic analysis finds that orthogonalizing optimizers reach generalization at roughly 3x lower spectral norm and, controlling for how much the embedding actually moves, settle into a lower-norm solution rather than simply perturbing the embedding less. Third, reducing the Newton-Schulz iteration count from five to one accelerates reaching the threshold but makes the grokked solution fragile, prone to transient collapse, with fragility that grows with learning rate; a single iteration is fast and stable only at small learning rate, while the canonical five iterations are the learning-rate-robust choice. We also show spectral scaling can be dropped at no measured cost. A methodological thread runs throughout: under a stability-aware metric, "faster" claims about grokking optimizers can invert, so we report both first-crossing and sustained-grok times. To support reproducibility, we release our full training and analysis code at https://github.com/louiswang524/muon-grokking-frontier

</details>


### [175] [Scaling Closed-Loop Feature Channel Configuration with LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20516)
*Tolgay Atinc Uzun,Radu Timofte,Dmitry Ignatov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究将基于大语言模型的闭环通道配置搜索扩展至每轮微调250个候选网络，共分析2000个生成模型，经过筛选后得到462个有效的CIFAR-100评估结果。结果显示，每轮平均准确率呈显著正线性趋势（斜率9.87e-4，p=0.043），最佳性能前沿提升明显（从0.3144升至0.3676），且前5和前10名的平均表现也呈上升趋势。此外，最优模型在仅1180万参数下达到0.3676准确率，远优于早期高精度模型（16650万参数），表明参数效率显著提升。大规模采样还揭示了新的架构规律：41.8%的模型采用非2的幂次通道宽度，且高性能模型普遍呈现中前期通道宽度适中、中间或后期块通道扩展的结构模式。这些发现表明初始研究中的通道搜索信号在更密集采样下依然有效并可进一步挖掘。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证初始闭环大语言模型驱动的通道配置搜索结果是否能在更密集的采样环境下保持有效性，并探索在更大规模评估中可能浮现的额外架构规律与参数效率提升。

Method: 将同一通道配置搜索框架扩展至每轮微调250个候选网络，进行8轮完整循环，共生成2000个网络；通过任务与元数据过滤，保留462个有效的CIFAR-100评估样本；分析每轮平均准确率、最佳性能前沿及模型参数量变化，并识别架构模式。

Result: 每轮平均准确率呈现显著正线性趋势（斜率9.87e-4，p=0.043）；最佳准确率从0.3144提升至0.3676；前5和前10名平均表现亦呈上升趋势；最优模型以1180万参数达到0.3676准确率，显著优于早期模型（16650万参数）；41.8%的模型采用非2的幂次通道宽度，高性能模型表现出中前期适度宽度、后期扩展的结构性特征。

Conclusion: 初始研究中观察到的通道搜索信号在更密集采样条件下依然有效，且大规模评估揭示了更优的参数效率和清晰的架构规律，支持通过生成式搜索持续优化神经网络结构。

Abstract: Promising initial results in closed-loop large-language-model-based channel-configuration search demonstrated that neural-network widths can be optimized directly through executable code generation and accuracy feedback. However, those results were obtained from a relatively sparse set of valid evaluations, leaving open whether the observed optimization behavior transfers to a denser sampling regime and whether additional architectural regularities emerge when more generated networks are evaluated. To test this, the same search setting is scaled to 250 candidate networks per fine-tuning cycle. The analysis covers 2000 generated candidates from 8 complete cycles, yielding 462 verified CIFAR-100 evaluations after task and metadata filtering. Per-cycle mean accuracy exhibits a positive linear trend with slope 9.87e-4 (p=0.043), while the high-performing frontier improves more strongly: the best observed accuracy increases from 0.3144 to 0.3676, and both the top-5 and top-10 cycle-level means exhibit positive trends. The scaled run also reveals improved parameter efficiency. The best model reaches 0.3676 with 11.8M parameters, compared with an early high-performing model at 0.3144 with 166.5M parameters. Beyond accuracy, the larger sample exposes architectural regularities that were difficult to assess from sparse observations. Non-power-of-two channel widths occur in 41.8% of verified candidates, and the strongest models share structured channel-allocation patterns characterized by moderate early widths and expanded middle or later blocks. These findings indicate that the channel-search signal observed in the initial study transfers

### [176] [Multimodal CoLRAG-TF: Triple-Filtered Retrieval for Complex PDFs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20517)
*Takato Yasuno*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Multimodal CoLRAG-TF，一种四轴融合架构，结合密集文本嵌入、BM25关键词匹配、知识图谱三元组过滤和基于图像的相似性，用于复杂文档的鲁棒检索。系统构建了包含2,403个文本块的多模态索引，支持混合OCR管道和LLM生成的图像描述。通过提取11,414个OpenIE三元组并使用FAISS进行索引，实现亚秒级查询与层级相关性传播。采用受HippoRAG2启发的粗到细检索器（整体→章节→块）缩小搜索空间，贝叶斯优化显示三元组轴权重需主导（α_triple = 0.44）以对抗词汇偏差并维持多跳推理质量。在457对基准测试中，系统达到0.9909的检索召回率，并在多跳问答中实现71.6%的相似度提升。视觉输入管道也验证了该方法的适用性。结果表明，三元组过滤的多模态融合对噪声、异构PDF中的结构化推理至关重要，且具有跨领域通用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有检索增强生成（RAG）在异构PDF集合上面临挑战，包括多模态内容、领域术语及跨分散证据的多跳推理需求。传统方法难以有效处理复杂文档中的信息碎片与语义关联，亟需一种融合多种信号、支持结构化推理的高效检索框架。

Method: 设计四轴融合架构：整合密集文本嵌入、BM25关键词匹配、知识图谱三元组过滤与图像相似性；构建2,403个文本块的多模态索引，依赖混合OCR与LLM生成图像描述；提取11,414个OpenIE三元组并用FAISS索引以实现快速查找；采用粗到细检索策略（体积→章节→块）压缩搜索空间；通过贝叶斯优化动态调整各轴融合权重，确保三元组轴主导。

Result: 在457对测试数据上，系统取得0.9909的检索召回率，多跳问答答案相似度较单跳提升71.6%；三元组轴权重被确定为关键（α_triple = 0.44），显著缓解词汇偏差问题；视觉输入管道成功验证方法在图像数据上的可扩展性。

Conclusion: 三元组过滤的多模态融合是实现对噪声、异构PDF中结构化推理的核心机制，该框架不仅适用于灾害案例分析，还具备跨领域的通用潜力。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) over heterogeneous PDF collections remains challenging due to multimodal content, domain-specific terminology, and the need for multi-hop reasoning across dispersed evidence. We present Multimodal CoLRAG-TF, a four-axis fusion architecture that integrates dense text embeddings, BM25 keyword matching, knowledge-graph triple filtering, and image-based similarity for robust retrieval over complex documents. Our system constructs a multimodal index of 2,403 blocks extracted from 43 Japanese disaster lesson PDFs, supported by a hybrid OCR pipeline and LLM-based caption generation. To enhance compositional reasoning, we extract 11,414 OpenIE triples and index them with FAISS, enabling sub-second triple lookup and hierarchical propagation of relevance signals. A HippoRAG2-inspired coarse-to-fine retriever (volume $\to$ chapter $\to$ block) narrows the search space before final fusion scoring. Bayesian optimization over fusion weights reveals that the triple axis must dominate ($α_\text{triple} = 0.44$) to counteract lexical bias and sustain multi-hop retrieval quality. Evaluated on a 457-pair benchmark, Multimodal CoLRAG-TF achieves a Retrieval Recall of 0.9909 and a 71.6$\%$ improvement in multi-hop answer similarity over single-hop queries. An image-to-lesson pipeline using a vision LLM further demonstrates the applicability of the approach to visual inputs. These results show that triple-filtered multimodal fusion is essential for structured reasoning over noisy, heterogeneous PDFs and provides a general framework applicable beyond the disaster domain.

</details>


### [177] [Adaptive Depth in Looped Transformers: Diagnosing Learned Halting Gates and Trajectory Readouts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20519)
*Andrei Cristian Popescu,Haitz Sáez de Ocáriz Borde,Pietro Liò*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Looped Transformers use recurrent blocks with adaptive depth, but traditional learned halting policies entangle exit selection with trajectory formation. This work dissects the problem into trajectory and readout components, showing that fixed-prior depth supervision creates difficulty-aware trajectories, and simple confidence-based readouts often outperform learned gates. Training gates on frozen trajectories reveals that failure mainly stems from poor trajectory induction, not gate expressivity. Results on synthetic tasks and Ouro models confirm practical inference savings and highlight that adaptive depth is a joint issue of trajectory and readout, not just gate learning.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand why learned halting policies in looped Transformers often underperform, especially in adaptive computation. The study aims to decouple trajectory formation from exit readout to diagnose failure modes.

Method: The paper conducts controlled experiments on synthetic tasks (modular arithmetic, binary parity) and large-scale Ouro-1.4B/2.6B models. It compares fixed-prior depth supervision (shaping trajectory without input-dependent halting) against learned gates, evaluates readouts post-hoc, and fits gates on frozen trajectories to isolate failure sources.

Result: Fixed-prior depth supervision generates difficulty-aware trajectories with strong stopping signals. Simple post-hoc confidence readouts match or exceed learned gate performance. Fitting gates on frozen trajectories shows that poor performance primarily arises from the induced trajectory, not limited gate capacity. Latency measurements confirm real-world inference benefits.

Conclusion: Adaptive depth in looped Transformers should be viewed as a joint problem of trajectory formation and exit readout, not solely gate learning. The design of the trajectory is critical; learned halting policies may fail due to poor trajectory induction rather than insufficient gate expressivity.

Abstract: Looped Transformers increase test-time computation by repeatedly applying a shared recurrent block. Learned halting objectives in looped Transformers typically use a single exit distribution both as the inference-time stopping rule and as the training-time weighting of per-depth losses. This entangles exit selection with trajectory formation: the gate not only chooses which recurrent state to use, but also determines how strongly each intermediate state is supervised. Consequently, poor adaptive-compute performance can arise from the readout, the induced trajectory, or their interaction. We study adaptive depth in looped Transformers through this trajectory--readout lens, across controlled synthetic tasks (modular arithmetic and binary parity) and large-scale Ouro-1.4B and 2.6B checkpoints. We find that fixed-prior depth supervision, which shapes the trajectory without an input-dependent halting policy, produces difficulty-aware trajectories whose intermediate states expose useful stopping signals, and that simple post-hoc confidence readouts often match or outperform learned linear and MLP gates. Fitting gates on frozen trajectories localizes the failure: it appears to stem mainly from the trajectory induced by joint gate training rather than from limited gate expressivity. The same pattern is present in Ouro evaluations, where pretrained ponder gates are competitive but not uniformly Pareto-optimal, and measured latency confirms that the resulting reductions in average exit depth translate into practical inference-time savings. Our systematic diagnostic evaluation reframes adaptive depth in looped Transformers as a joint problem of trajectory formation and exit readout, rather than gate learning alone, highlighting a distinction that prior learned-halting work has often left implicit.

### [178] [Generative Bayesian Filtering for State Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20521)
*Lei Cao,Sihang Feng,Jixin Yan,Tao Sun,Naichen Shi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为生成贝叶斯滤波（GBF）的新框架，用预训练的条件变分自编码器（CVAE）替代传统滤波中的简单观测模型，以应对高维传感器信号中日益复杂的非线性与异质模式。该方法通过基于得分的采样实现在线推理，结合动态先验与生成模型诱导的似然，具备灵活性和不确定性量化能力。在合成数据及制造系统监控、心律失常诊断等真实场景中，GBF显著提升了状态估计的准确性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统滤波方法（如卡尔曼滤波）依赖于线性高斯观测模型，难以刻画高维传感器信号中的非线性与异质性模式，因此需要更灵活且能有效处理复杂观测数据的滤波框架。

Method: 采用预训练的条件变分自编码器（CVAE）构建灵活的观测模型，并将滤波过程转化为基于得分的后验采样问题，通过贝叶斯预测-更新递归实现在线状态推断。

Result: 在合成数据和真实应用（如制造系统监控、心律失常诊断）中，GBF相较于基线方法在状态估计的准确性与鲁棒性方面均有显著提升。

Conclusion: GBF通过结合生成模型的灵活性与贝叶斯推理的不确定性量化能力，为复杂动态系统的状态估计提供了一个高效且强大的新框架。

Abstract: The state of a dynamic system evolves over time, switching among several latent modes that govern its observable behavior. Filtering methods infer the latent state from observations. Classical filtering approaches, including Kalman filters, typically rely on simple observation models, such as linear-Gaussian models, that are incapable of characterizing the increasingly nonlinear and heterogeneous patterns in high-dimensional sensor signals. To tackle the challenge, we propose Generative Bayesian Filtering (GBF), a filtering framework that replaces restrictive observation models with pretrained conditional generative models parametrized by conditional variational autoencoders (CVAE). For online inference, GBF performs a Bayesian prediction-update recursion in which the measurement update is formulated as a posterior sampling problem that combines the dynamical prior with the CVAE-induced likelihood. The resulting filtering problem is then transformed into a score-based sampling problem, which naturally inherits the flexibility from generative models and the uncertainty quantification capabilities from ensembling. Experiments on synthetic datasets and real-world applications involving manufacturing system monitoring and arrhythmia diagnosis demonstrate that GBF improves state estimation accuracy and robustness relative to baseline approaches.

### [179] [Do Active SAE Feature Planes Carry More Holonomy? A Preregistered Reversal in Gemma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20522)
*Larry Richards*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究检验了在Gemma 2 2B模型中，全连接层12到13的残差流读出处，主动稀疏自编码器（SAE）特征平面是否表现出全息性集中。通过局部框架沿小回路的受限雅可比传输规则测量全息性，并对结果旋转进行面积归一化。实验设计、材料阈值、分析和裁决规则均预先注册并冻结。结果显示，主动特征平面的全息性低于匹配的混合特征控制组，调整后的对数对比度为-0.29439，95%置信区间为[-0.43989, -0.14889]，支持预测被证伪。该设计下仅大小解释不成立，而随机、混合特征与主动特征平面之间的三向排序在匹配大小下因共同支持失败而未定义。冻结后诊断在小验证子集上支持面积律，且配对回归显示中心位移受控，同时识别出传输畸变为潜在机制或混杂因素。结论为一个狭窄、可审计的操作性反转，而非因果主张‘意义抑制全息性’。原因仍待探索，包括激活强度几何、特征参与程度、字典几何、中心位移、激活流形接近度及传输剪切等均为活跃候选解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验全息性是否集中在主动稀疏自编码器（SAE）特征平面上，以验证更广泛的语义集中预测。

Method: 在Gemma 2 2B模型的第12至13层残差流读出处，使用受限雅可比传输规则携带局部框架绕小回路，测量全息性并按包围面积归一化；所有实验设计、材料阈值、分析方法和裁决规则均预先注册冻结。

Result: 主动特征平面的全息性显著低于匹配的混合特征控制组，调整对数对比度为-0.29439，95%置信区间为[-0.43989, -0.14889]，表明原预测被证伪；仅大小解释不成立，三向排序在匹配大小下未定义；冻结后诊断支持面积律，且发现传输畸变是潜在机制或混杂因素。

Conclusion: 结果为一个狭窄、可审计的操作性反转，非因果主张‘意义抑制全息性’；原因仍开放，激活强度几何、特征参与程度、字典几何、中心位移、激活流形接近度及传输剪切等均为活跃候选解释。

Abstract: This paper tests whether holonomy concentrates on active sparse-autoencoder (SAE) feature planes in Gemma 2 2B, a concrete operationalization of the broader semantic-concentration prediction. Holonomy is measured at the final-token layer-12 to layer-13 residual-stream readout by carrying a local frame around small loops using the instrument's restricted-Jacobian transport rule, then normalizing the resulting rotation by enclosed area. The design, materiality threshold, analysis, and verdict rules were preregistered and frozen before the analysed measurements were inspected. The prediction was falsified in reverse: active-feature planes carried less holonomy than matched mixed-feature controls, with an adjusted log contrast of -0.29439 and 95% interval [-0.43989, -0.14889]. A magnitude-only explanation was not supported in this design, while the three-way ordering across random, mixed-feature, and active-feature planes was undefined at matched magnitude because common support failed. Post-freeze diagnostics at the same readout supported the area law on a small validation subset, bounded matched-center displacement under a simple paired regression, and identified transport distortion as a live mechanism or confound. The result is therefore a narrow, auditable operational reversal, not a causal claim that meaning suppresses holonomy. The cause remains open, with activation-strength geometry, degree of feature engagement, dictionary geometry, matched-center displacement, activation-manifold proximity, and transport shear as live alternatives.
