### [180] [Uncertainty-Aware Trust Estimation for Multi-LLM Systems via Structured Expert Judgement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20529)
*Jiawei Zheng,Jiazhen Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于不确定性感知信任估计的多大语言模型（LLM）聚合方法，通过借鉴决策理论中的结构化专家判断，利用上下文感知校准问题来评估各模型的可靠性。采用Cooke风格的对数加权机制，惩罚过度自信但错误的预测，奖励校准良好的专家。在MMLU和MMLU-Pro上的实验表明，该方法在异质性和污染专家场景下显著优于传统聚合方法，具备更好的准确率与可靠性平衡，并在引入不可靠专家时仍保持鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多LLM聚合方法假设所有模型具有同等可信度，忽视了不同模型在不确定性处理质量上的差异，这在异质性较强的LLM环境中可能导致脆弱性，尤其是面对不可靠或对抗性专家时。因此需要一种能够动态评估并校准模型间信任度的方法。

Method: 将多LLM聚合建模为不确定性感知的信任估计问题，采用结构化专家判断中的Cooke风格对数加权方法，通过设计上下文相关的校准问题，基于模型输出的概率分布质量评估其可靠性，从而实现对预测结果的加权融合。

Result: 在同质、异质及包含不可靠专家的专家组上进行测试，结果显示：在同质设置下各方法表现相近；但在异质和污染环境下，所提方法显著提升准确性与可靠性之间的平衡，且对不可靠专家具有强鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 多LLM聚合不仅需要整合预测结果，更需在不确定性基础上进行信任校准。引入不确定性感知的信任估计机制，特别是基于校准的加权策略，是提升系统整体可靠性的关键。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) ensembles are increasingly used to improve reliability by combining predictions from multiple LLMs. However, existing aggregation methods typically assume that all models are equally trustworthy, overlooking differences in uncertainty quality. This assumption is poorly suited to heterogeneous LLMs, whose reliability and capability vary significantly, making naive aggregation vulnerable to unreliable or adversarial experts. In this work, we formulate multi-LLM aggregation as a problem of uncertainty-aware trust estimation. We adapt structured expert judgment from decision theory, using context-aware calibration questions to estimate expert reliability based on the quality of its probabilistic predictions. Specifically, we employ Cooke-style log weighting, which penalises overconfident incorrect predictions and favours well-calibrated experts. We evaluate our approach on MMLU and MMLU-Pro across homogeneous, heterogeneous, and contaminated expert panels. Results show that while aggregation methods perform similarly in homogeneous settings, Cooke weighting becomes critical under heterogeneity and contamination. It achieves a superior accuracy-reliability balance and remains robust when unreliable experts are introduced. These findings suggest that Multi-LLM aggregation requires not just combining predictions, but calibrating trust under uncertainty.

They also benefit from a well-established theoretical foundation that yields several interesting results for data science. However, their main limitation is poor scalability to high-dimensional settings. In this paper, we introduce CLOE, a new method that combines an autoencoder for dimensionality reduction with a Christoffel Function--based detector applied in the latent space. To better align representation learning with anomaly detection, we design a novel loss function that leverages the Christoffel Function to guide the autoencoder toward representations that better capture the support of the normal data distribution. We further propose a principled procedure to set the detection threshold and an efficient strategy to tune the single remaining hyperparameter. Method: 提出构建‘测试空间’，将用户反馈数据与系统任务目标进行技术映射，使飞轮机制由被动响应转向主动预防，同时通过数学建模分析其长期性能优势。

Abstract: Many modern AI systems are designed to operate under diverse, open-ended, use-cases. However, when used as the primary maintenance mechanism, these flywheels often ignore the broader context of these errors within the system's objectives, failing to preempt potential future edge cases, which leads to more unnecessary flywheel iterations. Also, it is statistically increasingly difficult to collect remaining errors due to the long-tail nature of open-world use-cases. This position paper argues that a proactive test-driven flywheel is required to address reactive flywheel's limitations and to approach a generalizable system. We advocate for creating a "test space" to technically map feedback data to task objectives, evolving the flywheel from reactive to proactive. We augment our position by mathematically proving a proactive one achieves better long-term scaling with fewer iterations than the reactive flywheel.

Motivation: 传统预测型数字孪生在物理域或边界条件变化时需大量重新训练或微调，缺乏灵活性和通用性。为突破这一局限，亟需一种无需重新训练即可适应新几何和物理条件的数字孪生方法，以提升系统实时性、可扩展性和跨域泛化能力。

Method: 提出零样本数字孪生框架，融合实时视觉感知与几何无关的物理信息推理引擎；核心为热力学图神经网络（Thermodynamics-Informed GNN），基于度量-热力学形式化，在图消息传递中强制执行能量守恒与非负熵产生；引入辅助图神经网络从稀疏初始视觉边界推断应力张量、速度与能量分布等不可观测场；采用连续闭环数据同化机制，结合深度分割网络与稀疏光流，实时追踪宏观变形与自由表面边界，动态修正自回归仿真，防止数值漂移。

Result: 在粘弹性梁的大变形和黏性流体的非线性晃动两个不同物理场景中，该框架均能在未见过的几何结构上生成物理上准确的仿真，无需针对具体案例进行再训练；系统运行延迟约25毫秒/帧，满足实时性要求；可通过增强现实技术直接可视化潜伏机械变量，展现出卓越的泛化能力与工程实用性。

Conclusion: 所提出的零样本数字孪生框架成功实现了对复杂物理系统的即时、高保真、无需重训练的仿真建模，具备强大的跨几何与跨物理场景泛化能力，为实时数字孪生应用提供了新的范式，尤其适用于动态变化环境下的智能监控与决策支持。

Abstract: Traditional Predictive Digital Twins often remain geometrically rigid, requiring extensive retraining or fine-tuning whenever the underlying physical domain or boundary conditions change. To overcome this limitation, we present a novel framework for \textit{Zero-Shot Digital Twins} that seamlessly couples real-time visual perception with a geometry-agnostic, physics-informed reasoning engine. At the core of our architecture is the Thermodynamics-Informed Graph Neural Network architecture, a Geometric Deep Learning solver grounded in a metriplectic thermodynamic formalism that enforces energy conservation and non-negative entropy production locally through graph message passing. The framework integrates an auxiliary Graph Neural Network to infer unobservable fields (such as stress tensors or velocity and energy distributions) directly from sparse initial visual boundaries, mitigating numerical start-up transients. To bridge the sim-to-real gap, we implement a continuous closed-loop data assimilation mechanism; the pipeline tracks macroscopic deformations and free-surface fluid boundaries in real-time using deep segmentation networks combined with sparse optical flow, dynamically correcting the autoregressive simulation rollout and eliminating numerical drift. To test the validity of our approach, we demonstrate the extreme generalization capabilities of our approach across two disparate physical regimes: the large deformations of a viscoelastic beam and the non-linear sloshing of a viscous fluid. In both scenarios, the unified framework instantiates physically accurate simulations on novel, unseen geometries without case-specific retraining, operating well within real-time latency budgets (approximately 25 ms per frame) and enabling the direct projection of latent mechanical variables via Augmented Reality.

### [185] [ReliableTableQA:How Much Supervision Does Reliability Annotation Need?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20537)
*Huei-Chung Hu,Hsin-Tai Wu,Koyo Kobayashi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出ReliableTableQA框架，用于训练大模型判断表格问答结果的统计可靠性，而非答案可回答性。针对企业分析中因小样本、置信区间过宽或混杂因素导致的不可靠回答问题，构建了10类可靠性分类体系（R1-R10），设计基于上下文无关语法的程序化数据生成管道，生成5万条带标签训练数据，并通过实验证明少量、分层的监督微调（SFT）即可显著提升可靠性检测性能（F1从0.61升至0.98），使不可靠自信回答率（UCAR）归零，且模型在未见零售领域表现优异；而强化学习微调（GRPO）仅在SFT不足时有轻微帮助，充分SFT后无明显优势，揭示可靠性标注是数据效率问题，明确GRPO适用边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在真实企业数据分析中，即使SQL查询语法正确，其结果也可能因样本量过小、置信区间过宽或混杂因素过多而缺乏统计意义，但现有系统仍自信给出答案，导致不可靠决策。本文旨在解决‘不可靠自信回答’这一关键缺陷，提升表格问答系统的可信度。

Method: 提出一种程序化数据生成流程，基于公共零售数据模式的上下文无关语法生成5万条训练样本，采用分层监督微调（SFT）与基于奖励的强化微调（GRPO）对比实验，构建10类可靠性分类体系（R1-R10），涵盖小样本聚合、多重比较膨胀、分布尾部不匹配等风险。

Result: 200个分层SFT样本即可将可靠性标志F1从0.61提升至0.98，解析率从0.52升至1.00，使不可靠自信回答率（UCAR）降为零，并在未见零售数据集（如H&M）上实现0.997的可靠度F1；GRPO仅在SFT训练不足时有小幅提升，充分训练后无显著收益，且在复杂多标签任务和跨域评估中验证了该结论的稳健性。

Conclusion: 可靠性标注本质上是数据效率问题。少量高质量、分层的监督微调足以实现卓越的可靠性判断能力，而强化学习微调（GRPO）并非必要，仅在初始训练不足时提供边际收益。这为高效构建可信表格问答系统提供了清晰路径。

Abstract: We introduce ReliableTableQA, a framework for training an LLM to annotate the statistical reliability of tabular QA results, not whether the query is answerable, but whether the computed answer is statistically meaningful. In real enterprise analytics, a syntactically correct SQL query can return a value that is based on too small a sample, has an excessively wide confidence interval, or is too confounded to support action. Existing systems answer confidently in all such cases, a failure we quantify as the Unreliable Confident Answer Rate (UCAR). We contribute (1) a ten-category reliability taxonomy (R1-R10) covering hazards such as small-sample aggregates, multiple-comparison inflation, and distribution-tail mismatch; (2) a program-first data pipeline that generates 50,000 reliability-labeled training examples from a context-free grammar over public retail schemas, with schema-stratified SFT/GRPO splits; and (3) a controlled study of how much supervision calibrated reliability annotation actually requires. We find that a small, schema-stratified SFT set is remarkably sufficient: 200 examples raise reliability-flag F1 from 0.61 to 0.98 and parse rate from 0.52 to 1.00, drive UCAR to zero, and yield a model that generalizes to an unseen retail domain (Rel-F1 0.997 on held-out H&M). Against this strong SFT baseline, GRPO, commonly assumed to be essential, helps only when SFT is under-trained (+0.06-0.16 exact-flag-set match at 100 examples, in- and out-of-distribution) and provides no measurable benefit once SFT is adequate, a null result we confirm across a hard compound-flag slice, a strict exact-match metric, and out-of-distribution evaluation. Our findings reframe reliability annotation as a data-efficiency problem and delineate precisely when reinforcement fine-tuning does and does not pay off.

### [186] [Codec-Gauge: Learning Compression-Friendly Gauges for Transformer KV Caches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20538)
*Yitao Jiang,Yaoqing Yang,Luyang Zhao,Muhao Chen,Devin Balkcom*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Codec-Gauge，一种后训练的缓存坐标层，通过学习小的正交通道变换来提升KV缓存压缩与量化后的模型行为保真度。该方法基于频率分布目标，结合DCT谱质心损失与平滑率代理，将KV能量集中在低频编码布局中。在六种模型上，3、4、6比特/值条件下，相比原始坐标，平均降低zfp KL散度44.0%，优于随机、Hadamard、DCT和PCA/KLT等基线。同时在块均匀及KIVI风格量化中也提升质量。27B模型实验验证了其在长上下文任务中的有效性，存储与时间测量确认压缩路径实现可行。结果表明，缓存坐标几何可作为无需修改模型权重或注意力语义的实用优化变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长上下文Transformer推理依赖于KV缓存压缩或量化，但现有方法在保持模型行为忠实性方面存在局限。研究发现，键值向量的通道基底影响固定后端对模型行为的保留能力，因此需要一种轻量级、可后训练的方法来优化缓存坐标布局以提升压缩保真度。

Method: 提出Codec-Gauge，一种后训练的缓存坐标层，学习小的正交通道变换；采用频率分布目标函数，结合token-channel DCT谱质心损失与平滑率代理，引导能量集中在低频编码方向；适用于现有压缩与量化后端，无需修改模型权重或编码规则。

Result: 在六种模型上，3、4、6比特/值条件下，平均降低zfp KL散度44.0%；优于随机、Hadamard、DCT和PCA/KLT基线；在块均匀与KIVI量化中提升质量；27B模型长上下文实验验证效果；存储与时间测量证实压缩路径有效。

Conclusion: 缓存坐标几何是提升压缩保真度的实用后训练变量，可在不改变模型权重、注意力语义或后端编码规则的前提下，显著改善压缩与量化性能。

Abstract: Long-context Transformer inference increasingly relies on KV-cache compression or quantization. Prior rotation and transform-coding results suggest that the channel basis of each key/value vector affects how faithfully a fixed backend preserves model behavior. We introduce Codec-Gauge, a post-training cache-coordinate layer that learns small orthogonal channel transforms around existing compression and quantization backends. Its frequency-distribution objective combines a token-channel DCT spectral-centroid loss with a smooth rate proxy to concentrate KV energy in low-frequency codec-facing layouts. We evaluate actual compression and decompression using measured bytes and rolling compressed-history scoring. Across six models at $3$, $4$, and $6$ bits/value, learned gauges reduce zfp KL divergence by $44.0\%$ on average relative to raw coordinates and outperform random, Hadamard, DCT, and PCA/KLT controls. The same gauges improve quality preservation for block-uniform and KIVI-style quantization. Experiments on a 27B model and long-context task prompts reproduce the quality trend, while serial storage and timing measurements validate the implemented compressed-cache paths. These results establish cache-coordinate geometry as a practical post-training variable for improving compression fidelity without changing model weights, attention semantics, or backend coding rules.

### [187] [Leveraging Biokinetic Knowledge Priors for Data-Scarce Bioprocess Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20539)
*Kyunghoon Hur,Eunjung Jeon,Hyun Woo Kim,Gyubok Lee,Seongjun Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了如何将生物动力学常微分方程（ODE）先验知识注入神经网络，以应对生物制造中数据稀缺的问题。通过对比数据级先验（在模拟的ODE曲线基础上预训练通用解码器）与架构级先验（将ODE嵌入解码器结构），发现两者均显著优于无先验基线，在11个数据集和7种微生物上表现一致。核心结论是两种方法具有可替代性：仅用模拟数据预训练的通用解码器即可达到使用真实数据训练的生物结构化解码器的效果，为数据稀缺下的深度学习提供了一种简单高效的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物制造领域面临数据稀缺问题，因生物反应器实验成本高、耗时长且公开共享少，导致每个研究仅有少量实验数据。尽管已有成熟的生物动力学常微分方程（ODE）模型描述微生物生长，但如何系统地将此类先验知识融入神经网络尚未被充分研究。

Method: 提出两种注入先验知识的方法：（1）数据级先验——在模拟的ODE曲线基础上对通用解码器进行预训练；（2）架构级先验——将ODE模型直接嵌入解码器结构中。通过在11个数据集和7种微生物上的实验，系统比较两种方法的性能。

Result: 两种方法在所有测试场景中均显著优于无先验的基线模型。更重要的是，仅通过模拟数据预训练的通用解码器性能可媲美使用真实数据训练的生物结构化解码器，表明两种方法具有高度可替代性。

Conclusion: 在生物过程数据稀缺的背景下，利用模拟的ODE数据对通用神经网络进行预训练，是一种简单且数据高效的深度学习策略，能够有效整合领域先验知识，显著提升模型性能。

Abstract: While deep learning has accelerated drug discovery, its impact on biomanufacturing has been considerably more limited. The reason is data scarcity. Bioreactor experiments are high-cost, take days to weeks, and are rarely shared in public form, leaving each research work with only a handful of experiments. The domain itself, however, is rich in prior knowledge. Biokinetic ordinary differential equation (ODE) models have described microbial growth for decades, yet how to inject this knowledge into a neural network has not been studied systematically. We present the first systematic study of how to inject this ODE knowledge into a neural network, comparing a data-level prior that pre-trains a generic decoder on simulated ODE curves against an architecture-level prior that embeds the ODE inside the decoder. Both consistently outperform no-prior baselines across 11 datasets and 7 microbial species. Our central finding is that the two are substitutable. A generic decoder pre-trained on simulation matches a fully bio-structured decoder trained on real data. Simulation pre-training therefore offers a simple, data-efficient recipe for deep learning under bioprocess data scarcity.

### [188] [From Atoms to Entropy: Optimal Noise Allocation for Diffusion Training in the Convex Regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20540)
*Luca Ambrogioni,Giulio Franzese,Alberto Foresti,Gabriel Raya,Bac Nguyen,Georgios Batzolis,Yuhta Takida,Naoki Murata,Chieh-Hsin Lai,Yuki Mitsufuji*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种统计框架，用于研究扩散模型训练中噪声水平分配的渐近最优性。研究发现，在耦合与独立学习两种情形下，最优噪声调度具有有限支撑（即集中在有限个噪声水平上），并提出了基于生成熵率平方根的信息论代理指标。在多种控制实验中验证了理论预测的有效性，并在大规模实验中显示该调度方法能显著提升离散域训练效率，同时在连续图像上表现优于或媲美现有启发式方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前扩散模型的噪声调度主要依赖启发式或经验调参，缺乏理论指导。本文旨在建立一个通用的统计框架，以理论上优化噪声水平的选择与分配。

Method: 构建了适用于完全耦合和理想化独立学习情形的理论框架，结合凸性、Polyak-Lojasiewicz 条件及随机矩阵分析，推导出最优噪声调度的原子解，并提出基于生成熵率平方根的信息论代理指标。通过控制实验直接优化目标函数，并在真实神经网络中验证其有效性。

Result: 理论分析表明最优噪声调度为有限支撑；在低维流形、Dirac 混合和 MNIST 上，优化调度均呈现有限支持；信息论代理指标在神经网络中紧密跟踪最优解，但在全耦合参数情形下失效，符合理论预期；大规模实验显示平方根熵调度在离散域显著提升效率，且在连续图像上与标准 EDM 方法相当。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于生成熵率平方根的噪声调度策略，具有坚实的理论基础，能够有效提升扩散模型训练效率，尤其在离散建模中优势明显，为未来设计更高效、更可解释的扩散训练流程提供了新方向。

Abstract: How should a diffusion model decide which noise levels to train on, and how much? Despite the importance of this choice, current noise schedules are based largely on heuristics or empirical tuning. Here, we develop a general statistical framework for studying asymptotically optimal noise-level allocation in diffusion training. Our first main result concerns the fully coupled regime, where information can spread between different time points. Under convexity or Polyak-Lojasiewicz-type assumptions, we show that the optimized training schedule admits an atomic minimizer, concentrated on finitely many noise levels. Our second main result specializes this framework to an idealized independent-learner regime, intended to model temporal specialization in neural networks. Under an additional feature-noise decoupling condition, a random-matrix analysis leads to an information-theoretic proxy: the decoupled sampling density is proportional to the square root of the generative entropy rate, the rate at which conditional entropy grows along the forward process. We test these predictions in controlled settings where the coupled objective can be optimized directly, including Dirac mixtures, low-dimensional manifolds, and MNIST. In these settings, the optimized schedules are consistently finite-support, while the smooth entropic proxy closely tracks the atomic optimum in neural-network models and breaks down mainly in the fully coupled parametric case, as the theory suggests. We then evaluate the entropic schedule in larger-scale experiments, where full schedule optimization is currently intractable. The results indicate that square-root entropy scheduling can substantially improve training efficiency on discrete domains and remains competitive with standard EDM-style heuristics on continuous images.

Abstract: We introduce HypNO, a graph-based neural operator for scalar hyperbolic conservation laws. HypNO operates directly on a space-time graph of finite-volume cells and uses adjacency-factored, physics-informed message passing to respect upwinding and entropy admissibility near shocks. We benchmark the architecture on the Lighthill-Whitham-Richards (LWR) and Aw-Rascle-Zhang (ARZ) traffic-flow models, a stress test for operator-learning methods because of their simultaneous global transport and shock formation. In collaboration with the Sierra Leone national government, we performed a staggered, nationwide deployment of our system as a decision support tool. Our econometric evaluation finds an estimated 19% increase in consumption of allocated products in treated districts, demonstrating its efficacy at improving access to essential medicines. Our tool was subsequently scaled nationwide, covering an estimated 2 million women and children under five. Our work demonstrates how machine learning methods can improve efficiency at very low cost in resource-constrained global health settings.

</details>


### [191] [When RLVR Shrinks the Reasoning Boundary: Diagnosing Pass@k Inversion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20543)
*Todd Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了强化学习中可验证奖励（RLVR）导致的pass@k反转现象，即模型在单次采样时准确率提升，但在多次采样时反而表现更差。问题集中在边界提示上，基础模型中存在稀疏但可恢复的正确轨迹，而这些轨迹在有限的RLVR回溯组中难以稳定出现。作者提出‘无证据失败’的双模式解释，并引入简单有效的证明概念——每问题基础锚定（PBA），通过强化提示中的基础正确证据并锚定到基础分布来解决该问题。在Omni-MATH-Test和MATH500上的实验表明，PBA在Pass@1和高预算覆盖率上均优于匹配的GRPO。诊断研究表明，普通GRPO会丢失基础可解的边界问题，而PBA能有效保留稀有验证通过的轨迹。该结论对视觉-语言代理等依赖外部验证器的任务同样适用，强调推理后训练需判断优化强度与优化提示的安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RLVR在提升单次采样准确率的同时可能导致重复采样性能下降，尤其在边界提示上，基础模型中存在稀疏但可恢复的正确路径，却因样本不足无法被可靠捕捉，形成‘无证据失败’。需要一种机制来识别并保护这些稀有正确轨迹，避免优化过程将其丢弃。

Method: 提出每问题基础锚定（PBA）方法：通过冻结基础模型的正确证据来锐化提示，并将高风险提示锚定至基础分布，以防止在强化学习过程中丢失关键正确轨迹。采用数学验证器作为可控测试平台，进行多种子、大规模诊断实验（3000个提示）。

Result: 在Omni-MATH-Test和MATH500上，PBA在Pass@1和高预算覆盖率上均显著优于标准GRPO；3000提示的控制实验一致显示，普通GRPO丢失边界可解问题，而PBA有效保留稀有验证通过轨迹。该现象在视觉-语言任务中也存在，提示需谨慎选择优化对象。

Conclusion: RLVR可能因忽略稀有正确轨迹而导致性能倒退，应通过如PBA等机制主动保护基础模型中的关键正确路径。推理后训练不仅需考虑优化强度，还需评估哪些提示适合优化，以避免‘无证据失败’。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) can improve one-sample accuracy while making a model worse under repeated sampling. We study this pass@k inversion: after training, the policy may solve fewer distinct problems than its base model at large $k$. The failure concentrates on boundary prompts, where the base model contains rare correct trajectories that are recoverable by sampling but too sparse to reliably appear in finite RLVR rollout groups. We argue that a two-mode account explains this as an absence-of-evidence failure: rare correct trajectories may disappear before RLVR samples and reinforces them often enough. The main contribution is this diagnostic and mechanistic framing. Per-Problem Base Anchoring (PBA) is a deliberately simple proof-of-concept: sharpen prompts with sufficient frozen-base correct evidence, and anchor risky prompts to the base distribution. Across three training seeds on Omni-MATH-Test, with MATH500 as a secondary high-coverage validation benchmark, PBA improves both \PassK{1} and high-budget coverage over matched GRPO. A 3000-prompt regime-controlled diagnostic study is consistent across seeds with the expected signature: ordinary GRPO loses base-solvable boundary prompts, while PBA preserves rare verifier-positive trajectories. We use mathematical verifiers as a controlled testbed for verifier-guided optimization; the same pass@k inversion risk applies to ECCV-relevant vision-language agents when repeated visual, spatial, or chart-reasoning attempts are checked by external tools or verifiers. Reasoning post-training should decide not only how strongly to optimize, but which prompts are safe to optimize.

</details>


### [192] [Conflict Resolution under Degraded Surveillance in Air Corridors Using Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20547)
*Esrat Farhana Dulia,Syed Arbab Mohd Shihab,Caleb Adams,Ruben Del Rosario*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种基于深度Q网络的多智能体强化学习框架，用于在三维走廊内对异构小型无人机和电动垂直起降飞机进行去中心化的冲突解决。通过局部观测和14个动作空间（包括保持航向、转向、垂直机动、着陆和速度控制）训练两类飞行器的独立策略。仿真考虑了飞行器动力学、能耗、走廊约束、观测噪声、通信延迟、信息丢失、风扰动、执行器不确定性和模型不确定性。在90种交通密度与最小间隔阈值组合下评估训练策略，结果表明冲突频率和持续时间随交通密度和间隔要求增加，但多数事件可在1秒内解决。安全条件下，飞行器约79%时间保持运动；冲突中，转向占33%，保持运动29%，速度控制25%，垂直机动13%。六组帕累托最优配置揭示了安全与走廊容量间的权衡。该框架支持在监视条件退化情况下对更安全的先进空中交通冲突解决策略进行基于仿真的评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 安全的先进空中交通（AAM）运行需要在监视信息存在噪声、延迟、不完整或暂时不可用的情况下维持飞行器之间的间隔。现有方法难以应对复杂动态环境中的多重不确定性，亟需高效、鲁棒的去中心化冲突解决机制。

Method: 采用深度Q网络（DQN）构建多智能体强化学习框架，为两类飞行器分别训练独立策略。每架飞行器基于局部观测决策，动作空间包含14种行为：保持航向、转向、垂直机动、着陆和速度控制。仿真环境整合了真实飞行器动力学、能量消耗、走廊边界限制、观测噪声、通信延迟、信息丢失、风扰动、执行器及模型不确定性。使用大规模参数组合进行训练与验证。

Result: 在90组交通密度与最小间隔阈值组合下测试，损失间隔的频率和持续时间随交通密度和间隔要求上升，但绝大多数冲突可在1秒内解决。在安全状态下，飞行器约79%的时间保持正常运动；冲突期间，转向占33%，保持运动29%，速度控制25%，垂直机动13%。识别出六组帕累托最优配置，展现出安全与系统容量之间的可调平衡。

Conclusion: 所提出的多智能体强化学习框架能够有效应对复杂、不确定的监视环境下异构飞行器的冲突解决需求，具备良好的安全性与适应性，适用于未来先进空中交通系统的仿真评估与策略优化。

Abstract: Safe Advanced Air Mobility operations require aircraft to maintain separation when surveillance information is noisy, delayed, incomplete, or temporarily unavailable. This study develops a Deep Q-Network-based Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning framework for decentralized conflict resolution among heterogeneous small unmanned aerial vehicles and electric vertical takeoff and landing aircraft operating within a structured three-dimensional corridor. Separate policies are trained for the two aircraft categories using local observations and a 14-action space that includes maintaining course, turning, vertical maneuvering, landing, and speed control. The simulation incorporates aircraft-specific dynamics, energy use, corridor constraints, observation noise, communication delay, information dropout, wind disturbance, actuator uncertainty, and model uncertainty. The trained policies are evaluated across 90 combinations of traffic density and minimum separation thresholds. Loss-of-separation frequency and duration generally increase with traffic density and separation requirements, although most events are resolved within 1s. Under safe conditions, agents maintain their motion approximately 79% of the time. During conflicts, turning accounts for 33% of actions, followed by maintaining motion at 29%, speed control at 25%, and vertical maneuvers at 13%. Six Pareto-optimal configurations reveal trade-offs between safety and corridor capacity. The framework supports the simulation-based evaluation of safer AAM conflict-resolution strategies under degraded surveillance conditions.

### [193] [SOAP, Muon, and Beyond: Pushing LLM Pretraining Scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20548)
*Mikail Khona,Aditya Vavre,Boxiang Wang,Deyu Fu,Hao Wu,Mike Chrzanowski,Bryan Catanzaro,Dheevatsa Mudigere,Jeff Pool,Michael Lightstone,Mohammad Shoeybi,Mostofa Patwary,Nima Tajbakhsh,Tijmen Blankevoort*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了高阶优化器（如SOAP和Muon）在大规模语言模型预训练中的应用，解决了其计算成本高和数值不稳定性问题。通过引入每步QR正交化和改进的预条件策略，消除了大批次训练中的损失波动，实现了稳定训练。通过更新-RMS匹配进行公平比较，实验表明SOAP和Muon在多十亿参数模型上优于AdamW，尤其在高达1亿令牌的大批次下仍保持稳定性和性能。作者还提出一种与Megatron-LM兼容的分层分布式优化器，平衡内存与通信开销，避免近似计算以保留收敛优势，并结合系统级优化加速训练。代码已开源以支持社区研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有高阶优化器（如Muon、SOAP）虽收敛更快，但因计算开销大和数值不稳定，难以在大规模语言模型训练中广泛应用。尤其在大批次场景下，现有方法易出现训练崩溃或性能下降，限制了其实际部署。因此亟需改进算法稳定性并实现高效可扩展的实现。

Method: 提出基于预条件梯度的方法改进：1）引入每步QR正交化处理数值不稳定性；2）设计更优的预条件策略；3）采用更新-RMS匹配确保不同优化器间学习率公平转移；4）开发与Megatron-LM兼容的分层分布式优化器，实现内存与通信平衡；5）实施系统级优化提升执行效率。

Result: 在超过十亿参数、万亿级令牌规模的模型训练中，所提方法在高达1亿令牌的大批次下保持训练稳定，且训练质量和收敛速度显著优于AdamW。SOAP和Muon在各种规模下均表现更优，验证了其在大规模训练中的有效性与鲁棒性。分层分布式实现有效降低通信开销，同时不牺牲优化器精度。

Conclusion: 本工作成功克服了高阶优化器在大规模语言模型训练中的稳定性与可扩展性瓶颈，证明了其在超大规模训练场景下的优越性。提出的算法改进与系统实现为未来高效训练提供了坚实基础，开源代码将推动该领域进一步发展。

Abstract: Higher-order optimizers such as Muon and SOAP offer faster convergence than AdamW, but their computational cost and numerical stability challenges have limited adoption at scale. In this work, we adapt and enhance preconditioned gradient methods to overcome the practical challenges of large-scale LLM pretraining. We first identify instabilities in SOAP at large batch sizes and propose algorithmic modifications including per-step QR orthogonalization and improved preconditioning strategies that eliminate loss spikes and enable stable training in these regimes. We then present a unified empirical study of SOAP, Muon, and AdamW using update-RMS matching to ensure fair learning rate transfer across optimizers. As part of this analysis, we empirically evaluate the orthogonalization quality of Muon. Our experiments on multi-billion-parameter models trained on trillions of tokens reveal that SOAP and Muon consistently outperform AdamW at the scales we tested. Notably, at batch sizes of up to 100M tokens for next-token prediction, these optimizers maintain training stability and quality while AdamW degrades. To enable efficient training at large scale, we introduce a layer-wise distributed optimizer compatible with Megatron-LM. Our implementation balances memory and hides communication while avoiding approximations to the optimizer computations, thus retaining their convergence benefits. Additionally, we identify and build specific system-level improvements to further accelerate our layer-wise implementation. To support the research community, we release a codebase that contains emerging algorithms for optimization: https://github.com/NVIDIA-NeMo/Emerging-Optimizers

### [194] [SevDiff: Severity-Conditioned Diffusion for Long-Tail Conflict Trajectory Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20549)
*Eni Solomon Laughter*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出SevDiff，一种基于严重性条件的去噪扩散概率模型（DDPM），可接受目标最小时间到碰撞（TTC）值作为输入，并生成匹配该请求严重性的车辆交互轨迹。在UTE SQM-W-1高速公路交织段数据集上训练后，对TTC目标0.5–1.5秒实现100%命中率（误差±0.5秒），2.0–2.5秒为97–99%，5.0秒时降至39%。生成轨迹物理合理，12个运动特征中最大越界率为4.7%，96.5%以上样本无负速度或间距。命中率下降模式具有物理可解释性，反映条件信号与训练先验的相对强度，是生成器精度的精准刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成方法无法以可测量误差控制生成目标时间到碰撞（TTC）值，而真实车辆冲突事件稀少且高成本，需精准可控的生成模型用于评估自动驾驶辅助系统（ADAS）。

Method: SevDiff是一种严重性条件化的去噪扩散概率模型（DDPM），以标量形式输入目标TTC值，通过扩散过程生成车辆交互轨迹，使实际冲突严重性匹配目标值。使用hit-rate指标评估生成结果与目标的匹配程度。

Result: 在TTC目标0.5–1.5秒时达到100%命中率（误差±0.5秒），2.0–2.5秒为97–99%，5.0秒时为39%。生成轨迹物理合理，12个运动特征中最大越界率仅4.7%，超过96.5%样本无负速度或间距。命中率下降具有物理可解释性，体现条件信号强度与训练分布的关系。

Conclusion: SevDiff实现了对目标冲突严重性（以TTC表示）的精确可控生成，生成轨迹兼具物理合理性与高命中率，其性能退化模式提供了对生成器能力的深层理解，适用于高风险场景下ADAS系统的评估。

Abstract: Trajectory datasets used in ADAS evaluation are heavily biased toward routine driving; genuine vehicle-to-vehicle conflict events are rare, and the rarer the event, the higher the cost when an ADAS system fails to handle it. Existing generative approaches address this imbalance by conditioning on scene-level properties - spatial goals, agent structure, or natural-language adversarial objectives - but none can accept a target Time-to-Collision (TTC) value as input and be held to producing it within a measurable error. This paper introduces SevDiff, a severity-conditioned denoising diffusion probabilistic model (DDPM) that accepts a requested minimum TTC value as a scalar conditioning signal and generates paired vehicle interaction trajectories whose realized conflict severity matches the request, evaluated through a hit-rate metric. Trained on 468 interaction windows extracted from the UTE SQM-W-1 expressway weaving-section dataset (1,041 vehicles, 822,691 observations after smoothing), SevDiff achieves 100% hit-rate within +/-0.5 s for TTC targets of 0.5-1.5 s and 97-99% at 2.0-2.5 s, with graceful degradation to 39% at TTC = 5.0 s. Generated kinematic features are physically plausible, with a maximum out-of-range rate of 4.7% across 12 features and no negative speed or gap values in more than 96.5% of samples. The hit-rate degradation pattern is physically interpretable as the strength of the conditioning signal relative to the training prior, making it a precision characterization of the generator rather than a pass/fail result.

</details>


### [195] [Beyond SBDD: Geometric Deep Learning in Polypharmacology and Multi-target Drug Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20550)
*Tianming Han,Zhijie Pan,Wenchi Ge,Qi Zhao*

Abstract: The traditional "one drug, one target" paradigm of structure-based drug design (SBDD) frequently proves inadequate for treating multifactorial diseases such as cancer and neurodegenerative disorders, owing to compensatory signaling pathways and the emergence of drug resistance. While polypharmacology offers a synergistic therapeutic strategy, the rational design of ligands capable of simultaneously satisfying the geometric constraints imposed by multiple targets remains a major computational bottleneck. This review positions geometric deep learning (GDL) as a powerful integrative approach to overcome these limitations. We systematically survey GDL architectures ranging from invariant graph neural networks to SE(3)-equivariant diffusion models that harness non-Euclidean molecular data to capture intrinsic three-dimensional (3D) structural interdependencies. We critically analyze GDL applications across three core dimensions, including the characterization of shared binding pockets via geometric embeddings, multi-target bioactivity prediction through heterogeneous graph fusion, and de novo generation of dual-target ligands. Particular emphasis is placed on emerging structure-conditioned generative algorithms that integrate diffusion models with reinforcement learning to autonomously resolve complex geometric conflicts between competing binding sites. Furthermore, we evaluate the pivotal role of multimodal omics integration and specialized geometric benchmarking infrastructures in validating these models. By synthesizing these methodological advances, this review elucidates the paradigm shift in drug discovery from serendipitous exploration to rational, structure-driven polypharmacological molecular engineering, thereby providing a clear, structured guide for navigating the complexities of next-generation therapeutics.

### [196] [SenCos-GEM: SENet-Calibrated and Law-of-Cosines-Constrained Geometry-Enhanced Molecular Representation for Property Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20551)
*Tianming Han,Li Zhang,Qi Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SenCos-GEM 是一种新型的显式解耦几何增强分子表示学习框架，通过引入基于余弦定律的物理引导几何一致性损失，构建高保真、数学不变的3D空间先验，并结合轻量级Squeeze-and-Excitation模块与双调制预测头（FiLM与SE结合），实现动态特征重校准。该方法在MoleculeNet多个任务上表现优异，尤其在3D构象敏感回归任务中显著提升性能，相对误差降低12.9%（RMSE）、5.3%（RMSE）和8.2%（MAE），同时在立体异构体区分和构象扰动识别方面表现出更强的空间建模能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自监督学习方法在大规模预训练中缺乏显式物理约束，易受粗粒度经验力场引起的几何噪声影响，且忽视下游适应过程中的动态特征调节，导致灾难性遗忘和负迁移问题。

Method: SenCos-GEM 采用基于余弦定律的物理引导几何一致性损失以获取数学不变的3D空间先验；在主干网络中嵌入轻量级SE模块作为任务特定适配器；设计双调制预测头，融合FiLM与SE机制，实现特征的动态重校准。

Result: 在MoleculeNet基准测试中表现卓越，特别是在FreeSolv、Lipophilicity和QM9等3D构象敏感回归任务上分别实现12.9%、5.3%和8.2%的相对误差下降；具备更强的立体异构体区分能力和构象扰动判别能力。

Conclusion: SenCos-GEM 在准确分子性质预测方面取得重大突破，通过显式物理约束与动态特征调节相结合，显著提升了模型对三维结构信息的建模能力。

Abstract: Effective molecular representation learning is crucial for accurate molecular property prediction. Recently, numerous self-supervised learning (SSL) approaches leveraging 3D GNNs have been developed to capture comprehensive 3D structural information for drug discovery. However, existing methods lack explicit physical constraints and are highly susceptible to geometric noise induced by coarse empirical force fields during large-scale pre-training.Furthermore, they overlook dynamic feature modulation during downstream adaptation, often resulting in catastrophic forgetting and negative transfer. To address these limitations, we introduce SenCos-GEM, a novel explicitly decoupled geometry-enhanced molecular representation learning framework that incorporates SENet-calibrated and law-of-cosines-constrained enhancements. SenCos-GEM employs a physics-guided geometric consistency loss based on the law of cosines to derive high-fidelity and mathematically invariant 3D spatial priors. In addition, lightweight Squeeze-and-Excitation (SE) modules are integrated into the backbone as task-specific adapters, while a dual-modulation prediction head combines Feature-wise Linear Modulation (FiLM) and SENet mechanisms to enable dynamic feature recalibration. SenCos-GEM demonstrates highly competitive performance across diverse classification and regression tasks on MoleculeNet benchmark, establishing new state-of-the-art results specifically on 3D conformation-sensitive regression tasks, such as FreeSolv, Lipophilicity, and QM9, achieving relative error reductions of 12.9% (RMSE), 5.3% (RMSE), and 8.2% (MAE), respectively. Moreover, our model exhibits superior capability in distinguishing stereoisomers and discriminating conformational perturbations, underscoring its robust spatial modeling performance. Collectively, SenCos-GEM represents a significant breakthrough in accurate molecular property prediction.

</details>


### [197] [Thermodynamic Weight Decay: Exploring Grokking Acceleration via Attention Specific Heat](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20552)
*Chitraansh Pandey*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了神经网络中的Grokking现象，即模型在长期训练后才开始泛化，而在此之前已记忆训练数据。基于Transformer注意力与热力学系统的类比，作者将注意力logits的方差视为比热容Cv，发现其峰值总在泛化转变前出现。为此提出CvAdamW，一种可直接替换AdamW的优化器，通过在线监测Cv并在检测到相变时动态调整权重衰减来注入‘热能’以促进泛化。通过迭代改进，解决了初始化噪声、小批量波动和‘slingshot blinding’等三类失败模式，引入记忆门和指数移动平均减震器。在模97加法任务中，CvAdamW使模型在2802轮内实现Grokking（基线未实现），且在10组种子中，冷启动版本平均提前257轮（6.0%），8/10种子表现更优；所有10组中Cv峰值均早于Grokking。结果表明，泛化前存在可检测的物理信号，且基于物理启发的自适应干预可有效提升泛化效率。代码与数据公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Grokking现象耗时长且不可预测，阻碍高效训练。现有方法难以在固定计算预算下触发泛化。本文旨在寻找泛化前的可检测信号，并设计可控干预机制，以加速并稳定泛化过程。

Method: 将Transformer注意力的方差建模为热力学系统中的比热容Cv，利用其峰值作为泛化前兆。提出CvAdamW优化器，动态调节权重衰减以注入‘热能’。针对三个失败模式：1）初始化噪声，引入记忆门抑制；2）小批量微波，采用指数移动平均减震器平滑；3）Slingshot Blinding，通过结构改进避免。进一步提出尺度不变的z-score重参数化，消除任务依赖超参。

Result: 在模97加法任务中，CvAdamW在4000轮内实现泛化（基线未实现），冷启动版本平均提前257轮（6.0%），显著改善8/10种子；所有10组中Cv峰值均先于泛化发生。结果验证了可检测的前兆信号与有效干预策略。

Conclusion: 神经网络泛化前可能存在可检测的物理信号（如注意力方差峰值），通过基于热力学启发的自适应优化干预，可在固定计算预算内可靠加速并提升泛化能力。该方法具有普适性潜力，为理解深度学习中的相变行为提供新视角。

Abstract: Grokking -- the delayed generalization of neural networks long after they have memorized their training data -- wastes thousands of training epochs and is notoriously unpredictable. Building on the recent result that Transformer attention is formally isomorphic to a thermodynamic system, we treat the variance of attention logits as a specific heat Cv and show that its peak reliably precedes the generalization transition. We introduce CvAdamW, a drop-in AdamW variant that monitors Cv online and injects thermal energy by dynamically scaling weight decay when a phase transition is detected. Through a strictly iterative development process we identify three failure modes -- initialization noise, mini-batch micro-ripples, and slingshot blinding -- and resolve them with a memorization gate and an exponential-moving-average shock absorber. On modular arithmetic (a+b mod 97), CvAdamW enables grokking at epoch 2802 in a 4000-epoch budget where the baseline never groks. We further propose a scale-invariant z-score reformulation that removes task-specific hyperparameters, and evaluate it across 10 paired seeds. A paired analysis shows the cold-start variant reduces mean grokking latency by 257 epochs (6.0%; median 166 epochs; Wilcoxon p=0.049, Cohen's d=0.68, bootstrap 95% CI [53,489]), improving 8 of 10 seeds; on this single task Cv peaks before grokking in all 10 seeds. Our results indicate that neural networks may expose detectable precursors of impending generalization transitions, and that a physically motivated, proportional intervention can facilitate generalization within a fixed compute budget. Code and data are public.

### [198] [Double-Scoring: Reliable Extraction of Strong Lottery Tickets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20555)
*Bryce A. Christopherson,Jack Baretz,Darian Colgrove,Salah Dandan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为double-scoring的新方法，用于改进强彩票票券（strong lottery tickets）的提取效率。该方法通过在扩展的评分空间中进行优化，取代了传统的逐层稀疏度搜索，从而克服了现有方法中的瓶颈。实验表明，double-scoring显著提升了强票券的提取性能，且对稀疏度超参数的敏感性更低，优于固定密度的edge-popup和初始化剪枝基线，并在可重绕稀疏训练拓扑上表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在提取强彩票票券时存在困难，特别是由于层间稀疏度选择带来的瓶颈。需要一种更高效、鲁棒性强的提取机制来提升稀疏子网络的发现能力。

Method: 提出double-scoring方法，通过引入增强的评分空间参数化，将层间稀疏度搜索转化为在扩大的评分张量上的优化。证明了固定密度掩码在增强评分空间中仍能访问所有原始坐标掩码，并将该方法解释为在零增强网络上的edge-popup。

Result: 在控制实验中，double-scoring显著优于固定密度edge-popup和初始化剪枝基线；性能超越可重绕稀疏训练拓扑；对稀疏度超参数的敏感性明显降低。消融实验表明，性能提升并非仅因增加可训练评分参数，而是源于增强评分空间中的竞争机制所诱导的有效原始稀疏度。

Conclusion: double-scoring通过增强评分空间实现更有效的强彩票票券提取，不仅提升了性能，还增强了对超参数的鲁棒性，为稀疏子网络的发现提供了新范式。

Abstract: The lottery ticket hypothesis proposes that large random neural networks contain sparse subnetworks that can match the performance of dense models after comparable training. A stronger version asserts that sufficiently overparameterized random networks contain subnetworks that are already accurate before any weight training. Existing theory establishes that such strong lottery tickets exist, but reliable extraction remains difficult. We revisit edge-popup, a frozen-weight score-training method for extracting strong tickets, and identify layerwise sparsity selection as a central bottleneck. We introduce double-scoring, an augmented score-space parameterization that replaces a layerwise sparsity search with optimization over enlarged score tensors. We prove that fixed-density masking in an augmented score space preserves access to all original-coordinate masks, and we show that the resulting method can be interpreted as edge-popup on a zero-augmented network. In controlled experiments, double-scoring substantially improves strong-ticket extraction over fixed-density edge-popup and pruning-at-initialization baselines, improves on the performance of rewound sparse-training topologies, and exhibits markedly lower sensitivity to sparsity hyperparameters. Ablations show that the gain is not merely due to additional trainable score parameters, but is tied to the augmented score-space competition that induces the effective original sparsity.

### [199] [Monkey King Bang: A Unified Scientific Multimodal Foundation Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20557)

### [200] [StabilityBench: Benchmarking Instability in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20558)
*Emma Kondrup,Zachary Yang,Anne Imouza,Reihaneh Rabbany*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出StabilityBench，一种将单轮基准测试转化为多轮交互历史的通用、模型无关的基准操作工具，通过引入真实用户模拟（如人口统计代理或奉承诱饵）来增强现有基准，同时保持原始任务意图。在四个涵盖数学推理、健康问答和安全性的基准上评估九个大语言模型，结果表明模型在注入后表现普遍不稳定，三个基准性能显著下降。为此提出StabilityBench-Mini，一种成本不变但能跨多样化维度采样的精简版本，以实现更真实的评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前评估协议多为静态、单轮，难以捕捉实际对话场景中的复杂性和变化性，尤其在医疗、政府等高风险领域中，AI助手的真实行为缺乏深入理解，亟需更动态、多轮的评估方式。

Method: StabilityBench通过将单轮测试用例转换为多轮交互历史，结合真实用户行为模拟（如基于人口统计特征的代理或诱导性提问），在不改变原任务目标的前提下增强测试情境的复杂性；StabilityBench-Mini则在保持数据规模不变的基础上，通过多样化轴线采样提升评估的代表性与效率。

Result: 在四个基准上的实验显示，九个大语言模型在引入模拟用户行为后，性能普遍出现显著下降，尤其是在数学推理与健康问答任务中，表明静态评估无法反映模型在真实复杂交互中的稳定性。StabilityBench-Mini有效实现了更高效、更具代表性的评估。

Conclusion: 静态、单轮的评估方法存在明显局限，无法准确衡量大语言模型在真实多轮交互中的稳定性。StabilityBench及其精简版StabilityBench-Mini提供了可扩展、可复现且成本可控的评估框架，推动了面向真实场景的模型评测发展。

Abstract: AI Assistants are increasingly deployed in high-stakes settings, such as healthcare or government services. Yet their real-world behavior remains poorly understood due to strong context dependence. Current evaluation protocols follow a defense-in-depth paradigm with compounding layers of safeguards, ranging from traditional benchmarks to live or adversarial testing. Such benchmarks remain largely static and single-turn, limiting their ability to capture real-world variability in conversational settings. We propose StabilityBench, a principled, general and model-agnostic benchmark operator that transforms single-turn benchmark queries into multi-turn interaction histories. StabilityBench augments existing benchmarks by injecting realistic user simulations, through demographic proxies or sycophantic baits, while preserving original task intent. We apply StabilityBench to four benchmarks spanning mathematical reasoning, health question-answering and safety, and evaluate nine large language models under these conditions. Our results show that model performance is consistently unstable under these injections, with considerable performance degradations on three out of four benchmarks studied. These highlight important limitations of static evaluations and motivate more realistic evaluation settings. To this end, we propose StabilityBench-Mini: a size-preserving variant of StabilityBench that samples across diversification axes, enabling more realistic evaluation without increasing costs.

This study introduces a deep learning framework, JuGAAD, using Indian census and survey data from 2001 and 2011 as a case study. Results confirm the methodology predicts socioeconomic indicators at fine scales with strong accuracy.

### [202] [Chronofy: A Temporal-Logical Decay Architecture for Information Validity in Time-Aware Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20560)
*Muntaser Syed,Marius Silaghi,Sheikh Abujar,Sharun Akter*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Chronofy 是一个三层次神经符号框架，通过引入时间逻辑衰减架构（TLDA），将时间有效性直接嵌入到 RAG 系统的表示、检索和推理层中，以解决时间幻觉问题。它利用马特罗什卡嵌入中的专用时间子空间、基于贝叶斯决策理论的可学习指数衰减函数，以及信号时序逻辑（STL）鲁棒性评估，实现对过时信息的有效过滤，并在多个基准测试中验证了其在提升检索精度、减少时间幻觉和触发数据重获取方面的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前 RAG 架构忽视事实的时间来源，导致模型可能使用过时但看似合理的知识，引发时间幻觉，影响输出准确性。特别是在医疗等时效敏感领域，旧信息可能造成严重误导。因此需要一种机制来显式建模知识的时间有效性。

Method: Chronofy 采用三层架构：1）在 Matryoshka 嵌入中设计专用时间子空间，使事实年龄不可剥离；2）在基于图的检索中引入可学习的指数衰减函数，衰减系数 $β_j$ 基于贝叶斯决策理论，近似潜过程的均值回归速率；3）使用信号时序逻辑（STL）鲁棒性函数评估知识的时间有效性，遵循可能性最弱链原则，以最陈旧证据限制最终输出置信度。

Result: 在时间知识图谱预测、TimE 时间问答基准和领域特定敏感性分析中，Chronofy 显著提升了检索精度，有效减少了时间幻觉现象，并能根据时间上下文不足自动触发数据重新获取机制，展现出更强的时效感知能力与可靠性。

Conclusion: 通过将时间有效性从表示到推理全过程显式建模，Chronofy 为 RAG 系统提供了可解释、可调控的时间感知能力，是应对时间幻觉问题的系统性解决方案，适用于高时效性应用场景。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems retrieve and integrate external knowledge to ground large language model (LLM) outputs. However, current RAG architectures treat all retrieved facts as equally valid regardless of temporal provenance, leading to temporal hallucination, where plausible but obsolete facts corrupt the output. A clinical lab reading from yesterday is actionable; the same reading from six months ago is noise. We present Chronofy, a three-layer neuro-symbolic framework implementing the Temporal-Logical Decay Architecture (TLDA) that embeds temporal validity directly into the representation, retrieval, and reasoning layers of RAG systems. Layer 1 reserves a dedicated temporal subspace within Matryoshka embeddings to make fact age structurally irremovable from the representation. Layer 2 integrates learnable exponential decay functions into graph-based retrieval, where the decay coefficient $β_j$ is grounded in Bayesian decision theory as an approximation of twice the latent process mean-reversion rate. Layer 3 applies Signal Temporal Logic (STL) robustness functions to evaluate the temporal validity of retrieved knowledge, not LLM output confidence, and enforces the possibilistic weakest-link principle to bound output confidence by the most decayed evidence in the reasoning chain. We evaluate Chronofy on temporal knowledge graph forecasting benchmarks, the TimE temporal QA benchmark, and a domain-specific sensitivity analysis, demonstrating that explicit temporal decay modeling improves retrieval precision, reduces temporal hallucination, and enables principled data re-acquisition triggers when temporal context is insufficient.

</details>


### [203] [CT-Merging: Consensus Directions and Task-Level Scaling for LoRA Adapter Merging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20561)
*Keumseo Ryum,Joonhyuk Kang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CT-Merging 是一种 LoRA-aware 的合并算法，通过估计任务间的共识方向并分配任务级的 RMS 系数尺度，解决了现有 SVD 基 LoRA 合并方法中系数不匹配的问题。它利用任务 SVD 子空间的重复支持构建公共基，减少对秩级别 SVD 幅度的依赖，在 DC-Merge CLIP 适配器基准上优于现有方法，分别在 ViT-B/32 和 ViT-L/14 上提升 2.56 和 1.51 点的平均归一化准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 SVD 基 LoRA 合并方法中，直接使用原始任务 SVD 的系数会导致系数幅度与任务更新诱导的系数差异大，造成性能损失；同时，继承系数虽保持高秩相关性但缺乏对任务特性的精确建模，因此需要一种更鲁棒的合并方式来统一方向与尺度。

Method: 提出 CT-Merging，通过任务间子空间的重复支持构造共识方向（common basis），并基于任务级 RMS 指标重新分配最终更新的系数尺度，降低对原始 SVD 幅度的依赖，实现更合理的系数融合。

Result: 在 DC-Merge CLIP 适配器基准测试中，CT-Merging 实现了优于当前最优合并方法的平均归一化准确率，相较于 DC-Merge 在 ViT-B/32 上提升 2.56 点，在 ViT-L/14 上提升 1.51 点。

Conclusion: CT-Merging 有效缓解了 LoRA 合并中方向与系数不一致的问题，通过共识方向和任务级尺度校准显著提升了多任务模型性能，为高效、可扩展的 LoRA 适配器部署提供了新思路。

Abstract: LoRA adapters provide an efficient way to specialize a pretrained model for many downstream tasks, but deploying one adapter per task requires adapter storage and task selection at inference time. Model merging addresses this issue by combining independently trained adapters into one multi-task adapter. Recent SVD-based LoRA merging methods mainly focus on constructing shared or task specific directions, while the coefficients assigned to the final directions are often directly from the original task SVD. On a fixed merged basis, inherited coefficients preserve component order with high rank correlation, yet their magnitudes differ substantially from the coefficients induced by the task updates. To address this mismatch, we propose CT-Merging, a LoRA-aware merging algorithm that estimates consensus directions from average task subspace projectors and assigns task-level RMS coefficient scales in the final update. CT-Merging uses repeated support across task SVD subspaces to construct the common basis, while reducing reliance on rank wise SVD magnitudes after direction construction. On the DC-Merge CLIP adapter benchmark, CT-Merging achieves superior average normalized accuracy compared to state-of-the-art merging methods and further improves over DC-Merge by 2.56 points on ViT-B/32 and 1.51 points on ViT-L/14 KnoTS-trained checkpoints.

</details>

Experimental validation on an Electrochemical Simulation (ES) dataset demonstrates that our pipeline significantly outperforms state-of-the-art point cloud baselines in prediction accuracy. Furthermore, the proposed method reduces the computational overhead by orders of magnitude, providing a scalable and efficient framework for high-throughput battery design and optimization.

### [205] [Fisher Widths: Local Learning Geometry and Anisotropic Recovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20578)
*Vu Khac Ky*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究统计流形上的高斯宽度复杂度，引入由费舍尔度量和逆费舍尔度量诱导的两个泛函：原生费舍尔宽度 $w_G(T)$ 与逆费舍尔宽度 $w_{G^{-1}}(T)$。前者衡量费舍尔信息诱导几何中局部参数波动的规模，适用于费舍尔正则损失，可实现小费舍尔球内的尺度估计；后者刻画由逆费舍尔信息决定的各向异性高斯测量的影响，对稀疏恢复问题提供双侧统计维数估计及支持敏感的恢复结果，并建立不同支持在费舍尔谱下的自然排序。最后，证明两者满足不等式 $w_G(T)w_{G^{-1}}(T)\geq w(T)^2$，表明费舍尔各向异性可转移复杂度，但无法同时降低相对于欧氏尺度的宽度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究统计流形上复杂度的几何特性，理解费舍尔度量及其逆度量在学习与恢复任务中的作用，揭示各向异性如何影响统计学习性能并建立理论边界。

Method: 通过定义基于费舍尔度量和逆费舍尔度量的高斯宽度泛函，结合统计学习与稀疏恢复中的几何分析，使用几何概率工具进行双侧估计，并推导出原生与逆费舍尔宽度之间的紧致不等式关系。

Result: 建立了费舍尔宽度与逆费舍尔宽度之间的乘积下界 $w_G(T)w_{G^{-1}}(T)\geq w(T)^2$；在学习中实现了小费舍尔球内尺度 $w_G(H_r)/\\sqrt{n}$ 的可达性；在恢复中得到支持敏感的恢复精度与统计维数估计，以及由费舍尔谱决定的支持排序。

Conclusion: 费舍尔各向异性在学习与恢复之间转移复杂度，但不能同时降低两种几何下的复杂度相对于欧氏尺度的水平，这一关系为统计学习的几何建模提供了统一框架。

Abstract: We study Gaussian-width complexity on statistical manifolds through a pair of functionals: the primal Fisher width $w_G(T) = w(G^{1/2}T)$, induced by the Fisher metric, and the inverse-Fisher width $w_{G^{-1}}(T) = w(G^{-1/2}T)$, induced by the inverse Fisher metric. The two widths play complementary statistical roles.
  On the learning side, the Fisher width measures the size of local parameter fluctuations in the geometry induced by the Fisher information. For Fisher-regular losses, we prove that the scale \(w_G(H_r)/\sqrt n\) is attained on sufficiently small Fisher balls.
  On the recovery side, the inverse-Fisher width captures the effect of anisotropic Gaussian measurements whose covariance is determined by the inverse Fisher information. For sparse recovery, the resulting geometry depends not only on sparsity but also on the position of the active coordinates in the Fisher spectrum. We obtain a two-sided estimate for the corresponding statistical dimension, together with support-sensitive recovery estimates and a natural ordering of supports with different curvature profiles.
  Finally, we establish a sharp relation between the primal and inverse-Fisher widths. On any common compact coordinate set $T$, they satisfy \[ w_G(T)w_{G^{-1}}(T)\geq w(T)^2. \] Thus, Fisher anisotropy may transfer complexity from one geometry to the other, but cannot reduce both widths relative to the Euclidean scale.

### [206] [Bayesian uncertainty estimation improves clinical decision making in medical AI agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20582)
*Frederik Hauke,Patrick Wienholt,Christiane Kuhl,Dyke Ferber,Jakob Nikolas Kather,Sven Nebelung,Daniel Truhn*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究利用蒙特卡洛丢弃法在多任务胸部X光分类器中生成表征认知不确定性（epistemic uncertainty）的信号，该信号能跟踪模型在不同训练集规模下的泛化能力，并识别出看似自信但易出错的预测。将此不确定性信号结合点预测后，错误检测的AUROC从0.74提升至0.77（ΔAUROC +0.023）。在一项2×2因子实验中，临床决策支持系统仅在接收到二元错误风险标志而非原始分数时有效利用该信息，使不可靠发现上的自信误诊率从8.5%降至2.7%。结果表明，认知不确定性包含超越点预测的决策相关信息，但其下游应用价值取决于信息传递方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医学影像分析中的机器学习模型通常缺乏可靠的置信度度量，限制了其在模糊或非典型病例中的应用。需要一种能够反映模型不确定性的机制，以增强临床决策支持系统的可靠性。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛丢弃法构建多任务胸部X光分类器（识别八种胸腔异常，使用137,593张训练图像），通过该方法生成认知不确定性信号，并评估其在不同训练集规模下的泛化性能；进一步设计控制实验，测试不确定性信号以二元风险标志或原始分数形式传达时对临床决策支持系统的影响。

Result: 添加不确定性信号后，错误检测的AUROC提升至0.77（Δ+0.023，95% CI [+0.014, +0.033]）；在临床决策支持系统中，仅当不确定性以二元错误风险标志形式提供时，才能显著降低自信误诊率，从8.5%降至2.7%。

Conclusion: 认知不确定性估计不仅提供了超越点预测的决策相关性信息，且其实际效用高度依赖于信息呈现方式。因此，在临床部署中应优先以清晰、可操作的形式（如二元风险标志）传递不确定性，以提升系统安全性与可信度。

Abstract: Machine learning models for medical image analysis typically lack a reliable measure of confidence, limiting their use in ambiguous or atypical cases. Here we show that Monte Carlo dropout, applied to a multi-task chest-radiograph classifier (eight thoracic findings, 137,593 training images), provides an epistemic uncertainty signal that tracks generalisation across training-set scales and flags confident yet error-prone predictions. Adding this signal to the point prediction raised error-detection AUROC from 0.74 to 0.77 ($Δ$AUROC +0.023, 95% CI [+0.014, +0.033]). In a controlled 2x2 factorial experiment, a clinical-decision-support agent exploited this uncertainty only when it was delivered as a binary error-risk flag rather than as raw scores, cutting confident misdiagnoses on unreliable findings from 8.5% to 2.7%. Epistemic uncertainty estimation thus carries decision-relevant information beyond point predictions, but its value for downstream agents depends on how it is communicated.

### [207] [Exact ReLU realization of affine one-dimensional refinement iterates via residual memory and offset frames](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20586)
*Boldsaikhan Bolorkhuu,Tsogtgerel Gantumur*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有有限支持矩阵掩码和紧支集连续分段线性输入及强迫数据的向量值仿射细化算子。通过建立齐次实现定理，证明当 $M \ge 3$ 时，任意有限仿射迭代 $W^n\gamma$ 均可被精确的固定宽度ReLU网络实现，深度为 $O(n)$。核心创新在于引入残差记忆控制器，将非可逆残差动力学替换为单射斜积结构，实现反向精确重播残差状态以支持霍纳型求和。偏移帧将强迫原子对齐至残差接缝之外，允许互补循环读取精确恢复其值。分支选择歧义仅出现在累积仿射状态已消失的位置。对于 $M \ge 3$，结果适用于任意紧支集连续分段线性强迫项；对于 $M=2$，该构造适用于普通帧接缝分离的强迫项。此外还给出了针对固定有限维连续分段线性强迫项的阶段依赖扩展，并记录了在开曲线、有限状态、希尔伯特与莫顿型递归构造下的线性深度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决向量值仿射细化算子在神经网络实现中的精确表达问题，特别是如何在有限深度下准确模拟具有复杂动态行为的分段线性系统。现有方法难以处理非可逆残差动态与强迫项的耦合，因此需要新的机制来保证状态可逆回放与精确计算。

Method: 基于齐次实现定理，提出残差记忆控制器，将非可逆残差系统重构为单射斜积形式，实现反向状态重播；利用偏移帧隔离强迫原子与残差接缝，确保互补读取能精确恢复值；结合霍纳型求和策略，实现高精度仿射强迫项的逐层展开。

Result: 当 $M \ge 3$ 时，任意有限仿射迭代 $W^n\gamma$ 可由固定宽度的ReLU网络精确实现，深度为 $O(n)$；对于 $M=2$，在特定条件下（普通帧接缝分离）也成立；进一步推广至有限维分段线性强迫空间，获得线性深度提升，在多种递归构造中表现优异。

Conclusion: 本研究成功构建了向量值仿射细化算子的精确深度有界ReLU实现框架，揭示了残差记忆控制与偏移帧设计在保持状态可逆性与精确重建中的关键作用，为分段线性系统的神经网络建模提供了理论基础与有效算法。

Abstract: We study vector-valued affine refinement operators of the form [
(Wγ)(t)=\sum_{j\in\mathbb{Z}} A_jγ(Mt-j)+B(t), ]
with finitely supported matrix mask and compactly supported continuous piecewise linear input and forcing data. Building on the homogeneous realization theorem for (B\equiv 0), we prove that, for (M\ge 3), every finite affine iterate (W^nγ) admits an exact fixed-width ReLU realization whose depth is (O(n)).
  The main new ingredient is a residual memory controller. It replaces the noninvertible residual dynamics by an injective skew-product and permits exact backward replay of the residual states required by a Horner-type evaluation of the affine forcing sum. Offset frames align the forcing atoms away from residual seams, allowing complementary loop readouts to recover their values exactly. The remaining branch-selection ambiguity occurs only where the accumulated affine state has already vanished.
  For (M\ge 3), the result applies to arbitrary compactly supported continuous piecewise linear forcing terms. For (M=2), the same construction applies to ordinary-frame seam-separated forcing. We also prove a stage-dependent extension for forcing terms in a fixed finite-dimensional continuous piecewise linear span and record the resulting linear-depth upgrade for open-curve, finite-state, and Hilbert- and Morton-type recursive constructions.

### [208] [Detecting Neural Network Failures through Spectral Analysis of Internal Activations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20590)
*Arunan J*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出Self-Detecting Neural Networks (SDNN)框架，通过分析神经网络内部激活的频域特征（即谱漂移）来检测模型误分类。利用短时傅里叶变换、小波分解和统计矩捕捉多尺度谱特征，结合课程学习训练轻量级检测器，在CIFAR-10上实现79.0±25.3%的AUROC，显著优于基于置信度的方法。结果表明，内部激活的谱特性可揭示输出层无法反映的故障信号，为提升模型可靠性提供了新方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于输出置信度的错误检测方法难以有效识别神经网络的误分类，因为错误信号在最终输出层被掩盖；而内部激活中存在可见的谱不稳定现象，提示可通过分析内部过程提升检测能力。

Method: 采用短时傅里叶变换（STFT）、小波分解与统计矩提取内部激活的多尺度谱特征，构建轻量级检测网络，通过课程学习在自然误分类、分布偏移和对抗扰动等渐进挑战数据上进行训练。

Result: SDNN在CIFAR-10上达到79.0±25.3% AUROC，显著优于MaxSoftmax（50.5%）和Energy Score（52.9%），提升约25-30个百分点；小波分解与统计特征贡献稳定，STFT作用尚不明确。

Conclusion: 内部激活的谱漂移是误分类的可靠指示信号，其在输出层被掩盖，因此基于输出的检测方法受限。本研究证明谱分析为提升神经网络可靠性提供了一条有前景的新路径，揭示了输出不可见的诊断信息。

Abstract: Neural network misclassifications exhibit characteristic spectral instability in internal activations that is invisible at the output layer. This phenomenon is identified and formalized as Spectral Drift -- the frequency-domain distance between consecutive layer activations -- with empirical validation showing that failures exhibit significantly higher drift than correct predictions (1.9% increase, p<0.001). This spectral signature emerges during internal processing but becomes masked in final outputs, explaining why confidence-based detection methods struggle.
  This work introduces Self-Detecting Neural Networks (SDNN), a framework that monitors spectral dynamics across network depth using Short-Time Fourier Transform, wavelet decomposition, and statistical moments to capture multi-scale spectral features. A lightweight detector network (5% parameter overhead) learns to identify failure-indicative patterns via curriculum learning on progressively challenging distributions: natural misclassifications, distribution shifts, and adversarial perturbations.
  Experiments on CIFAR-10 demonstrate that SDNN achieves 79.0 +/- 25.3% AUROC across three seeds, substantially outperforming confidence-based baselines including MaxSoftmax (50.5%) and Energy Score (52.9%) by approximately 25-30 percentage points. Ablation studies reveal that wavelet decomposition and statistical features make consistent contributions, while STFT's role remains unclear. This work establishes spectral analysis of internal activations as a promising direction for neural network reliability, revealing diagnostic information inaccessible to output-based approaches.

*Jan Linnenbrink,Jakub Nowosad,Marvin Ludwig,Anna Frederike Jablotschkin,Fabian Schumacher,Teja Kattenborn,Hanna Meyer*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出STeMP协议，分为概述、模型和预测三部分，包含元数据、预测因子、评估方法、软件工具等关键要素；配套开发R包及网页应用，支持手动或半自动填写，并提供错误预警功能。

Result: STeMP协议已通过GitHub发布并集成于R包中，可实现模型流程的标准化记录与质量控制，提升模型可重复性与评审效率，促进社区协作完善。

Conclusion: STeMP为时空机器学习建模提供了首个系统化、可操作的标准化报告框架，有助于推动环境建模研究的透明化、规范化与可复现性发展。

Abstract: Spatio-temporal machine-learning modelling is an important tool in environmental research. However, machine-learning models are highly sensitive to both the characteristics of the training data, such as its distribution, and methodological choices, including the cross-validation strategy. Each decision has impact and implications on the model itself as well as the estimation of the model quality and applicability for certain purposes. Taking into account the large role of machine-learning based maps of the environment in science and their transfer into practice, transparent reporting of spatio-temporal models, ideally using standardized model protocols, is essential to enable trust, transparency and comparability. However, such protocols are currently lacking for spatio-temporal modelling.
  We propose STeMP (Spatio-Temporal Modelling Protocol) to fill this gap by serving two purposes: standardized reporting to understand the model functioning as well as providing guidance during the modelling process by pointing at critical decisions and parameters. The protocol is structured in three sections: Overview, Model and Prediction. The Overview section contains metadata, while the Model and Prediction sections go into detail, describing predictors, evaluation and software, and further relevant elements of the modelling workflow.
  The protocol definition is hosted on GitHub and accompanied by an R-package (https://github.com/LOEK-RS/STeMP). The R-package contains a web application that can be used to fill the protocol either manually or in a semi-automated way from provided modelling objects. Warnings are returned from the protocol when common pitfalls are encountered, which may help authors as a guide through the modelling process but also support reviewers in the assessment of modelling studies. Via GitHub, incorporation of contributions and feedback from the community is encouraged.

### [210] [When Does Recurrence Become an Algorithm? Convergence Selection in Weight-Tied Looped Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20594)
*Tong Zhang,Junhao Hu,Yun Peng,Tao Xie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了权重共享的循环变压器（一个模块重复应用T次）何时能实现真正的算法。通过在群词问题上的受控实验，得出四个发现：(1) 预算定律——训练过程确立线性计算边界，每轮处理v个位置，速度由训练合同决定（v ~ n_train/T_train），SGD选择满足最低要求的边界，且可通过增加测试时循环次数来恢复延迟位置，从而得到合理的停止规则T* = ceil(n / v-hat)；(2) 架构先验决定算法选择而非表达能力——标准深度变压器学习并行扫描，而权重共享使其转向串行边界，即使提供对数深度扫描的位置地址也如此；(3) 计算复杂度所预测的“墙”并非真实障碍——NC1完全性无成本，但群阶（如S5的120×120算子）导致联合学习死锁，而算子优先课程可打破所有种子的障碍；(4) 机制具有可迁移性而非强制性——跨预算合同的热启动可转移算法并重新定价速度，而输入调度强制串行则失败。这些现象无法被传统方法捕捉，因它们仅在固定训练循环点饱和。本文提出头仪器（convergence-time scaling tau(n,i)），通过损伤锥验证因果关系，并证明其在分布内测量可预测分布外表现，优于尾部指标。结果在公开的easy-to-hard基准上复现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解权重共享循环变压器何时真正执行算法，揭示其内在计算机制与泛化能力，突破传统评估方法的局限。

Method: 在群词问题上构建受控实验，使用收敛时间缩放函数tau(n,i)作为头仪器，结合损伤锥分析验证因果性，通过热启动和课程学习等手段探究机制迁移性与算法选择。

Result: 发现预算定律、架构先验主导算法选择、非传统计算复杂度壁垒、机制可迁移性；提出有效评估工具，可在分布内预测分布外性能，且结果在公开基准上复现。

Conclusion: 权重共享循环变压器的算法行为由训练合同与架构先验共同决定，其机制具有可迁移性，传统评估方法无法捕捉其动态演化。引入的新工具可有效预测模型泛化能力，为理解深度学习模型的内在机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: When does a weight-tied looped transformer -- one block applied T times -- implement an actual algorithm? We answer with four findings from controlled populations on group word problems. (1) The budget law: free training installs a linear computation frontier, a mechanism that solves v positions per loop, whose speed is priced by the training contract: v ~ n_train/T_train (exponent 0.98 +/- 0.04, R^2=0.99), exactly unity under T=n training. SGD selects a frontier matching the minimum the contract demands; granting more test-time loops than ever trained rescues late positions at fixed input length, yielding a principled halting rule T* = ceil(n / v-hat). (2) Architecture prior, not expressivity, picks the algorithm: standard-depth transformers learn parallel scans on this family; weight tying flips the selection to the serial frontier, even when positional addressing for a log-depth scan is supplied. At matched depth and parameters, untied models extrapolate worst and fail to learn A5 at all. (3) The walls are not where circuit complexity says: NC1-completeness costs nothing (A5 generalizes fully), while group order does (S5's 120x120 operator deadlocks joint learning) -- and an operator-first curriculum dissolves the wall in every seed. (4) Mechanisms are portable, not mandatable: warm-starting across budget contracts transfers the algorithm in every seed, re-pricing its speed, while imposing seriality through the input schedule fails where free training succeeds. These results are invisible to standard instruments, which provably saturate at the fixed points trained loops converge to. We introduce a head instrument, the convergence-time scaling tau(n,i), validate it causally via damage cones whose slope reproduces v, and show in-distribution head measurements predict out-of-distribution fate where tail metrics do not. Results replicate on the public easy-to-hard benchmark.

</details>


### [211] [Are Single-Token Sparse Autoencoder Features Causally Necessary? Layer-Depth and SAE-Family Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20596)
*Seonglae Cho,Zekun Wu,Kleyton Da Costa,Rishi Kalra,Ilham Wicaksono,Adriano Koshiyama*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究分析了6个模型和3种稀疏自编码器（SAE）家族中的390万特征，发现单令牌特征在解码器空间中聚类更紧密且集中于早期层。零消融实验显示，在208个全层条件下，178个条件中这些特征的消融导致显著的对数几率下降，且深度影响损害是否级联或直接影响输出。跨家族因果关系差异超过家族内部尺度效应：同一基础模型上，GemmaScope和BatchTopK特征保持因果稳定性，而LlamaScope特征则表现出局部冗余性。目标令牌排名在消融后96-98%的时间内恢复至基线的2倍以内，且激活函数对比显示符号反转，表明训练方法是解释性主张敏感性的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究稀疏自编码器（SAE）特征在大型语言模型中的因果角色是否在不同SAE家族间保持稳定，特别是在单令牌特征这一可提供真实标签的诊断案例中。

Method: 采用全层深度的零消融法，分析3.9百万特征，涵盖六个模型和三种SAE家族，评估特征在解码器空间中的分布、因果影响及跨家族一致性。

Result: 单令牌特征在解码器空间中聚类更紧密，集中于早期层；消融导致显著的对数几率下降，且因果作用受模型深度影响；跨家族因果差异大于家族内部尺度效应，训练方法而非激活函数或规模是决定解释性主张的关键因素。

Conclusion: 跨SAE家族的解释性结论高度依赖于训练方法，而非仅由激活函数或模型规模决定，提示需谨慎对待不同训练策略下特征的因果解释。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoder (SAE) features are used to interpret and steer large language models, yet whether a feature's causal role is stable across SAE families remains untested. Single-token features that activate on one vocabulary item provide the diagnostic case where ground truth permits direct comparison. We analyze 3.9M features across six models and three SAE families using zero-ablation at full layer depth. Single-token features cluster 4.7x tighter in decoder space and concentrate in early layers (Layer 0 in GPT2-Small; L0-L4 in Gemma). Ablating them yields Benjamini-Hochberg-significant logit reductions in 178 of 208 full-layer conditions, with depth controlling whether damage cascades downstream or shapes the output directly. Cross-family causal differences exceed within-family scale effects: on the same base model, GemmaScope and BatchTopK features remain causally anchored, while LlamaScope features are locally redundant. The target token's rank recovers to within 2x baseline 96-98% of the time after the same ablation, and a controlled activation-function comparison reverses sign within the same model, leaving training recipe as the residual candidate. Cross-family interpretability claims are therefore sensitive to training methodology, not just activation function or scale.

*Afsaneh Mahanipour,Hana Khamfroush*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于梯度的联邦学习方法在临床机构因专业限制只标注部分疾病类别（任务异质性）时表现不佳，存在收敛慢和缺失标签导致系统性假阴性偏差的问题，亟需一种能有效处理此类异质性且无需大量通信的新型方法。

Method: 提出三种闭式操作：平衡标签投影以消除类别不平衡偏倚；每类绝对聚合法则从标注客户端上传的充分统计量中独立构建最优岭回归分类器；可选的分析伪标签精炼步骤将高置信度教师分类器的知识传播至未标注客户端。

Result: 在ChestXray14数据集上，四种不同缺失类别配置下，该方法相比最先进的联邦多标签方法FedMLP，平均提升18.44 BACC点和13.24 AUC点，同时大幅减少通信开销。

Abstract: Federated learning (FL) enables multiple clinical institutions to collaboratively train a shared disease classifier without centralizing patient data. In practice, however, each institution annotates only the pathologies within its area of expertise, so the federation operates under task heterogeneity: each client holds labels for a strict subset of the target disease categories while the remaining classes are entirely unobserved at that site. Existing gradient-based FL methods fail under this setting because they require hundreds of communication rounds to converge and because missing class labels introduce systematic false-negative bias that the model cannot correct without a principled mechanism. We propose an analytic federated learning framework for multi-label medical image classification under task heterogeneity. The proposed method replaces iterative gradient optimization with three closed-form operations: a balanced label projection that neutralizes class-imbalance bias by normalizing positive and negative contributions to equal total mass; a per-class absolute aggregation law that independently assembles the optimal ridge-regression classifier for each disease category from the sufficient statistics uploaded by its annotating clients; and an optional analytic pseudo-label refinement round that propagates missing-class knowledge from a confidence-filtered teacher classifier to non-annotating clients. The entire procedure requires at most two communication rounds, irrespective of the degree of task heterogeneity or the number of participating clients. Experiments on ChestXray14 under four progressively severe missing-class configurations demonstrate that the proposed method consistently outperforms the state-of-the-art federated multi-label method FedMLP by up to 18.44 BACC points and 13.24 AUC points, while reducing the communication.

### [213] [Scaling Interpretable Transformers with Parity Bottleneck Layers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20652)
*Andrew Mack,Kraig Yuheng Tou,Mark Henry,Zhengxun Wu,Lauren Greenspan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出ParityTransformer架构，通过深度奇偶性瓶颈（DPB）实现高效且稀疏的中间表示，无需显式训练即可获得可解释的特征，克服了传统稀疏自编码器（SAE）在内存和计算上的高成本问题。该方法在稀疏探测、特征吸收、可控干预等任务上表现优于后处理SAE，且其特征直接嵌入前向传播中，真正实现模型内部表征的可解释性设计。

Method: 引入ParityTransformer，采用深度奇偶性瓶颈（DPB），以参数无关的代数字典替代学习型过完备基，提供确定性非相干性保证；通过分层混合专家结构实现高效稀疏化，并设计硬件感知实现，显著降低稀疏激活与密集训练之间的开销差距。

Result: ParityTransformer在稀疏探测任务中表现不劣于后处理SAE，且在特征吸收、可控干预和因果推理方面更优；其特征天然存在于前向传播中，验证了模型使用的真实特征，为可解释模型的设计提供了新路径。

Conclusion: ParityTransformer通过设计实现高效稀疏与可解释性，标志着从后处理可解释性向构建时可解释性的转变，是迈向透明人工智能的重要一步。

Abstract: Language models are thought to exhibit the phenomenon of superposition, representing many more features than dimensions in their residual streams. Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) are designed to recover such features post-hoc, but training models that are interpretable by construction has remained impractical, as a per-layer over-complete bottleneck is prohibitively expensive in both memory and compute. To overcome this issue, we introduce the ParityTransformer, a GPT-2-scale architecture whose intermediate representations are efficient and wide / sparse by design. At each layer, a Deep Parity Bottleneck (DPB) replaces a learned over-complete basis with a parameter-free algebraic dictionary, providing a deterministic incoherence guarantee and eliminating the memory requirements that have prevented per-layer interpretable bottlenecks at scale. A DPB is a hierarchically structured sparse bottleneck which efficiently enforces sparsity using a multi-level mixture-of-experts approach: a hardware-aware implementation that closes the cost gap between activation sparse and dense training to a manageable interpretability tax. Empirically, ParityTransformers perform at least as well as post-hoc SAEs on sparse probing tasks, while out-performing on measures of feature absorption, steering effectiveness, and fine-grained causal interventions. Because subsequent computation acts only on features that survive the sparse bottleneck, the ParityTransformer's features are native to the model's forwards pass by construction, addressing the question of whether SAEs probe features the model actually uses during computation. We see this as a step toward training models whose internal representations are interpretable by design rather than recovered post hoc.

To address these gaps, we propose SalesLoop, a reinforcement learning framework that establishes a closed feedback loop between model predictions and real-world business outcomes.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Machine learning (ML) models are increasingly integrated into optical network automation frameworks to support tasks such as failure management, performance monitoring and resource allocation. In these environments, ML-driven predictions may be directly coupled with control-plane actions where incorrect decisions can immediately impact service quality, resource efficiency, and network stability. As automation levels increase, ensuring the reliability of individual decisions at deployment time becomes a critical requirement. Explainable artificial intelligence (XAI) techniques have emerged to improve transparency by highlighting the factors influencing ML predictions. In addition to identifying influential features, they provide insights into the underlying reasoning process of the model, revealing how different input variables contribute to the final outcome and how feature interactions shape the decision boundary. In this work, we introduce explanation-based runtime verification, an approach that exploits model explanations to assess the soundness of individual ML decisions before they are executed in the network control loop. The proposed approach evaluates explanation coherence and physics grounding consistency at runtime, enabling the system to defer or reject decisions flagged as uncertain. We demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach on a representative use case of lightpath quality of transmission classification. Experimental results show that explanation-based verification can intercept a significant fraction of erroneous decisions while preserving high automation rate.

*Salavat Ishbulatov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于准线性Fisher市场的框架，用于连接个人与组织规划系统中计划任务与实际执行记录之间的偏差。通过将计划任务视为预算受限的买家、已完成行为作为可分割商品，并引入融合文本、结构与时间信号的估值机制，构建了一个能实现预算约束、资源守恒及垃圾过滤的市场模型。引入卖方保留价格和买方现金选项作为市场机制，确保硬性预算上限与理论保证。针对市场算法在任务接近完成时的收敛难题，提出饱和阈值不动点解法，在满足对角占优条件下证明其存在性和局部唯一性。实验验证了该方法在随机与对抗性实例中的有效性。进一步设计去循环化多种子基准测试，揭示原模型对相似度噪声敏感的问题，由此提出熵正则化的一般化模型与自适应调节规则以增强鲁棒性。研究强调可复现性，讨论局限性，并关联到多触点归因、最优传输与在线Fisher市场算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有规划系统在连接计划任务与实际执行记录时采用全有或全无的绑定方式，导致真实相关但未链接的任务被孤立，且误判活跃目标为停滞状态。为解决这一问题，需要一种更灵活、可量化且具备理论保障的桥梁机制，以准确反映任务进展与资源分配关系。

Method: 将计划任务建模为预算受限的买家，实际执行行为作为可分割商品，构建准线性Fisher市场；使用融合文本、结构与时间特征的信号作为买家估值依据；引入卖方保留价格与买方现金选项两个市场机制以保证预算约束与资源守恒；针对任务进度趋近计划时的收敛问题，提出基于饱和阈值的不动点解法；并通过熵正则化推广模型，结合自适应规则提升对噪声的鲁棒性。

Result: 所提模型在理论上实现了预算硬约束、资源守恒与垃圾过滤；在随机与对抗性数据上验证了算法稳定性与有效性；相较于传统最优传输方法，新模型在噪声环境下表现出更强的鲁棒性，尤其通过熵正则化与自适应调节机制显著降低对相似度噪声的敏感性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的熵正则化Fisher市场框架成功弥合了计划与执行之间的鸿沟，不仅具备严格的理论基础，而且在面对现实噪声时展现出优越的稳健性。该方法为任务追踪、多触点归因与动态资源分配提供了新的建模范式，并为未来在线市场算法的发展提供了可扩展的技术路径。

Abstract: Personal and organizational planning systems maintain two records that drift apart: what was planned (a task's effort budget) and what was done (a logged action's duration and description). Existing systems bridge them with an exclusive, all-or-nothing link that strands genuinely related but unlinked effort and reports false stalls on active goals. We formulate the bridge as a quasi-linear Fisher market: planned tasks are budget-constrained buyers, performed actions are divisible goods, and a fused text/structural/temporal signal sets each buyer's valuation. Two market instruments - a seller reserve price and a buyer cash option - yield conservation, a hard budget cap, and a provable junk filter as theorems. We extend the market with a concave completion utility discounting progress as a task nears its plan; standard convergence theory for the market's algorithm does not transfer here, resolved by a satiation-threshold fixed point with existence (Brouwer) and local uniqueness under an explicit diagonal-dominance condition, validated empirically on random and adversarial instances. A de-circularized, multi-seed benchmark - observed affinity corrupted independently of the scored ground truth - surfaces a genuine weak spot: the market's sharp, zero-entropy equilibrium is more sensitive to affinity noise than entropy-regularized optimal transport's permanently smoothed one. We resolve this with a one-parameter entropy-regularized generalization unifying the two, plus a noise-adaptive rule for its regularization strength. We report full reproducibility parameters, discuss limitations candidly, and relate the result to multi-touch attribution, optimal transport, and online Fisher-market algorithms.

</details>


### [219] [CEDAR: Causal Edge Discovery for Autoregressive Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20696)
*Mohammad Fesanghary*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CEDAR 是一种用于稀疏自回归时间序列中滞后因果边发现的约束基方法，通过 AR(1)-残差化、U-中心化距离相关性筛选候选滞后，再对每个显著的跨变量滞后候选进行两次针对性的条件独立性检验，并每对变量最多接受一个滞后。通过稳定MCI剪枝步骤去除间接边，可选的确定性C节点用于调整指定的趋势类非平稳性。在稀疏情形下，CEDAR在筛选后仅需O(d²)次条件独立性检验，同时保持边级可解释性。当数据稀缺且变量表现出滞后1自动态时效果最佳；随着T增大或高阶自回归、同时多滞后效应常见时，具有更丰富条件集的方法更具优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在稀疏自回归时间序列中，传统因果发现方法在处理滞后依赖和非平稳性时效率低下，尤其在数据稀缺情况下难以准确识别因果边。因此需要一种高效且可解释的滞后因果边发现方法，以应对实际时间序列分析中的挑战。

Method: CEDAR采用两阶段方法：首先利用AR(1)-残差化与U-中心化距离相关性进行候选滞后筛选；其次对每个显著候选进行两次针对性的条件独立性检验，结合稳定MCI剪枝去除间接边，并引入可选的确定性C节点处理趋势型非平稳性。

Result: 在稀疏场景下，CEDAR仅需O(d²)次条件独立性检验，显著降低计算成本，同时保持边级可解释性；在数据有限且存在滞后1自动态的情况下表现优异；随着样本量T增加或存在高阶自回归/多滞后效应时，其优势减弱，其他更复杂方法更适用。

Conclusion: CEDAR是一种高效且可解释的滞后因果发现方法，特别适用于数据稀缺且系统具有滞后1自动态的场景，在稀疏结构下具备良好的性能和计算效率。

Abstract: We propose CEDAR (Causal Edge Discovery for Autoregressive Processes), a constraint-based method for lagged causal edge discovery in sparse autoregressive time series. CEDAR screens candidate cross-variable lags using AR(1)-residualized, U-centered distance correlation, then applies two targeted conditional-independence tests per significant cross-variable lag candidate and accepts at most one lag per ordered pair. A stable MCI pruning step removes indirect edges, and optional deterministic C-nodes adjust for specified trend-like nonstationarity. In sparse regimes where few lags survive screening, CEDAR requires $O(d^2)$ CI tests after screening while retaining edge-level interpretability. CEDAR is most effective when data are scarce and variables exhibit lag-1 self-dynamics; methods with richer conditioning sets become preferable as $T$ grows or when higher-order autoregressive or simultaneous multi-lag effects are common.

</details>


### [220] [Perspective Latents as an Architectural Condition for Causal Emergence in Active Inference Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20708)
*Hongju Pae*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在无奖励环境下的主动推断代理中，因果涌现通过集成信息分解（$Φ_r$）的表现。结果发现，$Φ_r$主要集中在慢速全局潜在变量 $g$ 中，其整体大小主要由架构决定，并随训练减少。学习的实质性影响仅在原子-组合层面显现：解耦导致符号反转并趋于环境不变，而向下因果则携带环境依赖性调整。研究指出 $g$ 是主动推断代理中 $Φ_r$ 相关时间组织的架构核心，反对将标量 $Φ_r$ 直接视为学习整合的指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究无奖励条件下主动推断代理中的预测组织如何与信息理论指标 $Φ_r$ 关联，特别是检验 $Φ_r$ 是否能反映学习过程中的整合增强。

Method: 构建一个分离快速感知潜变量 $z$ 与慢速全局潜变量 $g$ 的主动推断代理模型，其中 $g$ 由预测误差驱动且与策略梯度结构解耦，在无奖励的环境切换任务中测试 $Φ_r$ 的动态变化。

Result: $Φ_r$ 集中于 $g$，其总量主要受架构影响，随训练下降；学习效应仅在原子-组合层级显著：解耦使 $Φ_r$ 符号从负转正并趋于环境不变，向下因果承担环境适应性调整。

Conclusion: $g$ 是主动推断代理中 $Φ_r$ 相关时间组织的架构核心，标量 $Φ_r$ 并不能直接反映学习带来的整合程度，需结合层级分析理解其意义。

Abstract: A recent line of work measures causal emergence in reinforcement learning agents through Integrated Information Decomposition, reporting that $Φ_r$ grows with training and tracks reward improvement. For active inference, this raises the question of how reward-free predictive organization relates to such information-theoretic signatures. I test this within an active inference agent whose architecture separates a fast perception latent $z$ from a slow global latent $g$, where $g$ is driven by prediction error and structurally decoupled from policy gradients. In a reward-free environmental regime-switching protocol, $Φ_r$ concentrates in $g$; its aggregate magnitude is largely architectural and decreases with training. The substantive effect of learning becomes legible only at the atom-compositional level: decoupling flips sign from negative to positive and becomes regime-invariant under environmental change, while downward causation carries the regime-dependent adjustment. These results identify $g$ as the architectural locus of $Φ_r$-relevant temporal organization in an active inference agent, and argue against reading scalar $Φ_r$ as a direct index of learned integration.

### [221] [LLMs Get Lost in Evolving User Intent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20734)
*Jihoon Tack,Philippe Laban,Jennifer Neville*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究大语言模型（LLM）在动态对话中跟踪和执行用户意图演变的能力。尽管用户意图在实际交互中常随对话推进而不断变化，但现有评估大多基于静态、单轮设定，无法反映真实场景。为此，作者提出一个框架，将静态任务转化为多轮动态对话，使用户意图在对话中逐步揭示、修改甚至中途转向，同时保持原有评估协议不变，可直接复用现有基准测试。实验表明，即使在静态设置下表现优异的模型，在动态意图环境下性能显著下降，揭示了当前LLM在追踪演化意图方面存在根本性缺陷，这对未来作为协作代理的LLM发展构成关键挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型主要在静态、单轮、完全指定的任务上进行评估和训练，但真实用户交互是动态的，用户意图往往在对话过程中逐步披露、修改或改变。因此，亟需评估模型在动态意图下的表现能力，以推动其作为协作代理的实际应用。

Method: 提出一种框架，将现有的静态单轮任务转化为具有动态意图演化的多轮对话任务。通过在不改变原有评估协议的前提下，模拟用户意图在对话中逐步揭示、修订或重定向的过程，实现对现有基准的复用与扩展。

Result: 在多个任务上，模型在动态意图环境中的表现远低于静态设置，且不同模型家族均出现显著性能下降，说明强静态表现不能迁移至动态场景。

Conclusion: 当前大语言模型尚未具备有效追踪和响应用户演化意图的能力，这一缺陷在静态评估中被忽略，但在真实协作场景中至关重要。未来模型需在此方向上重点改进，以支持更自然、灵活的人机协同。

Abstract: As LLMs become more capable, they are increasingly deployed as collaborative agents, taking on user-delegated tasks through iterative interaction. Yet genuine interaction is inherently dynamic: users rarely specify their intent upfront, instead disclosing, revising, and reshaping it as the conversation unfolds. Despite this, LLMs are still predominantly evaluated or trained in single-turn, fully-specified settings, leaving open a fundamental question: how well do LLMs track and act on user intent as it evolves over the course of a conversation? To study this, we introduce a framework that transforms static, single-turn tasks into dynamic multi-turn conversations in which the user's intent evolves across turns--incrementally revealed, revised, and at times redirected mid-conversation--while preserving each task's original evaluation protocol, enabling existing benchmarks to be reused as controlled testbeds without new annotation. Across multiple tasks, we surface a consistent phenomenon: strong static-setting performance does not transfer to the evolving-intent setting, with substantial drops across model families. Our findings point to a fundamental gap: today's LLMs do not yet faithfully track and act on the user's evolving intent, a capability invisible to static evaluation yet critical for future collaborative agents.
