### [222] [Cardinality-Decomposed Loss: Matching Training Objectives to Relation Structure in Heterogeneous Recommendation Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20737)
*Parul Maheshwari,Amulya Paruchuri,Yiqing Zou,Alireza Sahami Shirazi,Farhad Farahani,Prakhar Mehrotra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对异构二分图中不同基数关系的Cardinality-Decomposed Loss（CDL）方法，通过结合交叉熵（CE）和BPR损失，解决传统单一损失函数导致属性嵌入退化的问题。实验表明，CDL能有效提升属性嵌入的可区分性，并在多数情况下改善推荐性能（NDCG），但需通过调节超参数lambda来平衡属性信号与排名任务之间的冲突。关键影响因素为语义对齐度和拓扑泄露度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统推荐系统中使用统一的BPR损失函数会导致属性嵌入退化，表现为几何结构接近随机，而这一问题不易被标准排名指标发现，进而污染用户嵌入，影响个性化等下游任务。

Method: 提出一种新的损失函数CDL，将交叉熵（CE）与BPR相结合，分别针对不同基数的关系进行优化；通过分析参数空间中的损失竞争现象验证了CE与BPR之间的冲突。

Result: 在五个数据集上验证了CDL的有效性，显著提升了属性嵌入的可区分性；当属性具有强偏好预测能力时，排名性能（NDCG）提升；当相关性弱时则可能下降，可通过lambda调节实现平衡。

Conclusion: CDL能够有效缓解因损失函数不匹配导致的嵌入退化问题，其性能受语义对齐与拓扑泄露双重影响，建议根据图结构特性调整超参数以获得最佳效果。

Abstract: Graph Neural Networks trained on heterogenous bipartite graphs form a common basis in recommendation systems. These graphs often express relations that vary in cardinality, for example, user-item preferences are one-to-many and user-attribute features are one-to-one. Traditionally, a unique loss function is applied for all of the network components which is often Bayesian Personalized Ranking (BPR). While BPR works well for the recommendation task, we find that it causes attribute embeddings to collapse to near-random geometry -- a silent failure that leaves standard ranking metrics largely unaffected and therefore invisible to conventional evaluation. This in turn pollutes user node embeddings, which are shaped by both edge types simultaneously, hurting downstream tasks like personalization, segmentation, etc. Here we propose a Cardinality-Decomposed Loss (CDL) that combines both Cross Entropy (CE) and BPR to enable the model to collectively optimize for relations across cardinalities. We confirm this CE-BPR conflict by showing the two losses compete in the shared encoder's parameter space. We evaluate CDL on five datasets spanning two structural configurations -- one-to-one attributes on user nodes (MovieLens-1M, Last.fm-360K, PayPal Audience Factory, BookCrossing) and on item nodes (Yelp) -- and find that CDL consistently improves discriminability in attribute embeddings. We also show that ranking (NDCG) improves when attributes carry meaningful preference signal, but conflicts with it when the correlation is weak. We use a lambda parameter to navigate this trade-off, and a lambda-sweep reveals that dataset behavior is governed by two graph properties -- semantic alignment and topology leakage. Semantic alignment measures whether the attribute predicts preferences, while topology leakage measures whether the graph's connectivity already encodes it.

</details>


### [223] [Adaptive Confidence-weighted Expansion for Trustworthy Multi-Omics Multimodal Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20742)
*Mohammad Raahemi,Ali Sekhavati,Alireza Maleki,Hamid Nasiri*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出ACE框架，通过生成互补模态并引入双层置信度机制，提升多模态融合模型在噪声数据下的鲁棒性和预测可信度，在多个多组学数据集上表现优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态融合方法在噪声或无信息数据下表现不佳，缺乏动态数据质量评估和可信置信度评分机制，限制其在医疗等高风险场景中的应用。

Method: ACE框架首先利用模态内相关性生成新的互补模态；然后采用双层置信度机制，分别对各模态进行可靠性自适应加权，并估算最终决策的全局置信分数。

Result: 在BRCA、KIPAN、LGG和ROSMAP四个多组学数据集上，ACE显著优于现有最先进算法，在分类性能和置信度校准方面均有提升，展现出更强的稳定性和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: ACE为多模态学习提供了一种更稳定、更可靠的融合方法，有助于推动其在高风险问题中的实际应用。

Abstract: Multimodal learning is a robust approach to improve predictive performance in applications such as medical prognosis. However, the clinical applicability of models that use multimodal learning is hampered by their poor performance under noisy or uninformative data streams. Present fusion approaches often lack robust mechanisms for the dynamic assessment of data quality and for the provision of a trustable confidence score on the final prediction. This dissuades their deployment in safety-critical settings. To address these limitations, we introduce Adaptive Confidence-weighted Expansion (ACE), a novel framework to enhance the trustworthiness of multimodal fusion models. ACE first enhances the multimodal space by generating new, complementary modalities from intra-modality correlations. It then employs a dual-level confidence mechanism that (1) adaptively reweighs all modalities by their reliability before fusion and (2) estimates a global trust score over the fused, final decision. To evaluate ACE, we used four challenging multi-omics datasets (BRCA, KIPAN, LGG, and ROSMAP). ACE significantly outperforms existing state-of-the-art algorithms in both classification performance and confidence calibration. Our framework provides a more stable and robust data fusion method that facilitates the use of multimodal learning in addressing high-stakes problems.

### [224] [GaugeQuant: Online Learning of Quantization-Optimal Bases from LLM Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20757)
*Miguel P. Bento,João Seabra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GaugeQuant 是一种在训练过程中通过引入 LogSumExp 损失项来打破 Transformer 内部连续对称性，从而选择更优的量化基底，减少激活值异常，实现高效低比特量化的方法。无需校准数据或量化模拟，训练开销极小，在 W4A4 和 W4A16 量化下显著降低困惑度，性能媲美需冻结模型和校准数据的后训练方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量化方法在低比特（如 W4A4）下性能受限，且常依赖校准数据或后处理步骤。本文旨在利用 Transformer 内部存在的连续对称性，通过在训练中主动引导量化基底选择，提升量化模型质量，同时避免额外的数据与计算开销。

Method: 提出 GaugeQuant，通过在损失函数中加入 LogSumExp 项以打破量化过程中的内部对称性，强制网络选择更稳定的激活分布；使用 stop-gradient 仅更新旋转矩阵，保证语言建模目标不变；整个过程无需校准数据、无需量化模拟，可直接在训练中应用。

Result: 在 LLaMA-2 7B 模型上，W4A4 量化下困惑度从 8.22 降至 6.73，W4A16 下从 11.16 降至 5.45，性能接近甚至超越依赖校准数据的后训练量化方法。

Conclusion: GaugeQuant 通过在训练中主动干预量化基底选择，实现了高性能、低成本的低比特量化，为大模型高效部署提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Transformers are known to have internal continuous symmetries that leave outputs invariant, while modifying quantization. GaugeQuant leverages this in-training by introducing a LogSumExp term to the loss that breaks the symmetries, thus selecting a basis that minimizes activation outliers. A stop-gradient operator ensures that only rotation matrices are updated, yielding the language modeling objective completely unaltered. Our requires no specific calibration data, no quantization simulation, and adds negligible training overhead. With the LLaMA-2 7B model under W4A4 quantization with group size 128, perplexity drops from 8.22 to 6.73, competing with post-training methods that require frozen models and calibration datasets. Under W4A16, perplexity drops from 11.16 to 5.45. Code is available at https://github.com/MPedraBento/gauge-quant.

### [225] [Memory-Computation Tradeoffs in Semi Amortized Parametric Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20769)
*Shijie Pan,Agustin Castellano,Zeyu Shen,Enrique Mallada*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在固定在线计算预算下，学习型决策系统为达到特定精度所需离线信息量的问题。通过分摊参数优化的视角，提出一种离线存储已解决问题实例、在线通过检索预热启动并执行K步投影梯度下降的方法。针对光滑凸参数优化问题，在紧致域上使用非参数预测器分析，对μ-强凸目标建立了匹配的上下界；对于满足β-增长条件（β>2）的凸目标，得到近似匹配的边界，并发现存在一个关于K的相变点，超过该点后增加内存不再有益。文章还提出了一个通用证明框架，量化了加速所需的内存成本，指出两个关键因素：在线优化器的收敛速率和解映射对问题参数的Lipschitz敏感性。实验在参数化岭回归中验证了预测的内存-计算-精度权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有学习型决策系统虽在实践中成功应用离线数据降低在线计算开销，但缺乏对所需离线信息量与精度、在线计算预算之间关系的理论理解。本文旨在填补这一空白，明确在给定在线计算资源下，达到期望精度所需的最小离线记忆量。

Method: 采用分摊参数优化框架，设计离线阶段存储历史求解实例，线上阶段基于存储信息构建预热起点，结合K步投影梯度下降进行快速求解。利用非参数预测器建模离线解，针对光滑凸及满足β-增长条件的凸问题，运用数学分析推导记忆需求的上下界。

Result: 对μ-强凸问题，建立匹配的上下界，精确刻画记忆需求；对β>2的凸问题，获得近似匹配边界，并揭示存在相变现象：当在线迭代次数K超过某一阈值后，增加记忆不再提升性能。此外，提出通用框架，量化加速所需内存，识别出收敛速率与解映射敏感性为决定因素。实验结果支持理论预测的内存-计算-精度权衡关系。

Conclusion: 本研究为学习型优化系统提供了清晰的理论指导，明确了离线记忆量与在线性能之间的定量关系，揭示了加速机制的核心驱动因素，并通过实验证明了其有效性，对高效智能系统的工程设计具有重要参考价值。

Abstract: Learning-enabled decision systems often use offline data or computation to reduce online compute cost. Despite the empirical success of such approaches, there is limited general understanding of how much offline information is needed to achieve a desired accuracy under a fixed online computation budget. We study this question through the lens of amortized parametric optimization: an offline phase stores a finite memory of solved problem instances, and an online phase produces a solution to a new instance by retrieving a warm start and applying $K$ steps of projected gradient descent. We analyze this setup for smooth convex parametric optimization over a compact domain, using a nonparametric predictor built from the stored offline solutions. For $μ$-strongly convex objectives, we establish matching upper and lower bounds on the memory required to guarantee $\varepsilon$-accuracy under a fixed online iteration budget $K$. For convex objectives satisfying a $β$-growth condition ($β>2$), we obtain near-matching bounds and identify a phase transition in $K$ beyond which additional memory provides no benefit. We further provide a general proof framework that (i) explicitly quantifies the memory cost of acceleration---how much offline memory is required to achieve a prescribed speedup over the unaided online optimizer---and (ii) identifies two key quantities driving this cost: the convergence rate of the online optimizer and the Lipschitz sensitivity of the solution map to the problem parameter. Experiments on parameterized ridge regression confirm the predicted memory--computation--accuracy tradeoffs.

</details>


### [226] [Toward Mechanistic Interpretability of an AI Foundation Model Fine-Tuned for Atmospheric Chemistry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20778)
*Jason Y. Hu,Ivan Higuera-Mendieta,Patrick Obin Sturm,Makoto M. Kelp*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究首次分析了微軟的Aurora模型在細調後對大氣化學的學習情況，通過施加受控化學擾動並測試其是否符合已知光化學關係，發現該模型雖能捕捉臭氧對活性氮的一階響應，但未強制執行過程模型中的化學約束，產生化學不一致的物種組合，且弱化如野火煙霧等局部排放特徵。內部表示仍主要圍繞預訓練時繼承的氣象結構，化學特徵結構有限。使用稀疏自編碼器識別出因果控制化學預測的內部元件，但這些元件不對應單一的大氣過程。研究提出了一套評估AI預測系統是否從再分析數據中學習到大氣化學機制的框架，強調未來應以內部機制而非僅以預測技能來評估環境政策決策中的成分預測。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 當前天氣預報基礎模型（FMs）被用於空氣質量預測，具有快速、低成本優勢，但其不顯式建模物理或化學過程，因此高預測精度無法說明模型是學習了真實化學機制還是僅利用了訓練數據中的統計規律。亟需評估這些模型是否真正理解大氣化學，以確保其在環境政策決策中的可信度。

Method: 對微軟的Aurora模型施加受控化學擾動，檢驗其預測是否符合已知光化學關係；分析模型內部表示，使用稀疏自編碼器識別因果控制化學預測的內部組件。

Result: Aurora模型能捕捉臭氧對活性氮的一階響應，但未能遵守化學約束，產生化學不一致的物種組合，並弱化局部排放特徵（如野火煙霧）。內部表示主要依賴預訓練時的氣象結構，化學特徵結構較弱。識別出的內部組件雖具因果影響，但不對應單一化學過程。

Abstract: Weather forecasting foundation models (FMs) are increasingly fine-tuned to predict air quality, offering fast global pollution forecasts at lower computational cost than conventional chemical transport models. These FMs are typically trained on reanalysis data and generate forecasts through autoregressive rollout. They do not explicitly represent governing physical or chemical processes. Therefore, high forecast skill does not reveal whether a model has learned physical mechanisms or exploits statistical regularities in its training data. Here, we present the first study of what a FM fine-tuned for atmospheric chemistry has learned by examining Microsoft's Aurora model. We impose controlled chemical perturbations on its forecasts and test them against known photochemical relationships. We then examine the internal representations that generate these forecasts. We find that Aurora captures a first-order ozone response to reactive nitrogen but does not enforce the chemical constraints that a process-based model encodes. It generates chemically inconsistent combinations of related species and relaxes localized emission features such as wildfire plumes toward background. Internally, its representations remain largely organized around the meteorology inherited during pretraining, with little structure specific to chemistry. Using sparse autoencoders, we identify internal components that causally control the chemical forecast but do not map cleanly onto individual atmospheric processes. This work provides a framework for testing whether AI forecasting systems learn atmospheric chemistry from reanalysis data. As these models are increasingly positioned to inform environmental policy decisions, we argue that composition forecasts should also be judged by their internal mechanisms rather than by benchmark skill alone.

### [227] [Synthetic minority data is redundant or invalid: a data-dependent validity theory and a de-biased test](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20787)
*Ahmad B. Hassanat,Ahmad S. Tarawneh,Ghada A. Altarawneh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种去偏的评估方法，用于检验合成少数类样本的有效性。传统方法通过将合成点与生成它们的数据进行对比来验证有效性，但该方法存在偏差。本文引入一个基于保留真实数据的稳健估计器，将有效性定义为合成点真正属于少数类的概率，从而更准确地衡量其真实性。实验表明，传统测试在96-99%的情况下严重低估了无效性，而新方法能更精确地捕捉真实情况。研究证明有效性是数据本身的属性，而非生成方法的特性：类别重叠设定了无法避免的无效下限，因此当类别可分时过采样冗余，当类别重叠时则无效。在91种方法、三种分类器和医学、金融等多领域数据集上的实验显示，即使某些生成器通过了传统测试，也未能同时满足有效性与信息增益的双重标准，多数方法对校准造成损害，且性能提升微弱（中位数F1低于0.01）。作者发布了一个可安装的审计工具，将证明责任转移至合成数据本身：必须在实际数据上证明其有效性和信息增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统合成少数类样本的方法依赖于不可靠的验证机制，即用生成数据自身作为评估基准，导致对有效性的误判。这种自洽性检查无法发现合成样本的真实偏差，尤其在类别重叠情况下会严重低估无效性。因此亟需一种去偏、可信赖的评估框架，以准确判断合成数据是否真正代表少数类，从而推动公平、有效的不平衡学习实践。

Method: 提出一种去偏的合成样本有效性评估方法，利用保留的真实数据作为外部参考，构建一致性估计器，计算合成点属于少数类的真实概率。通过比较合成点与独立保留的真实样本之间的分布差异，实现对合成数据有效性的量化评估。同时，建立双重验证标准：合成数据必须既具备高有效性，又带来显著的信息增益。

Result: 传统评估方法在96-99%的实验条件下严重低估合成数据的无效性；新提出的去偏估计器能准确反映真实无效水平。所有测试方法中，无一能同时满足有效性与信息增益的标准，大多数方法仅带来极微弱的性能提升（中位数F1 < 0.01），且破坏模型校准。结果表明，在类别重叠场景下，合成数据难以避免无效性，过采样并非普遍适用策略。

Conclusion: 合成少数类样本的有效性是数据固有的属性，受类别重叠程度限制，无法通过改进生成方法完全克服。因此，过采样在类别分离时冗余，在类别重叠时无效。研究强调应采用去偏审计工具对合成数据进行严格验证，并将‘证明有效性’的负担转嫁给生成方。未来应优先考虑非合成方法，或确保合成数据在真实数据上经过充分验证。

Abstract: For two decades, the standard remedy for class-imbalanced learning has been to fabricate synthetic minority examples, and the standard evidence of their validity has been a check that cannot fail: synthetic points are scored against the very data that generated them. We de-bias the check. Validity becomes a population quantity -- the probability that a synthetic point truly belongs to the minority class -- with a consistent estimator that scores synthetic points against withheld real data. Where held-out ground truth is available, the classical test underestimates true invalidity in 96-99% of method-by-imbalance-ratio cells, while the de-biased estimator tracks it closely. We prove validity is a property of the data, not the method: class overlap sets an invalidity floor no faithful generator escapes, making oversampling redundant where classes separate and invalid where they overlap. Across 91 methods, three classifiers, and datasets spanning medicine and finance -- including a generator engineered to pass the classical check -- none clears both bars: gains over the best trivial baseline are noise-thin (median below 0.01 F1, a decision threshold's reach), and most damage calibration. We release the audit as a pip-installable test and flip the burden of proof: synthetic minority data must now demonstrate, on the data at hand, both validity and information gain.

</details>


### [228] [Memoir: Should a Model Write to Its Memory While It Thinks?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20792)
*Jaber Jaber,Osama Jaber*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Memoir introduces a novel architecture combining per-sample fast memory, shared slow parameters, variable-depth latent recurrence, and a future-latent energy objective. The study tests the riskiest aspect: whether iterative memory rewriting during pondering harms performance. On procedural associative recall with key interference, a coupled arm (where each iteration can rewrite its own fast memory) is compared to a read-only counterpart under identical conditions. Despite having the same number of parameters, forward MAC count, data, optimizer, schedule, and seeds, the read-only arm significantly outperforms the coupled arm after 240 training steps (0.6557 vs. 0.5203), with a paired t-test confirming statistical significance (p < 0.05). However, both arms eventually reach perfect performance (1.0000) after 960 steps, indicating that the observed difference is a learning-speed penalty rather than a fundamental capability limitation. Notably, no failure due to memory rewriting corrupting the energy signal occurred—the energy margin actually improved. Additionally, kernel restructuring reduced forward time from 0.907 ms to 0.351 ms.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To explore the feasibility and impact of dynamic memory rewriting within a recurrent latent process, particularly in high-risk scenarios where an iteration might overwrite the very memory it reads during computation. The goal is to assess whether such coupling undermines learning stability or performance, especially in tasks involving associative recall with interference.

Method: A controlled comparison between two variants of Memoir: one with coupled memory rewriting (where each pondering iteration can modify its own fast memory), and another with read-only memory access. Both models share identical hyperparameters, parameter counts, forward MACs, data, optimizer, learning schedule, and random seeds. Performance is evaluated on procedural associative recall with key interference across multiple training steps and seeds. Statistical analysis uses paired t-tests and confidence intervals.

Result: After 240 steps, the read-only arm achieves a mean score of 0.6557 (95% CI: [0.5953, 0.7160]) versus 0.5203 (95% CI: [0.4522, 0.5883]) for the coupled arm, with a significant paired t-value of 3.23 (df = 11). The read-only arm leads on 10 out of 12 seeds. After 960 steps, both achieve perfect performance (1.0000), indicating the initial gap reflects a learning-speed penalty, not a capability ceiling. No corruption of the energy signal occurred—energy margin increased over time. Kernel optimization reduced forward pass time by over 60%.

Conclusion: Despite the theoretical risk of memory rewriting corrupting the energy signal, the coupled Memoir variant remains stable and effective. The observed performance gap is attributable to slower convergence rather than instability or failure. This suggests that dynamic memory updates can be safely integrated into recurrent architectures when combined with appropriate energy objectives. Furthermore, computational efficiency gains are substantial through kernel restructuring.

Abstract: Memoir combines per-sample fast memory, shared slow parameters, variable-depth latent recurrence, and a future-latent energy objective. We test its riskiest coupling: each pondering iteration may rewrite the fast tier that the same iteration reads. On procedural associative recall with key interference, we compare a coupled arm against an otherwise identical read-only pondering arm. Both arms contain 81,738 parameters, including 76,362 trainable parameters, and use matched declared forward multiply-accumulate counts, data, optimizer, schedule, and seeds. After 240 training steps across 12 seeds, coupled recall is 0.5203 with a 95 percent interval of [0.4522, 0.5883], while read-only recall is 0.6557 with [0.5953, 0.7160]. The arms are paired per seed, and the read-only lead of 0.1354 gives a paired t of 3.23 on 11 degrees of freedom with a 95 percent interval of [0.0431, 0.2277] on the difference, winning on 10 of 12 seeds. After 960 steps across 8 seeds, both arms reach 1.0000, so the measured effect is a learning-speed penalty at a fixed budget, not a demonstrated capability penalty. That longer control is ceiling limited, leaving convergence on a non-saturating task unmeasured. A predicted failure in which memory rewriting corrupts the energy signal did not occur: the energy margin grew and held. Kernel restructuring also reduced delta-rule forward time from 0.907 ms to 0.351 ms on the stated device. Code and evidence are available at https://github.com/RightNow-AI/Memoir

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有标量指标在评估聚类时忽视了信息性与简洁性之间的核心权衡，容易因损失压缩而误导评估结果。

Method: 基于信息瓶颈原理改进，提出不鼓励损失压缩的同质性与简洁性得分；扩展到集合匹配与成对评估，构建统一的评价框架。

Result: 所提方法在簇细化过程中具有单调性，优于已有方法；成对设置下的权衡等价于二分类器的ROC曲线；联合使用得分可有效识别帕累托最优解，提升特征选择与算法比较能力。

Abstract: Scalar metrics are often used to evaluate clusterings against known classes, but they can obscure a fundamental trade-off: clusterings should be informative about class labels while avoiding unnecessary fragmentation. Here we describe normalized scores of cluster homogeneity and parsimony that quantify this trade-off. These scores build on the information bottleneck principle, modified to not reward lossy compression. We show by example and mathematical proof that our definitions of these scores have the intuitive property of varying monotonically under cluster refinement in contrast to related proposals. Extending the information-theoretic framework beyond Shannon entropies, we furthermore derive set-matching and pair-based counterparts of the homogeneity and parsimony scores. These unify commonly used evaluation criteria and show that, in the pair-based setting, the homogeneity-parsimony trade-off recovers the receiver operating characteristic of binary classifiers. We demonstrate the framework's utility for feature selection and algorithm comparison, illustrating how considering scores jointly can clarify clustering operating points and identify Pareto-optimal solutions.

Abstract: In spite of the fundamental role of neural networks in contemporary machine learning research, our understanding of the computational complexity of optimally training neural networks remains incomplete even when dealing with the simplest kinds of activation functions. Indeed, while there has been a number of very recent results that establish ever-tighter lower bounds for the problem under linear and ReLU activation functions, less progress has been made towards the identification of novel polynomial-time tractable network architectures. In this article we obtain novel algorithmic upper bounds for training linear- and ReLU-activated neural networks to optimality which push the boundaries of tractability for these problems beyond the previous state of the art. In particular, for ReLU networks we establish the polynomial-time tractability of all architectures where hidden neurons have an out-degree of $1$, improving upon the previous algorithm of Arora, Basu, Mianjy and Mukherjee. ### [231] [Robust Asynchronous Q-Learning under Reward and State Corruption via Batching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20822)
*Sreejeet Maity,Aritra Mitra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对恶劣环境中强化学习的挑战，本文提出一种新型的、基于轮次的鲁棒Q-learning算法BR-Async-Q，用于应对奖励和状态观测同时被对手扰动的情况。该算法通过将在线数据流分批以降低方差，并利用批次数据构建鲁棒的贝尔曼最优算子估计。理论分析表明，该算法在高概率下具有与标准Q-learning相当的ℓ∞误差界，仅多出一个与污染样本比例相关的微小项。这是首个针对异步Q-learning在同时面临奖励与状态污染下的鲁棒性保证；当仅奖励受污染时，其对污染比例的依赖达到极小极大最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在恶劣环境中进行强化学习时，学习者可能面临来自对手的恶意干扰，包括对奖励信号和状态观测的双重污染。现有方法缺乏对这种联合污染的鲁棒性保障，尤其在异步更新场景下。因此需要设计一种能有效抵御此类干扰的鲁棒学习算法。

Method: 提出BR-Async-Q算法，核心思想包括：(i) 将在线数据按时间分批以减少方差；(ii) 利用批量数据构造对贝尔曼最优算子的鲁棒估计。算法采用轮次机制，结合统计鲁棒性技术（如中位数或截断均值）处理污染数据，确保估计稳定性。

Result: 证明了BR-Async-Q在高概率下满足ℓ∞误差界，其性能与标准Q-learning相近，仅多出一个与污染比例相关的小项。当仅奖励受污染时，该误差界对污染比例的依赖达到极小极大最优。

Conclusion: 本文提出的BR-Async-Q是首个在同时存在奖励与状态污染情况下实现理论鲁棒性的异步Q-learning算法，具有良好的理论保证和实际应用潜力，为复杂环境下的强化学习提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Motivated by reinforcement learning in harsh environments, we consider the problem of learning an optimal policy subject to adversarially corrupted feedback. Specifically, at each time-step, an adversary can perturb both the reward and state observations of the learner following the Huber contamination model. To defend against such data corruption, we propose {\texttt{BR-Async-Q}}: a novel, epoch-based, robust \(Q\)-learning algorithm built upon two key ideas: (i) partitioning the online data stream into batches to reduce variance, and (ii) constructing robust estimates of the Bellman optimality operator using such batched data. We prove a high-probability $\ell_\infty$ error bound for {\texttt{BR-Async-Q}} that matches that for vanilla \(Q\)-learning, up to a small additive term that scales with the fraction of corrupted samples. To our knowledge, this provides the first robustness guarantee for asynchronous \(Q\)-learning subject to both reward and state corruption. Furthermore, when only rewards are corrupted, the dependence of our algorithm's bound on the corruption fraction is minimax optimal.

</details>

Abstract: Advanced Persistent Threats (APTs) remain difficult to detect because only a small fraction of events in large-scale logs are attack-related, and investigation is expensive and hard to scale. Prior machine-learning approaches can reduce analyst workload, but they often rely on heavily curated training data and sophisticated preprocessing pipelines. Building and maintaining such pipelines require substantial domain expertise and engineering cost. Motivated by insights from a study of a strong APT detection baseline, we propose CAPTAIN (Context-Augmented Perplexity-based Threat Activity log detectIoN), a perplexity-based detector that leverages general, pre-trained language models with minimal, domain-agnostic preprocessing, enabling robust scoring of long, minimally processed log entries. CAPTAIN encodes recent history with an encoder model and a Q-Former-style bridge, then injects the compact context tokens into the decoder input so that perplexity reflects temporal context. To improve stability, CAPTAIN additionally applies smoothing filters to the perplexity time series. Across APT-oriented benchmarks, CAPTAIN competes with strong existing baselines and remains robust under substantially less curated inputs, that reduces the development and operational cost of advanced log preprocessing.

*Ahad Jawaid*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决离线目标条件强化学习在长时程任务中因时域诅咒导致的价值估计误差累积问题，现有层次化方法受限于低层控制器的短视执行和偏差价值估计。

Abstract: Offline goal-conditioned reinforcement learning (RL) holds the promise of learning general-purpose policies from static datasets. However, scaling these methods to long-horizon tasks remains a challenge due to the curse of horizon, where value estimation errors can compound through long chains of bootstrapped Bellman backups. Existing hierarchical approaches mitigate this by decomposing tasks into subgoals, yet they often rely on low-level controllers that suffer from myopic execution and biased value estimates. In this work, we propose Hierarchical Implicit Q-Chunking (HiQC), an offline goal-conditioned RL algorithm that combines high-level latent planning with low-level action chunking. By conditioning the low-level critic on temporally extended action sequences, HiQC enables unbiased k-step value backups, compressing the horizon at both the planning and execution levels. We theoretically demonstrate that this dual decomposition results in a tighter bound on value error under a bounded per-backup error model compared to standard hierarchy or flat chunking alone. Empirically, HiQC achieves the highest aggregate performance among the compared methods on the OGBench suite, with its largest gains on long-horizon navigation tasks such as humanoid-giant.

### [234] [Multilevel Graph Wavelet Compressed Sensing with Scale-Aware Neural Recovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20857)

Abstract: Scientific machine learning methods such as neural operators and physics-informed neural networks have advanced engineering applications and inverse problems, but their training typically requires large volumes of simulated data. This makes data preparation and model training expensive. We propose Graph Wavelet Compressed Sensing (GWCS), a learning-based framework for offline compression of graph signals by representing them as sparse, interpretable wavelet-domain representations using the spectral graph wavelet transform. The framework combines a nonparametric multilevel importance sampler, which retains high-energy wavelet coefficients within each scale for a given compression ratio, with a scale-aware graph neural network that reconstructs the signal from the sparse coefficients. We evaluate the proposed framework on synthetic approximately band-limited graph signals over random graphs and four PDE simulation datasets over meshes, which include Turbulent Radiative Layer, Viscoelastic Instability, Kolmogorov Flow, and Dynamic Stall. ### [235] [Position Bias is Hidden Behind Ceiling Effects: A Permutation Diagnostic for LLM Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20864)
*Hiroki Tamba*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 inspect_permute 工具，通过穷举答案顺序排列并结合卡方检验与 Cramer V 指标，量化多选题大模型评估中的位置偏差。在 24,000 次 API 调用下对四个厂商模型在五项 MMLU 主题上的表现进行分析，发现位置偏差仅在约 60-95% 基线准确率的“黄金区域”内可检测；低于此范围因处理负载干扰而信号淹没，高于则因天花板效应导致方差压缩。检测到的偏差分为两类：单调递减（低性能模型，归因于处理负荷）和非单调突降（中等能力模型，归因于内容模糊性）。由于前沿模型普遍超出可检测区间，其无偏差信号应理解为不可测而非无偏。该研究明确了位置偏差测量的可检范围，使领域核心问题可验证化。代码、数据及预注册信息开源于 MIT 许可。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对大模型多选题评估中位置偏差的测量依赖单次答案顺序打乱，易受内容噪声和采样随机性干扰，难以可靠识别偏差信号。亟需一种更稳健、可重复的方法来精确量化位置偏差，并明确其可检测范围。

Method: 开发 open-source 工具 inspect_permute，集成至 inspect_ai 框架，对每道题执行所有可能的答案顺序排列（穷举），利用卡方检验与 Cramer V 统计量评估位置偏差，并采用自举法计算置信区间。实验涵盖四家厂商模型（gpt-4o-mini, claude-haiku-4-5, gemini-2.5-flash, grok-3），五个 MMLU 主题，24,000 次温度为 0 的生成调用，且使用 SHA-256 哈希预先注册了假定预测以保证透明性。

Result: 位置偏差仅在约 60%-95% 基线准确率区间内具有统计显著性。低于此区间的模型受处理负载主导，内容信号被掩盖；高于此区间的模型因接近完美准确率，方差过小而无法被卡方检验捕捉。检测到的偏差机制可分为两类：单调的 A→D 减少（低性能模型，源于处理负荷）与非单调的 D 项骤降（中等能力模型，源于内容模糊性）。所有前沿模型均位于不可检测区间，因此缺乏偏差信号不能推断为无偏。

Conclusion: 本研究定义了位置偏差可测量的理论边界，将原本模糊的问题转化为可验证的科学命题。未来评估应避免在高准确率模型上错误解读‘无偏差’，并推动建立基于可重复方法的位置偏差评估标准。

Abstract: Position bias in multiple-choice LLM evaluation is widely cited as a confound in capability comparisons, but published measurements rely on single answer-order shuffles whose results confound the bias signal with content-level noise and sampling stochasticity. I introduce inspect_permute, an open-source extension to the inspect_ai evaluation framework that runs exhaustive answer-order permutations per question and reports the chi-squared / Cramer V signature of position bias with bootstrap confidence intervals. I apply the tool across four vendors (gpt-4o-mini, claude-haiku-4-5, gemini-2.5-flash, grok-3) on five MMLU subjects, 24,000 API calls under temperature-0 generation, with falsifier predictions pre-registered via a public SHA-256 hash before half the data was observed. Position bias turns out to be statistically detectable only within a roughly 60-95% base-accuracy Goldilocks zone. Below it, processing-load dominance swamps subject-specific signal; above it, ceiling effects compress the variance below the chi-squared test resolution. Detectable cells separate into two mechanism types: monotone A-to-D decrease (processing_load, in low-tier models) and non-monotone D-drop (content_ambiguity, in a narrow capability band). Standard MMLU places every frontier-tier model above the detection band, so absence of signal there should be read as not measurable, not unbiased. Together with the ceiling-effect characterisation in arXiv:2606.26185, this work brackets the detectable region of position-bias measurement and makes the field central question askable in a verifiable form. Package, data, preregistration under MIT.

### [236] [TwistedMerge: Certified Higher-Order Diagnostics and Abstention for Model Merging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20887)
*Ting Gong,Shitan Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为TwistedMerge的模型合并方法，将模型合并视为一个有限下降问题，通过引入对齐映射、循环残差和上同调类等概念，实现对模型合并过程的严格认证。该方法在满足逆一致性、系数识别、中心性与闭包测试后才将残差提升为上同调类，否则返回普通或同步回退。研究证明了无禁区结果、三向误差控制定理及比较复形敏感性检验，并表明仅循环得分非零并不构成更高阶障碍。实验显示，受控中心系统可恢复预测的非上边界行为，而噪声估计则从认证转向回避，避免虚假提升。低秩适配器审计表明，朴素因子平均依赖于GLr代表的选择，而全局因子同步和密集-ΔSVD具有稳定性。在自然检查点集合中，循环残差无法预测合并性能下降，也未发现自然中心或周期指数类被认证。整体结果将下降理论定位为可证伪的认证与回避框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将模型合并建模为有限下降问题，其中检查点为局部对象，对齐映射为转移，循环乘积为残差。引入上同调理论中的概念，如逆一致性、系数识别、中心性与闭包测试，仅当所有条件满足时，残差才被提升为上同调类；否则采用普通或同步回退策略。使用周期一致同步修复人工对齐缺陷，并通过对比复形敏感性测试验证方法有效性。

Result: 实验表明，循环残差不能有效预测合并性能下降，自然数据集中未发现可认证的中心或周期指数类。受控系统能准确恢复非上边界行为，噪声干扰下系统自动切换至回避模式，避免错误提升。低秩适配器实验验证了全局同步方法的稳定性，而朴素平均方法则表现出对表示选择的敏感性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的下降理论框架提供了一个可证伪的模型合并认证与回避机制，强调了在缺乏充分一致性证据时应保持谨慎，而非强行输出结果。

Abstract: Model merging combines independently trained or fine-tuned models, but pairwise alignability does not imply globally consistent alignment. We formulate merging as a finite descent problem in which checkpoints are local objects, alignment maps are transitions, and cycle products are residuals. TwistedMerge is a conservative certification pipeline that separates fixed-chart averaging, synchronization-removable gauge inconsistency, a certified central obstruction on a specified comparison complex, and nonabelian holonomy. A residual is promoted to a cohomology class only after inverse-consistency, coefficient-identification, centrality, and closure tests; otherwise the method abstains and returns an ordinary or synchronized fallback. We prove a constant-edge no-go result, frozen-complex three-way and predeclared-family error-control theorems, and a refinement test for comparison-complex sensitivity. A planted neural alignment defect is removed by cycle-consistent synchronization, showing that a nonzero cycle score alone is not a higher obstruction. Controlled central systems recover the predicted non-coboundary and projective-rank behavior, while noisy estimates move from certification to abstention without false lifts on the tested controls. A trained low-rank-adapter audit shows that naive factor averaging depends on the chosen GLr representative, whereas global factor synchronization and dense-delta SVD are stable. On natural checkpoint collections, cycle residuals do not predict merge degradation and no natural central or period-index class is certified. The results position descent theory as a falsifiable certification and abstention framework.

### [237] [Information-Theoretically Secure Aggregation for Lightweight Federated Learning: Resilient to Dropouts and Adversaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20890)
*Hyeong-Gun Joo,Songnam Hong,Dong-Joon Shin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种轻量级、信息论安全的聚合框架，专为基于符号的联邦学习（FL）设计。通过单轮安全乘法实现多数投票（MV）多项式的计算，在诚实多数假设下确保端到端的信息论安全性，仅向服务器暴露最终聚合符号。引入两项关键技术：逆形式指数约简将有效MV多项式度数减半，降低通信与计算成本；单轮安全乘法实现线性离线复杂度和存储，仅需一次在线通信。相比传统方法，线上通信减少高达99.5%，延迟降低85.7%。同时利用固有的MDS码解码机制，具备对丢包和恶意行为的鲁棒性，准确率提升最高达20.65%和10.74%。该框架为大规模、低延迟、信息论安全的符号联邦学习聚合提供了实用基础。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出基于单轮安全乘法的多数投票多项式计算框架，结合逆形式指数约简技术降低多项式度数，实现高效的通信与计算优化；利用MDS码特性增强系统对丢包和恶意节点的鲁棒性。整个过程在诚实多数假设下实现信息论级别的安全保障，仅输出最终聚合符号。

Result: 实验表明，所提框架可使在线通信量减少高达99.5%，延迟降低85.7%；在存在丢包时准确率提升20.65%，面对恶意行为时准确率提升10.74%，同时保持端到端信息论安全。

Abstract: On-device federated learning (FL) enables privacy-preserving and personalized model training on resource-constrained devices such as smartphones and IoT nodes. To reduce communication cost, sign-based methods (e.g., signSGD) transmit one-bit gradients. However, exposing gradient signs makes them vulnerable to inference attacks, while existing secure aggregation schemes are often incompatible with such methods or incur significant computational and communication overhead. We propose a lightweight and information-theoretically secure aggregation framework tailored for sign-based FL. The framework securely computes the majority vote (MV) polynomial through single-round secure multiplication, ensuring end-to-end information-theoretic security under the honest-majority assumption while revealing only the final aggregated sign to the server. To enhance efficiency and scalability, we introduce two key techniques. First, inverse-form exponent reduction halves the effective MV polynomial degree, reducing both communication and computation costs. Second, we propose single-round secure multiplication, achieving linear offline complexity and storage with only a single online communication. Together, these techniques reduce online communication by up to 99.5% and latency by up to 85.7% compared to conventional approaches. Also, by leveraging inherent MDS-code-based decoding, the framework achieves robustness against both dropouts and adversarial behaviors, yielding accuracy gains of up to 20.65% and 10.74%, respectively. Overall, the proposed framework establishes a practical foundation for large-scale, low-latency, and information-theoretically secure aggregation in sign-based FL.

### [238] [HierarchicalDAEW: Domain-Aware Edge-Weighted Graph Convolution with Evidential Uncertainty for Multi-Section Spatial Gene Expression Prediction from H&E Histology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20896)
*Kritanu Chattopadhyay,Soumya Chatterjee,Ondrej Krejcar,Debotosh Bhattacharjee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HierarchicalDAEW 是一种双图架构，用于从 H&E 组织学图像预测空间分辨基因表达。它通过领域感知的边权重卷积处理组织异质性作为显式结构信号，并结合蛋白-蛋白相互作用和组织特异性共表达信息进行基因层面的信息融合。模型采用证据不确定性估计，提供更可靠的置信区间，优于蒙特卡洛丢弃方法。在六种人类 Visium 切片上，其表现优于13个现有基线，且在多种子可重复性和负向控制下依然稳健。消融实验表明，领域感知边类型和分层深度均对性能提升至关重要，同时校准的不确定性估计可识别低置信度预测，便于病理医生审阅后用于临床决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前空间转录组学成本高、技术复杂，限制了其在临床中的常规应用。从 H&E 图像预测空间基因表达可缩小这一差距，但现有方法通常忽略组织结构，且缺乏对预测可信度的量化评估。因此，需要一种能够显式建模组织架构并提供可靠不确定性估计的方法。

Method: HierarchicalDAEW 采用双图架构：第一层为点图（spot graph），使用领域感知的边权重卷积（Domain-Aware Edge-Weighted Convolution）区分域间、域内和边界边，基于 Leiden 聚类结果学习不同类型的投影；第二层为基因图，融合 STRING-DB 的蛋白-蛋白相互作用先验与学习到的注意力门控机制下的组织特异性共表达，实现从标记基因集到更广基因面板的预测传播。可靠性通过证据不确定性估计实现，以生成校准良好的置信区间。

Result: 在六个涵盖乳腺、结直肠、前列腺和小脑组织的人类 Visium 切片数据上，HierarchicalDAEW 在与真实表达的相关性方面显著优于13个现有基线方法。其优势在多种子重复实验和排除位置捷径的负向控制中依然保持。消融实验验证了领域感知边类型和分层结构的必要性。校准的不确定性估计能有效识别低置信度预测，支持临床前人工审查。

Conclusion: HierarchicalDAEW 通过显式建模组织结构和提供可校准的不确定性估计，实现了高精度、高可信度的空间基因表达预测，具备向临床转化的潜力，为非专家实验室开展空间转录组分析提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Spatial transcriptomics assays remain costly and technically demanding, restricting transcriptome-wide profiling to specialist settings and preventing routine clinical deployment. Predicting spatially resolved gene expression from H&E histology could close this gap, yet current methods largely ignore the underlying tissue architecture and rarely quantify how their predictions can be trusted. We introduce HierarchicalDAEW, a dual-graph architecture that addresses both gaps. On the spot graph, a Domain-Aware Edge-Weighted convolutional operator learns separate projections for inter-domain, intra-domain, and boundary edges derived from Leiden clustering, allowing the model to treat tissue heterogeneity as an explicit structural signal rather than an implicit one. A second gene-level graph then fuses protein-protein interaction priors from STRING-DB with tissue-specific co-expression through learned attention gating, propagating predictions from a landmark gene set to a broader gene panel. Reliability is handled through evidential uncertainty estimation, which produces far better calibrated confidence intervals than Monte Carlo dropout under identical conditions. Across six human Visium sections spanning breast, colorectal, prostate, and cerebellar tissue, and against thirteen published baselines, HierarchicalDAEW achieves the strongest correlation with ground-truth expression, with gains that hold up under multi-seed reproducibility checks and negative controls that rule out positional shortcuts. Ablations further confirm that both the domain-aware edge typing and the hierarchical depth are necessary to this improvement, and calibrated uncertainty estimates identify low-confidence predictions for pathologist review before clinical action.

</details>


### [239] [Multi-turn RL with Structural and Performance Aware Rewards for CUDA Kernel Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20908)
*Quazi Ishtiaque Mahmud,Nesreen K. Ahmed,Ali Jannesari*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CudaPerf提出一种新的强化学习框架，结合可验证的执行奖励和基于并行化特征的结构化代码奖励（如内存聚合、占用率、计算强度、同步模式），以优化LLMs生成的CUDA代码。该框架分两阶段：离线成对排序模块通过对比学习区分优劣代码候选；在线RL训练阶段联合优化正确性、性能与结构效率。通过迭代精炼和执行反馈实现持续改进。构建了包含2.9k C到CUDA和1k PyTorch到CUDA程序的数据集，涵盖多种输入配置和优化策略。在多个基准测试中显著优于基线模型，最高实现5倍和3.32倍加速，正确率提升17%和7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR方法主要依赖结果层面的奖励信号（如正确性和加速比），忽视了程序关键的结构性性能特征，导致生成的代码在实际并行执行中表现不佳。为提升生成代码的运行效率与结构合理性，需引入更细粒度的结构感知奖励机制。

Method: 提出CudaPerf框架，包含两个阶段：(1) 离线阶段使用对比学习进行成对排名，识别强/弱代码候选；(2) 在线阶段采用统一奖励信号联合优化正确性、性能与结构效率，并通过执行反馈进行迭代精炼。引入基于并行化特征的结构奖励，包括内存共用、设备占用率、算术强度和同步模式等。

Result: 在C to CUDA和PyTorch to CUDA任务上，CudaPerf相比Qwen-3-32B和CUDA Agent分别实现了最高5倍和3.32倍的加速比提升，正确率分别提高17%和7%。实验表明其在性能与结构质量方面均显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: CudaPerf通过融合结构感知奖励与执行反馈，在代码生成中有效提升了代码的正确性与性能，证明了结构化奖励在优化高性能计算代码生成中的重要性，为未来智能编译器与自动代码优化提供了新范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a powerful technique to enhance the reasoning capacity of LLMs for optimized code generation. However, existing RLVR approaches primarily rely on outcome-based signals such as correctness and speedup, overlooking performance-critical structural properties of programs that are essential for generating optimized code. In this work, we propose CudaPerf, a reflective RL framework that incorporates both verifiable execution rewards and structural code-aware rewards derived from parallelization features (e.g., memory coalescing, occupancy, Arithmatic Intensity, and synchronization patterns). CudaPerf operates in two stages: (1) an offline pairwise ranking module that learns to distinguish strong and weak program candidates via contrastive comparisons, and (2) an online RL training phase that jointly optimizes for correctness, performance, and structural efficiency through a unified reward signal. To further enhance learning, CudaPerf utilizes iterative refinement using execution feedback enabling progressive improvement of generated candidates. We also introduce a dataset comprising 2.9k C to CUDA and 1k PyTorch to CUDA programs, each paired with diverse input configurations and multiple CUDA implementations encompassing diverse optimization strategies. CudaPerf is evaluated across multiple benchmarks comprising both C to CUDA and PyTorch to CUDA transformations. Empirical findings suggest that CudaPerf significantly outperforms strong baselines, including Qwen-3-32B (for C to CUDA) and CUDA Agent (for PyTorch to CUDA) by achieving up to 5X & 3.32X improvements in speedup, and 17% & 7% improvements in correctness, respectively.

### [240] [Three-Pronged Spectral Control for Federated Parameter Efficient Fine Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20914)
*Shiva Raj Pokhrel,Dipsan Bhattarai,Anwar Walid*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TRISHUL 是一种用于联邦参数高效微调（PEFT）的谱控制框架，通过共享冻结的多头低秩基实现精确聚合，利用核范数近端收缩抑制客户端特有的高秩谱分量，并采用凹水填充预算规则非均匀分配适应头。该方法在不增加通信开销的前提下，显著提升了在非独立同分布（non-IID）数据下的收敛性、稳定性和性能，尤其在强异构场景下表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有联邦低秩适配（LoRA）方法在面对客户端数据非独立同分布（non-IID）时，因局部更新子空间谱对齐失败，导致聚合方差大、全局迁移性能差，亟需一种能有效控制谱结构、提升鲁棒性的联邦PEFT方法。

Method: TRISHUL 采用共享冻结的多头低秩基实现核心更新的代数精确聚合；在上传前对小规模核心矩阵施加核范数近端收缩以抑制客户端特有高秩成分；基于预训练模型各层容量，使用凹水填充策略非均匀分配适应头资源。

Result: 在视觉与语言多个基准测试（如CIFAR-100、SVHN、20 Newsgroups、MRQA、GLUE及LLaMA3.2-1B）上，TRISHUL 显著优于联邦LoRA基线，提升收敛速度、稳定性与最终性能，且在强异构条件下优势更为明显。

Conclusion: TRISHUL 通过谱控制机制实现了高效、鲁棒的联邦参数高效微调，在保持低计算与通信开销的同时，有效缓解了非IID环境下由谱错位引发的聚合问题，为边缘场景中的大规模模型适应提供了新范式。

Abstract: Federated parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) enables communication-efficient adaptation of large pretrained models on decentralized edge data, but it remains fragile under non-IID client heterogeneity. In low-rank adaptation (LoRA), different clients may learn locally useful but spectrally misaligned update subspaces, causing high-variance aggregation and poor global transfer. We propose TRISHUL, a spectral-control framework for robust federated PEFT. TRISHUL follows the FL no-raw-data-sharing setting but does not itself provide formal privacy guarantees. TRISHUL uses shared frozen multi-head low-rank bases to obtain algebraically exact aggregation of compact core updates, applies nuclear norm proximal shrinkage to suppress client-specific high-rank spectral components before upload, and allocates adaptation heads non-uniformly across layers using a concave water filling budget rule derived from pretrained layer capacity. Because shrinkage is performed only on small core matrices, TRISHUL adds negligible computation and no extra per-round communication over the underlying multi-head PEFT protocol. Across vision and language benchmarks, including CIFAR-100, SVHN, 20 Newsgroups, MRQA, and GLUE with LLaMA3.2-1B, TRISHUL improves convergence, stability, and final performance over federated LoRA baselines, with greater gains under stronger heterogeneity.

### [241] [Best-of-Evidence: Best-of-N Selection under Partial Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20950)
*Cenwei Zhang,Teng Fang,Yuxia Wang,Derek Li,Bryan Dai,Lei You*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Best-of-Evidence（BoE）框架，用于在部分验证条件下进行推理时的候选生成选择。与传统的Best-of-N（BoN）不同，BoE通过构建带符号的候选-因子图来表示可复用的主张，并在有限预算下执行证据操作以改变最终决策。该方法在无预算情况下退化为原始BoN，且理论上证明了残余证据容量对改进的限制，以及共享因子查询可实现从Θ(K)到O(log K)的查询效率提升。实验在四个医疗视觉问答任务中验证了BoE的有效性，表明其在证据可靠、对比性强且与决策相关时能提升固定池选择并补救BoN失败，但也揭示了通道质量与候选生成能力的瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多视觉语言任务仅支持部分验证（如片段、值、区域等），而无法依赖完整响应的可信验证器；同时，同一主张可能在不同候选中呈现相反立场，导致信息冲突。传统BoN方法在此类场景下受限，因此需要一种适应部分验证的新选择机制。

Method: 提出BoE框架，保持BoN候选池不变，使用带符号的候选-因子图表示可复用的主张，并引入有限预算下的证据行动机制来动态调整最终选择；设计基于分数的控制器，实现对证据价值的评估与调度。

Result: 在四个医疗视觉问答任务上的实验表明，当证据可靠、具有对比性和决策相关性时，BoE能够有效提升固定池的选择性能，并修复部分BoN失败案例；但其增益受制于通道质量和候选生成能力，无法实现普遍提升。

Conclusion: BoE是一种适用于部分验证场景的实用推理选择框架，能够在证据驱动下改善决策，但其性能上限由证据容量、通道质量和候选生成质量共同决定。

Abstract: BoN improves model outputs by sampling several candidates and selecting one with a proxy score, but it assumes that complete candidates can be evaluated reliably. Many vision-language tasks instead provide only partial verification: a finding, span, value, region, or relation may be checkable even when no dependable whole-response verifier exists. Moreover, the same claim may recur across candidates with opposing stances, allowing one observation to support part of the pool and contradict another. We introduce Best-of-Evidence (BoE), an inference-time selection framework that keeps the BoN candidate pool fixed, represents reusable claims with a signed candidate--factor graph, and allocates a limited budget to evidence actions that can change the final choice. BoE formalizes selection under partial verification and provides a practical score-based controller, with the zero-budget case recovering the underlying BoN decision. Theoretically, we show that residual evidence capacity limits any evidence-driven improvement and that shared factor queries can achieve an O(log K) versus Θ(K) query separation in a factor-code model. Common-ledger experiments on four medical VQA settings show that BoE can improve fixed-pool selection and rescue some BoN failures when evidence is reliable, contrastive, and decision-relevant, while also revealing the channel-quality and candidate-generation limits that prevent universal gains.

</details>


### [242] [The Weight of Silence: A Causal Case for Weights Over the Scratchpad in Latent Chess Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20952)
*Ishan S. Kshirsagar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过在国际象棋任务中引入渐进式隐式推理课程并进行强化学习（RL），发现模型的走法合法性从48%提升至61%，且完全消除误判将死的情况。通过六种因果干预实验发现，隐式思考向量的内容对性能影响较小，但经过RL后模型对噪声干扰更具鲁棒性，表明强化学习并未增强对隐式思考内容的依赖，反而提升了模型参数的稳定性。结果挑战了主流观点——即隐式推理是推理时主动调用的‘内部草稿板’，而更支持其主要作用是在训练阶段塑造模型参数。此外，该研究首次在非数学/逻辑领域（国际象棋）成功实现强化学习带来的性能增益，突破了以往同类方法在类似任务中失效的局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究普遍假设语言模型的隐式推理作为推理时主动查阅的内部草稿板，但这一假设尚未在强化学习环境下得到直接验证。尤其缺乏在模型训练前后对比分析隐式推理依赖性的实证研究，且多数分析局限于数学与逻辑任务。本研究旨在检验强化学习是否改变模型对隐式推理的依赖，并拓展到非传统领域（如国际象棋）以验证该范式的有效性。

Method: 采用渐进式隐式推理课程训练国际象棋模型，随后施加强化学习。通过六种因果干预手段（替换、添加噪声、完全移除等）对比模型在训练前后的表现，重点评估隐式思考向量内容的重要性及其对扰动的鲁棒性变化。同时，量化合法性与误判将死率等指标，分析强化学习带来的影响。

Result: 强化学习使走法合法性从48%升至61%，并将误判将死现象完全消除。在因果干预中，仅当使用精确零向量时性能崩溃；而经强化学习后，即使在精确零条件下，合法性仍保持9%（此前为1%），显示显著鲁棒性提升。其他扰动条件虽趋势相似但未达统计显著。结果表明，强化学习增强了对隐式推理扰动的鲁棒性，而非增加对其内容的依赖。

Conclusion: 隐式推理的主要作用并非在推理时作为主动查阅的‘内部草稿板’，而是通过训练过程塑造模型参数。强化学习带来的性能提升源于模型整体鲁棒性的增强，而非对隐式思想内容的更深度利用。该研究在国际象棋这一非数学/逻辑任务中成功实现了强化学习的有效增益，打破了先前相关方法在类似任务中失效的记录。

Abstract: Latent, or silent, reasoning lets language models carry out intermediate computation in continuous vector space instead of words, and is widely assumed to function as an internal scratchpad the model actively consults during inference. Whether that assumption survives reinforcement learning has not been tested directly: existing causal analyses of latent reasoning are confined to math and logic tasks, and compare a model's reliance on its thoughts within a single checkpoint, never before and after an RL stage. We train a chess-playing model through a staged latent-reasoning curriculum followed by reinforcement learning, and find legality climbs monotonically to 61% (from a 48% pre-RL baseline) while checkmate confabulation is eliminated entirely. To locate this gain, we run a six-condition causal intervention suite on the same model before and after RL: substituting or adding matched noise to the latent thought vectors leaves performance unchanged, ablating them causes only mild degradation, and only exact-zero vectors cause collapse. This robustness gap is itself the finding: under exact-zero corruption, legality collapses to 1% pre-RL versus 9% post-RL, a gap that survives correction for testing across the full battery; milder conditions trend similarly without independently reaching significance. RL appears to add robustness to disruption, not reliance on thought content. These results push back against the field's default assumption that latent thoughts function as an actively consulted inference-time scratchpad, and instead indicate latent reasoning's principal effect here is shaping the model's parameters during training. We also demonstrate a working RL gain in chess, a domain outside the math and logic settings where multiple groups report the same latent-reasoning-plus-RL recipe failing to improve accuracy over SFT.

</details>


### [243] [ADABORD: a novel AdaBoost approach for ordinal classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21003)
*Rafael Ayllón-Gavilán,Francisco José Martínez-Estudillo,David Guijo-Rubio,César Hervás-Martínez,Pedro A. Gutiérrez*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ADABORD 是一种专为序数分类（OC）设计的 AdaBoost 框架，通过引入序数 Gini 分割准则的决策树和基于绝对排名概率得分的误差函数，充分利用了类别的有序信息。在 TOC-UCO 基准库上的实验表明，ADABORD 在五类及以上数据集上显著优于现有方法，尤其在体现更强序数结构的数据上表现突出。代码与实验协议公开，支持可复现性与未来研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有序数分类方法大多将问题视为名义分类，未能充分挖掘类别间的有序关系，导致性能潜力未被释放。因此，亟需一种能有效利用序数信息的新型学习框架。

Method: 提出 ADABORD 框架，将序数特性融入 AdaBoost 的两个核心组件：1）使用具有序数 Gini 切分标准的决策树作为基学习器；2）采用绝对排名概率得分作为误差函数，用于更新样本权重及集成模型中分类器的权重，从而同时考虑类别顺序与距离。

Result: 在 TOC-UCO 基准集合上的大量实验及统计分析显示，ADABORD 显著优于七种先进方法，尤其在五类及以上数据集上优势明显，证明其对序数结构的有效建模能力。

Conclusion: ADABORD 通过系统融合序数信息于基学习器与误差度量中，在序数分类任务中展现出优越性能，为该领域提供了高效、可复现的新范式。

Abstract: Ordinal Classification (OC) deals with classification tasks where the classes follow a natural order. Despite the progress in OC, many existing approaches fail to fully leverage the ordinal information, treating the problem as nominal classification and thereby losing performance potential. In this work, ADABORD, an AdaBoost framework specifically designed for ordinal classification problems, is introduced. The ordinal nature of the classes is incorporated into two key components of the well-known AdaBoost algorithm: 1) the base estimator, where decision trees with the ordinal Gini splitting criterion are proposed; 2) the error function used to update sample weights at each stage and the weights of the classifier in the final ensemble model, given by the absolute ranked probability score, a measure that accounts for both the ordering and the distance between classes. ADABORD is extensively compared against seven state-of-the-art methods on the TOC-UCO repository, the largest benchmark collection for OC to date. The experimental results, supported by statistical analysis, show that ADABORD significantly outperforms competing methods, particularly on datasets with five or more classes, where the ordinal structure becomes more pronounced. Source code, along with all experimental protocols, is publicly available to ensure reproducibility and facilitate future research in OC.

### [244] [Weight-norm Criticality: A Mechanism for Loss Spikes Induced by the Normalization and Weight Decay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21005)
*Xiaolong Li,Zhangchen Zhou,Zhi-Qin John Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出在深度神经网络训练中，除了常见的学习率临界性（如边缘稳定性）外，还存在一种被忽视的权重范数临界性（weight-norm criticality）。该现象源于归一化带来的尺度不变性与权重衰减对参数范数的持续收缩之间的相互作用。随着权重衰减系数增大，尺度不变权重的范数逐渐趋近于零，同时损失曲面的尖锐度急剧上升，导致优化动态失稳并引发突增的损失。这一机制解释了为何权重惩罚有助于提升泛化能力但不能过强——过强的衰减会越过临界边界，破坏训练稳定性。作者通过实验证实了该理论的可预测性，为损失尖峰提供了新的机理理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多聚焦于学习率临界性导致的训练不稳定性，但忽略了权重衰减与归一化共同作用下可能引发的权重范数临界性。该问题在实践中影响模型训练的稳定性与性能，亟需从新角度揭示其内在机制。

Method: 通过分析归一化层与权重衰减的交互作用，构建理论模型解释权重范数随衰减系数变化的行为；利用损失曲面尖锐度指标和权重范数演化路径，识别临界点；设计实验验证理论预测，包括在具有尺度不变性的网络结构中观察损失尖峰与权重范数变化的关系。

Result: 实证结果表明，当权重衰减过大时，尺度不变权重的范数显著下降，损失曲面变得极度尖锐，训练中出现明显的损失尖峰。这些现象与理论预测高度一致，支持了权重范数临界性的存在及其对训练不稳定的决定性作用。

Conclusion: 权重范数临界性是深度神经网络训练中不可忽视的重要机制，它解释了权重衰减过度导致训练崩溃的原因。该发现不仅深化了对训练不稳定性的理解，还为超参数选择（尤其是权重衰减强度）提供了新的指导原则。

Abstract: Most explanations of training instability focus on \emph{learning-rate criticality}, typically characterized by the Edge of Stability, beyond which optimization becomes unstable. We argue that, in practical deep neural network training, there is an additional and often overlooked \emph{weight-norm criticality}. This criticality is induced by the interaction between normalization (which introduces scale-invariant components) and weight decay (which persistently shrinks parameter norms). As the weight decay coefficient increases, the norms of scale-invariant weights are progressively driven toward zero. Meanwhile, the sharpness of the loss landscape increases rapidly, destabilizing the optimization dynamics and resulting in abrupt loss spikes. This perspective provides a rationale for why weight penalties can improve generalization yet cannot be made arbitrarily strong: excessive decay drives scale-invariant weight norms past a critical boundary and destabilizes training. Our work provides a new mechanistic understanding of loss spikes through the lens of \emph{weight-norm criticality}. Moreover, \emph{weight-norm criticality} yields testable predictions that we validate empirically in networks with scale-invariant components, providing empirical support for the proposed mechanism.

</details>


### [245] [Regularized Optimization on Grassmann Manifold: Theory, Algorithm and Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21039)
*Zhuan Liang,Zheng Zhai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为RPMA的正则化投影矩阵近似框架，用于在噪声、异常值和模型扰动下更稳健地估计低秩投影矩阵。通过在流形上优化并利用格拉斯曼流形的几何特性，该方法实现了更稳定、稀疏且可解释的投影估计，并设计了高效的黎曼梯度投影算法和避免重复特征分解的Cayley-SMW梯度方法。实验表明，RPMA在合成和真实数据集上均显著提升了投影矩阵恢复精度，优于传统谱投影方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统谱方法在噪声、异常值或模型扰动下性能严重下降，亟需一种更鲁棒的投影矩阵估计方法以提升社区检测、聚类和图学习的可靠性。

Method: 将投影矩阵估计建模为在秩-K 投影矩阵流形上的优化问题，利用其与格拉斯曼流形的几何等价性，推导一阶和二阶最优性条件，分析临界点景观稳定性；设计基于回溯线搜索的黎曼梯度投影算法和无需重复特征分解的Cayley-SMW梯度方法求解非凸优化问题。

Result: RPMA在各种噪声环境下显著提升了投影矩阵的恢复精度，在社区检测和聚类任务中表现优于传统谱方法，具有更高的鲁棒性、稀疏性和可解释性。

Conclusion: RPMA框架有效解决了谱方法在噪声环境下的脆弱性问题，为低秩投影矩阵估计提供了新的理论基础和高效算法支持，适用于实际复杂场景中的社区发现与聚类任务。

Abstract: Spectral methods are among the most widely used techniques for community detection, clustering, and graph learning. Their performance, however, critically depends on the accurate estimation of the underlying spectral subspace and can deteriorate substantially in the presence of noise, outliers, or model perturbations. To address this limitation, we propose a Regularized Projection Matrix Approximation (RPMA) framework for robust estimation of rank-$K$ projection matrices. RPMA extends classical spectral projection by incorporating a regularization term, producing projection estimates that are more robust, sparse, and interpretable. We formulate the proposed model as an optimization problem on the manifold of rank-$K$ projection matrices and exploit its geometric equivalence to the Grassmann manifold. Based on this manifold characterization, we derive the first- and second-order optimality conditions, establish the local stability of the regularized leading eigenspace, and characterize the stability of the critical-point landscape under sufficiently small regularization. To efficiently solve the resulting nonconvex optimization problem, we develop a Riemannian gradient projection algorithm with backtracking line search, together with a more efficient Cayley--Sherman--Morrison--Woodbury (Cayley--SMW) gradient method that avoids repeated eigendecompositions. Extensive experiments on both synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that RPMA substantially improves the recovery accuracy of projection matrices and consistently outperforms conventional spectral projection methods for community detection and clustering under noisy environments.

To address this issue, this study presents CounterFundus, a novel CycleGAN-driven counterfactual explainability framework, integrating EfficientNet-B5-based retinal disease detection with visually interpretable disease-to-normal fundus image translation. To this end, EigenCAM-aligned evaluation demonstrates that the generated counterfactual explanations remain spatially consistent with classifier-relevant retinal evidence across all CCAS dimensions. ### [247] [From Evaluation to Optimisation: Hierarchy-Aware Training Signals for CWE Prediction in Python](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21069)

Method: 比较三种方法：监督微调、双头分类损失、基于归一化惩罚的强化学习（GRPO），评估其在分布外场景下的表现。

Result: 监督方法在分布外表现劣于零样本基线，而GRPO方法显著降低累积ALPHA惩罚，最优策略在贪心和采样解码下分别减少27.9%和25.5%，达到与更大零样本模型相当的性能。

Abstract: The original ALPHA benchmark introduced a taxonomy-aware penalty for evaluating CWE-level vulnerability prediction in Python and proposed that the penalty could theoretically also serve as a training signal. This paper provides that validation. We compare three delivery mechanisms: supervised fine-tuning, a dual-head classification loss, and reinforcement learning with a dense reward derived from the normalised penalty. We find that supervised approaches consistently regress below the zero-shot baseline under distribution shift, while GRPO succeeds. Our best policy reduces the cumulative ALPHA penalty of Qwen2.5-Coder-7B on Security Hardening and Adversarial Testing (SVEN) dataset by 27.9% under greedy decoding, and by 25.5% under sampled decoding(p = 0.005, Welch's t-test), reaching statistical parity with its 4.5x larger zero-shot teacher. We conclude that the value of a hierarchical penalty as a training signal depends largely on the directness of its delivery.

### [248] [Spectral Transformation for Layer-wise Global Rank Discovery in Federated LoRA for Vision Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21074)
*Hariharan Ramesh,Jyotikrishna Dass*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出SpecTraL，一种用于联邦微调视觉变换器（ViT）中低秩适配器（LoRA）的新型聚合方法。该方法通过在低秩潜在空间中进行正交Householder变换，直接对客户端的局部LoRA模块堆叠进行处理，避免了密集权重重建和辅助模型训练，显著降低服务器开销。利用随机矩阵理论中的尖峰协方差模型，SpecTraL可自动发现每层最优全局秩，无需人工调参。同时引入感知填充的初始化框架，使客户端可在不重新合并到预训练模型的前提下扩展残差适配维度，缓解收敛不稳定问题。实验表明，SpecTraL在准确率-通信效率权衡上优于现有方法，且减少了服务器计算量与超参数搜索成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有联邦学习中基于低秩适配器（LoRA）的方法存在聚合策略的根本缺陷：独立平均LoRA因子导致数学不一致与交叉项误差；而保留异构秩的拼接策略则大幅增加下载成本，并需在客户端合并全局更新，引发重初始化延迟和收敛不稳定；其他方法通过重建密集权重或训练辅助模型进一步提升服务器开销。因此亟需一种统一、高效、无需调参的聚合机制。

Method: SpecTraL采用分层谱变换策略：首先将各客户端的局部LoRA模块堆叠成一个高维低秩矩阵；随后在低秩潜在空间中执行正交Householder变换，实现无损压缩与噪声分离；基于随机矩阵理论中的尖峰协方差模型，自动识别出反映全局共识的信号成分，从而确定每层最优全局秩；为保持与本地秩一致，设计了一种感知填充的初始化机制，允许客户端在不重新合并至基模型的情况下引入新增的适配维度。

Result: 在DomainNet与NICO++数据集上对ViT-B/16和ViT-L/16进行联邦微调实验显示，SpecTraL在相同通信代价下取得更高准确率，显著降低服务器端计算负载，消除对秩选择的超参数调优需求，且避免了因频繁合并带来的收敛波动。

Conclusion: SpecTraL通过谱分析与正交变换实现了高效、自适应的联邦LoRA聚合，在精度、通信效率与系统开销之间取得良好平衡，为大规模视觉模型的分布式微调提供了新范式。

Abstract: Fine-tuning Vision Transformers (ViTs) with low-rank adapters (LoRA) promises better communication efficiency under federated setup, yet existing aggregation strategies face fundamental limitations. Independently averaging these LoRA factors is mathematically inconsistent, introducing cross-term aggregation error. In contrast, approaches that preserve heterogeneous client ranks by concatenating local adapters on the server substantially increase download cost and often require merging global LoRA updates into pretrained weights on the clients, causing reinitialization lag and unstable convergence. Other approaches further increase server-side overhead by reconstructing dense weight updates or training auxiliary models to refine aggregation error. In this work, we propose SpecTraL, spectral transformation for layer-wise global rank discovery, that resolves these challenges within a unified design. SpecTraL stacks local LoRA modules from clients and performs orthonormal Householder Transformation of the stacked adapters directly in the low-rank latent space, eliminating dense reconstruction of the global update and any auxiliary refinement on the server. By leveraging the Spiked Covariance Model from Random Matrix Theory, SpecTraL analytically separates the global consensus signal from non-IID noise, discovering optimal layer-wise global ranks without manual hyperparameter tuning. To match local ranks in subsequent rounds, we introduce a padding-aware initialization framework that lets clients incorporate residual LoRA dimensions without re-merging them into the pre-trained base model. Experiments on federated fine-tuning of ViT-B/16 and ViT-L/16 over DomainNet and NICO++ demonstrate improved accuracy-communication trade-offs, reduced server computation, and elimination of hyperparameter search for rank selection. Our code is available at https://github.com/DASS-Lab-Group/SpecTraL

</details>


### [249] [Nipping the Butterfly Effect in the Bud: Self-Output Fine-Tuning for Autoregressive Weather Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21080)
*Yun-Ye Cai,Hsuan-Tien Lin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了长时序天气预测中自回归深度学习天气预测（DLWP）的误差增长问题。理论与实证分析表明，误差增长源于输出误差与输入分布偏移之间的反馈循环，导致初始小误差被放大并逐步破坏后续输入分布，类似于大气科学中的蝴蝶效应。该分布偏移早在推理的第一步就已显现。为此，作者提出一种即插即用的策略——自输出微调（SOFT），利用模型自身的一步预测来校准第一步的偏差输入分布。实验表明，尽管方法简单，SOFT在长时序预测任务上达到领先性能，显著降低预测误差和分布差异，揭示了重新审视深度学习天气预测基础流程的重要性，是大气科学领域的重要进展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归深度学习天气预测（DLWP）虽具可扩展性和灵活性，但其预测误差随预报时间延长而快速累积，影响长期预测精度。现有方法未能有效解决这一核心问题，因此亟需从理论与实践角度深入理解误差增长机制，并提出有效缓解策略。

Method: 通过理论分析与实证研究揭示误差增长的根源——输出误差与输入分布偏移间的反馈循环；提出自输出微调（SOFT）策略，利用模型自身的一步预测结果对初始输入分布进行校准，以缓解分布偏移问题。

Result: SOFT在多个长时序天气预测基准上实现最先进的性能，显著降低预测误差与输入分布偏差，验证了其有效性与普适性。

Conclusion: 误差增长主要由自回归过程中的反馈循环驱动，且分布偏移始于推理初期。通过引入自输出微调（SOFT），可有效缓解该问题，为深度学习天气预测提供了关键的流程改进，具有重要科学意义。

Abstract: Long-horizon weather forecasting is a fundamental challenge in atmospheric science, for which autoregressive Deep Learning Weather Prediction (DLWP) has emerged as the primary paradigm. Although the autoregressive pipeline is highly scalable and flexible, its prediction errors grow rapidly over long forecasting horizons. In this work, we study this error growth phenomenon from both theoretical and empirical perspectives. Our analysis reveals that the growth is driven by a feedback loop between output errors and input distribution shifts. Specifically, the autoregressive process amplifies small initial output errors, which progressively corrupt subsequent input distributions, echoing the butterfly effect in atmospheric science and ultimately deteriorating forecasting accuracy over longer horizons. Furthermore, we show that this distributional shift originates at the earliest stage of inference, with out-of-distribution signatures detectable as early as the first autoregressive step. To mitigate this issue, we propose \textbf{Self-Output Fine-Tuning (SOFT)}, a plug-and-play strategy that leverages the model's own one-step predictions to calibrate the biased input distribution encountered at the first step. Extensive experiments demonstrate that, despite its simplicity, SOFT achieves state-of-the-art performance on long-horizon forecasting tasks and substantially reduces both prediction errors and distributional discrepancy. The success of SOFT highlights the importance of reexamining the fundamental pipeline of deep learning weather prediction, representing a critical pipeline advance for atmospheric science.

To address these limitations, we propose a novel Causal Adversarial Subspace Clustering (CASC) framework for discovering evolving latent regimes in high-dimensional spatiotemporal data. CASC integrates a U-Net-inspired deep adversarial clustering architecture with stacked FAConvLSTM layers to preserve spatial and temporal structure while learning robust latent representations. A graph attention transformer-based self-expressive network is introduced to jointly model local spatial relationships, global dependencies, and long-range temporal interactions. Furthermore, we propose two new learning objectives: (1) a Causal Subspace Preservation Loss that aligns self-expression coefficients with latent causal relationships, encouraging clusters to reflect underlying causal processes rather than simple feature similarity, and (2) a Dynamic Temporal Subspace Evolution Loss that captures evolving subspace structures and temporal regime transitions in nonstationary environments. Together, these components transform deep subspace clustering from a correlation-driven paradigm into a causal-temporal regime discovery framework.

### [251] [Training Large Language Models for Self-Explanation Faithfulness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21090)
*Yeoktatt Cheah,María Pérez-Ortiz,Noah Y. Siegel,Oana-Maria Camburu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种强化学习（RL）方法，直接优化大语言模型自解释的可信度（faithfulness），即模型生成的推理过程是否真实反映其内部决策机制。现有方法多聚焦于评估可信度或使用推理时提示框架提升可解释性，但无法直接优化模型参数以生成更可信的自解释。本文将可信度度量转化为强化学习的奖励函数，通过随机词插入和用户偏见插入两种干预方式，训练Llama3.1-8B和Qwen3-8B模型，在Phi-CCT指标上实现显著提升（分布内最高达0.664，分布外最高达0.691）。尽管跨干预泛化能力较弱，但部分模型表现出非零迁移效果，显示出模型与设置依赖的复杂行为。最后分析排除了奖励操纵等潜在问题，证明模型能隐式识别关键影响因素并披露，为提升大模型推理可信度提供了一条可扩展路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法无法直接优化模型参数以生成可信的自解释，缺乏对模型内部决策过程真实反映的训练机制，亟需一种可直接优化可信度的训练范式。

Method: 将现有的可信度度量（如Phi-CCT）转化为强化学习的奖励信号，采用随机词插入和用户偏见插入作为干预手段，构建每样本奖励，并基于此对Llama3.1-8B和Qwen3-8B进行微调训练。

Result: RL微调后的模型在Phi-CCT可信度指标上表现显著提升，分布内得分可达0.664，分布外任务（如StrategyQA）达0.691；部分模型展现出跨干预类型的非零泛化能力，且经分析排除了奖励操纵行为，表明模型具备识别并披露关键决策因素的能力。

Conclusion: 通过强化学习直接优化自解释的可信度是可行的，模型能够隐式识别影响决策的关键因素并主动披露，为解决大语言模型中不忠实推理问题提供了有效、可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: We propose a Reinforcement Learning (RL) method to directly optimize the faithfulness of self-explanations - the extent to which a model's generated reasoning accurately reflects its internal decision-making process. While existing work focuses on evaluating faithfulness or using inference-time prompting frameworks to improve an LLM's self-explanation's tractability, these approaches do not provide a mechanism to directly optimize a model's parameters to generate faithful self-explanations. We bridge this gap by modifying existing faithfulness metrics into an RL training objective. We investigate (1) if models can be trained to accurately detect factors that affect their decisions, and (2) whether RL can directly optimize for the disclosure of these factors thereby improving LLM self-explanations' faithfulness. We experiment with two intervention types: random-word insertions and user-bias insertions, using a per-sample reward derived from the Phi-CCT correlation metric. RL fine-tuned Llama3.1-8B and Qwen3-8B show substantial improvements on the Phi-CCT faithfulness metric, with in-distribution scores rising from near-zero to as high as 0.664, and out-of-distribution scores reaching up to 0.691 on held-out tasks such as StrategyQA. Cross-intervention generalization is weaker but more interesting: a priori we would not expect a model trained only on random word insertions to generalize to user-bias phrases, yet Llama3.1-8B shows non-zero transfer in this direction. The reverse direction and Qwen3-8B do not replicate this, indicating model-dependent and setup-dependent effects we cannot yet explain. Lastly we analyze model behavior to rule out reward gaming behaviors that often plague RL training. Ultimately, we show that models can be trained to implicitly identify influential factors and disclose them, offering a scalable path toward reducing unfaithful reasoning in LLMs.

</details>


### [252] [A Polynomial Architecture-Attribution Co-Design Framework for Exact Aumann-Shapley Attribution in GNNs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21094)
*Bizu Feng,Zhimu Yang,Shuming Wang,Shaode Yu,Yuan Cheng,Xiaojun Qian,Zixin Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出APEX框架，通过设计PolyGIN模型使图神经网络的Aumann-Shapley归因积分可精确计算。PolyGIN保持了标量输出的多项式形式，使得路径积分可通过高斯-勒让德求积法在有限点上精确求解，显著降低计算开销并提升归因保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于路径积分的归因方法（如Integrated Gradients）在深度GNN中依赖数值近似，存在精度与计算成本之间的权衡问题。为实现精确归因，亟需一种既能保持模型性能又支持解析归因计算的模型架构。

Method: 提出PolyGIN：一种保留多项式结构的GIN类图网络，其消息传递、归一化和变换操作共同维持输出为有界多元多项式；利用该性质，证明归因路径导数的次数上限为$2^L-1$，从而可用$2^{L-1}$个确定性点通过高斯-勒让德求积精确计算Aumann-Shapley积分。

Result: 实验表明，PolyGIN在合成及真实世界图数据集上具有与基线相当的预测性能；APEX框架在归因保真度上优于对比方法，且所需函数评估次数大幅减少。

Conclusion: 通过模型与归因的协同设计，APEX实现了图神经网络中特征级与节点级归因的精确计算，在保证模型性能的同时显著提升了归因效率与可靠性。

Abstract: We study feature-level and node-level explanations for graph neural networks (GNNs) through the lens of Aumann-Shapley attribution. Path-integral methods such as Integrated Gradients provide an axiomatic formulation of attribution, but their practical use in deep GNNs typically relies on finite-sample numerical approximations to the path integral, requiring a trade-off between quadrature error and computational cost. This paper proposes APEX, a model-attribution co-design framework that makes the attribution integral exactly computable under a polynomial GNN architecture. The key component is PolyGIN, a GIN-style graph network whose message-passing, normalization, and transformation operations preserve a bounded multivariate polynomial form for scalar model scores, such as pre-softmax logits. We show that, for a PolyGIN with $L$ polynomial transformation blocks, the derivative along the attribution path has degree at most $2^L-1$. Therefore, Gauss--Legendre quadrature can evaluate the Aumann--Shapley path integral exactly, up to floating-point precision, with $2^{L-1}$ deterministic evaluation points. The resulting attributions can be computed at the feature level and then aggregated into node-level scores while preserving completeness. Experiments on synthetic and real-world graph benchmarks show that PolyGIN maintains competitive predictive performance, while the complete APEX framework achieves higher attribution fidelity than the compared baselines and substantially reduces the number of evaluations required for path integration.

</details>


### [253] [Smooth Neural Point Processes via B-Splines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21098)
*Michele Bellomo,Riccardo Ramaschi,Alberto Dolara,Tomaso Aste*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新型神经时间点过程（Neural TPP）模型，直接将条件强度函数（CIF）参数化为B样条基函数的非负组合，其系数由神经网络预测。该方法实现精确的负对数似然（NLL）计算，无需数值积分，保留了神经网络架构的完全灵活性，支持训练时的高效并行化，并通过积分平方二阶导数自然实现CIF平滑正则化。实验表明，该方法在合成与真实数据集上均优于基准神经TPP模型，在计算效率和预测准确性方面均有提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经TPP方法虽能精确计算负对数似然（NLL），但通常建模补偿器而非直接建模条件强度函数（CIF），受限于神经网络结构，且训练时事件贡献需串行计算，导致效率低下。因此亟需一种既能精确计算、又具高灵活性与高效性的新方法。

Method: 提出直接以B样条基函数的非负线性组合来参数化CIF，利用神经网络预测各基函数系数；通过解析方式精确计算NLL，避免数值积分；借助B样条特性实现平滑正则化；支持并行化训练，提升计算效率。

Result: 在合成与真实世界数据集上的实验结果表明，所提方法在预测准确性和训练效率方面均显著优于现有基准神经TPP模型，且具有更强的模型灵活性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于B样条的神经TPP模型，实现了精确、高效、灵活的条件强度函数建模，为时间点过程的建模提供了一种更优的解决方案。

Abstract: Temporal point processes (TPPs) provide a general and flexible framework for modeling sequences of events in continuous time. Neural networks have been successfully employed to model TPPs in a highly expressive and data-driven way. Neural TPPs are typically trained via Maximum Likelihood Estimation (MLE) by minimizing the negative log-likelihood (NLL), which depends on both the conditional intensity function (CIF) and its integral over time, the compensator. Recent neural TPP approaches enable exact evaluation of the NLL without numerical integration. However, these methods typically model the compensator rather than the CIF directly, impose constraints on the neural network architecture, and are computationally expensive during training, as event contributions to the NLL are evaluated sequentially rather than in parallel. In this work, we propose a novel neural TPP model that directly parametrizes the CIF as a non-negative combination of B-spline basis functions, whose coefficients are predicted by a neural network. This formulation enables exact evaluation of the NLL, preserves full flexibility in the neural architecture, allows efficient parallelization during training, and naturally supports CIF smoothness regularization through the integrated squared second derivative. Experiments on both synthetic and real-world datasets show improved computational efficiency and predictive accuracy compared to the reference neural TPP baseline.

### [254] [TOUR: A Trajectory-Level Unlearning Benchmark for Offline Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21111)
*Chaofan Pan,Lingfei Ren,Xiangyu Jiang,Yanhua Li,Xuemei Cao,Xiangkun Wang,Hao Yu,Wei Wei,Xin Yang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: TOUR基准包含轨迹级划分、匹配的非成员控制组、重训练参考模型、保留性能锚点，并结合多种攻击方式（如参考模型、阈值、偏差、等价性、动作误差、表示基础、查询受限攻击）进行隐私审计。

Result: 实验显示，重训练和微调通常比均匀GA+Refit提供更好的保留效用参考；TrajDeleter虽有用但并非始终最优；单一似然分数会高估删除效果，且删除有效性结论不稳定，受多种因素影响。

Abstract: Offline Reinforcement Learning (RL) agents are trained on fixed behavioral trajectories, which makes trajectory-level deletion important when selected data must be removed after training. Evaluating such deletion is difficult because a lower membership score can reflect trajectory removal, residual memorization visible to another attack, or policy collapse that destroys useful behavior. We introduce Trajectory-level memOrization and Unlearning in offline RL (TOUR), a benchmark that combines trajectory-level partitioning, matched non-member controls, retraining references, retained-performance anchors, and multi-attack privacy auditing. Across D4RL locomotion experiments and an exploratory AntMaze extension, TOUR shows that common deletion baselines have environment-dependent privacy-utility behavior. Retraining and fine-tuning often provide stronger retained-utility references than uniform GA+Refit, while TrajDeleter remains a useful comparator but is not uniformly stronger under the same audit. Reference-model, threshold, deviation, equivalence, action-error, representation-based, and query-limited attacks further show that a single likelihood-based membership score can overstate deletion quality. In the evaluated settings, conclusions about offline RL unlearning are therefore not stable under single-score auditing. ### [256] [Relative Value Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21120)
*Marc Höftmann,Jan Robine,Stefan Harmeling*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出相对价值学习（RV）框架，通过反对称函数直接学习状态间的价值差，引入配对贝尔曼算子并证明其为γ-收缩映射，具有唯一不动点等于真实价值差；推导出1步、n步和λ回报目标，并从配对差异重构广义优势估计（R-GAE），获得无偏策略梯度估计器。在PPO中集成RV后，在Atari基准（49个ALE游戏）上表现与标准PPO相当，表明相对价值估计是绝对批评者的一种有效替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强化学习中，通常使用价值函数 $V(s)$ 估计状态的绝对好坏，但实际控制中只有价值差才是关键信息。因此，作者提出直接学习价值差的相对价值学习（RV）框架，以更有效地利用相关性信息。

Method: 提出一个反对称函数 $Δ(s_i, s_j) = V(s_i) - V(s_j)$ 来直接建模状态间的相对价值差；设计配对贝尔曼算子，证明其为γ-收缩映射且有唯一不动点；基于此构建1步、n步和λ回报的目标函数；进一步从相对差中重构广义优势估计（R-GAE），用于无偏策略梯度估计；将该框架集成到PPO算法中进行实验验证。

Result: 在49个Atari ALE游戏中，基于相对价值学习的PPO版本取得了与标准PPO相当的性能，验证了相对价值估计的有效性和可行性。

Conclusion: 相对价值学习是一种有效的替代传统绝对价值估计的方法，能够通过直接建模价值差提升学习效率，并在复杂环境中保持竞争力。

Abstract: In reinforcement learning, critics typically estimate absolute state values $V(s)$, estimating how good a particular situation is in isolation. However, it turns out that only differences in value are relevant for control. Motivated by this, we propose Relative Value Learning (RV), a framework that learns value differences directly via an antisymmetric function $Δ(s_i, s_j) = V(s_i) - V(s_j)$. We introduce a pairwise Bellman operator and prove it is a $γ$-contraction with a unique fixed point equal to the true value differences, derive well-posed $1$-step, $n$-step and $λ$-return targets and reconstruct generalized advantage estimation from pairwise differences to obtain an unbiased policy-gradient estimator (R-GAE). Beyond theoretical results, we integrate RV with PPO and achieve competitive performance on the Atari benchmark (49 ALE games) compared to standard PPO, indicating that relative value estimation is an effective alternative to absolute critics.

</details>

### [258] [Agree on the Model, Verify the Inference: GKR Protocols for HND-Based Transformer Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21162)

Conclusion: GKR-HND协议成功实现了对HND模型推理的高效、安全验证，在保持计算优势的同时防止了模型替换和不完整执行问题。

The retained verifier checks the GKR transcript and registered-weight openings, but delegates expensive public evaluations to an assigned computation worker. Assuming an honest retained verifier and prover--worker non-collusion, the verifier accepts only when the worker's signed, request-bound response agrees with the proof claims. Experiments with pretrained HND models validate the proof path and the delegated public computation without dense-matrix replay.
