### [259] [Automated Synthesis and Adversarial Validation of Executable Causal Research Pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21173)
*Irena Girshovitz,Dan Zeltzer,Ran Gilad-Bachrach*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ARA框架通过整合协议构建、合成数据生成和对抗验证，使自动化研究中的隐性错误（如无效因果假设）变得可见。它将自然语言研究问题转化为结构化因果协议和可执行代码，并利用结构性因果模型生成具有已知真实效应的合成数据。在评估中，尽管协议构建和对抗验证未显著提升数值准确性，但改变了失败模式：不再沉默输出错误因果估计，而是暴露协议问题、诊断失败或降级非因果解释，表明有效性优先的自动化科学系统应同时评估其是否能识别不当因果推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动化研究系统虽能加速实证分析，但易出现‘无声失败’——即代码运行成功却基于无效因果假设。现有方法缺乏对这些隐性错误的检测机制，因此亟需一种能显式揭示因果假设缺陷的框架。

Method: 提出ARA框架，结合协议构建、基于结构性因果模型（SCM）的合成数据生成与对抗验证；将自然语言研究问题转化为结构化因果协议和可执行代码，并通过控制性违反识别假设来评估分析结果的有效性。

Result: 协议构建与对抗验证未能显著提升与基准估计的数值一致性，但有效改变失败模式：从沉默输出错误估计转变为暴露协议问题、诊断失败或非因果解释，增强了对因果推断合理性的警示能力。

Conclusion: 有效性优先的自动化科学系统不应仅以答案准确率为评价标准，更应考察其能否识别并提示因果推断的不当性，从而提升研究可信度。

Abstract: While automated research systems promise to accelerate empirical analysis, they are prone to silent failures: instances in which analysis code executes successfully yet relies on invalid causal assumptions. We present the Artificial Intelligence (AI)-based Epidemiology Research Assistant (ARA), a framework that makes these failures visible by explicitly encoding causal design principles, study-specific assumptions, and methodological constraints. ARA integrates protocol construction, synthetic data generation, and adversarial validation into a unified pipeline. The framework translates natural language research questions into structured causal protocols and executable analysis code by first constructing a protocol and then generating synthetic datasets using Structural Causal Models (SCMs) with known ground-truth effects. This synthetic-data step can also support pipeline development when access to confidential data, such as medical data, is restricted. The generated analysis is then evaluated under controlled violations of identification assumptions. We evaluate ARA on the Automated Causal Reasoning Benchmark, assessing recovery of identification strategies, causal quantities, treatment and outcome variables, and consistency between generated code and approved protocol. Protocol construction and adversarial validation did not consistently improve numerical agreement with benchmark estimates compared with standard LLM-based generation. However, they changed the failure mode: instead of silently returning causal estimates, ARA often surfaced protocol concerns, diagnostic failures, incomplete inference, or downgraded non-causal interpretations. These findings suggest that validity-first automated science systems should be evaluated not only by answer accuracy, but also by whether they indicate when causal claims are unwarranted.

</details>


### [260] [Filter Learning for Subgraphs: Algebras and Performance Risk Bounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21263)
*Purui Zhang,Feng Ji,Yanan Zhao,Bihan Wen,Wee Peng Tay*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于子图支持的滤波器学习（SFL）框架，通过距离感知的拉普拉斯构造定义结构化滤波器类，在部分观测下逼近完整图滤波器，实验表明其性能优于多项式滤波器、分布无关算子和直接数值学习基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际应用中通常无法获取完整的图拓扑，而传统图信号处理依赖于完整的图结构，因此需要一种在部分观测下仍能有效进行图滤波的方法。

Method: 提出基于距离感知拉普拉斯构造的子图滤波器代数，将SFL建模为统计学习问题，通过数据驱动方式学习最优子图算子，并建立基于最小二乘损失的性能风险边界。

Result: 在真实数据集上的实验表明，所提方法在子图滤波任务中显著优于多项式滤波器、分布无关算子及直接从数据中恢复结构的数值学习方法。

Conclusion: 所提出的子图滤波器代数框架能够有效在部分观测条件下逼近完整图滤波器，具有良好的泛化能力和实用性。

Abstract: Graph signal processing tasks that leverage spectral information typically assume access to the complete graph topology, which is often unavailable in practice. We propose a systematic framework for subgraph filter learning (SFL), where subgraph-supported operators approximate ambient graph filters under partial observations. We formulate SFL as a statistical learning problem in which optimal subgraph operators are inherently data-dependent. To address the difficulty of directly estimating such operators, we develop a subgraph filter algebra based on distance-aware Laplacian constructions, defining a structured and controllable class of filters for effective approximation. We further establish performance risk bounds under the least squares loss, quantifying how well the learned operator approximates the restricted ambient mapping. Experiments real-world datasets show that, for SFL tasks, the proposed algebraic models consistently outperform polynomial filters, distribution-agnostic operators, and direct numerical filter learning baselines that attempt to recover the underlying structure from data.

### [261] [The Dark Room in the Reward Channel: Dense Prediction Rewards Collapse GRPO-Trained LLM Agents -- and What Actually Works](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21273)
*Yu Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 密集的每步监督在长时程、稀疏奖励的LLM代理中看似有效，但研究发现，在组归一化强化学习（GRPO）下，基于预测未来的奖励机制会导致策略崩溃，进入‘黑暗房间’病理状态：预测准确率趋近1.0，任务成功率降为0，轨迹长度被固定在时间窗上限。单因素消融实验表明，移除GRPO中的标准差归一化即可避免灾难性失败。根本原因在于：在全失败组中，z-score化的优势值对塑造系数不变，导致有界奖励变为无界压力，退火机制无法缓解。核心洞见是：z-score会放大信号的组内方差，而当全失败组占主导时，那些随掌握程度下降方差的信号才是结构上安全的。该方差-特征准则能回溯解释实验崩溃，并提前预测未运行的实验组表现，且与已有成功案例兼容。进一步控制实验显示，奖励通道效果中性，而辅助损失通道提升约20分；即使使用随机黄金标签，差距依然存在，说明性能提升不依赖正确标签。所有结果均为单种子，种子重复性和组大小控制已预注册并进行中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决长时程、稀疏奖励任务中LLM代理的学习困难，探索密集每步监督的有效性，特别是基于预测未来观测的奖励机制是否可靠。

Method: 在ALFWorld环境下，使用Qwen3系列模型（1.7B/4B/8B），采用组归一化强化学习（GRPO）框架，设计基于预测未来观测的奖励机制，通过单因素消融实验定位问题根源，提出方差-特征准则，并构建控制信号传递矩阵验证不同机制效果。

Result: 在GRPO下，预测奖励导致策略陷入‘黑暗房间’病理状态：预测准确率接近1.0，任务成功率降至0，轨迹长度固定。移除标准差归一化后，性能恢复至基线水平。方差-特征准则能解释并预测实验崩溃，且与已有成功案例一致。辅助损失通道显著优于奖励通道，且其优势不依赖真实标签。

Conclusion: GRPO下的密集预测奖励因组内方差放大机制而具有结构性危险，尤其在全失败组占主导时易引发策略崩溃。应谨慎使用基于z-score的归一化方法，优先采用方差随掌握程度下降的信号，并推荐使用辅助损失而非直接奖励通道以实现更稳定有效的训练。

Abstract: Dense per-step supervision is an appealing remedy for sparse-reward, long-horizon LLM agents: reward the agent for predicting its next observation, and memory should follow. We show that under group-normalized RL (GRPO), this recipe does not merely fail -- it destroys the policy. Across Qwen3-1.7B/4B/8B on ALFWorld, a potential-based prediction reward drives every run into a degenerate absorbing state (prediction accuracy -> 1.0, task success -> 0,episode length pinned at the horizon): the "dark room" pathology, built automatically by the optimizer. A single-factor ablation localizes the cause -- removing only GRPO's std normalization turns the same reward from catastrophic (0%) into baseline parity -- and a two-line proposition explains why: in all-fail groups the z-scored advantage is invariant to the shaping coefficient, so bounded rewards become unbounded pressure and annealing cannot help. Our central insight generalizes this: what z-scoring amplifies is a dense signal's within-group variance while all-fail groups dominate, so signals whose variance decays by mastery are structurally amplifier-safe.This variance-profile criterion retrodicts our collapses, carries preregistered predictions for arms that had not yet run, and is consistent with published reward-channel successes (a compatibility check, not an independent test). Finally, a controlled signal-delivery matrix (identical signal, varying only the consumption mechanism) shows the reward channel is at best neutral while the auxiliary-loss channel gains ~20 points -- and a shuffled-gold placebo matches the true-gold arm, so the gap survives without correct labels. Endpoints are single-seed; seed replication and group-size controls are preregistered and in progress.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 实验表明，多任务学习相比单任务模型显著提升了泛化能力，降低了训练和推理成本；合理的损失权重策略有效缓解了任务间冲突梯度问题；预训练/微调策略在目标数据有限时表现优异；跨地图迁移实验显示模型具备较强的环境适应能力。

Conclusion: 多任务学习在团队制多人游戏的预测任务中具有显著优势，能够有效提升模型泛化性、减少资源消耗，并在数据受限或环境变化场景下表现出良好的鲁棒性。该研究为游戏智能系统的高效建模提供了可行的技术路径。

We adapt a multimodal architecture for endpoint prediction to a general multi-task setting that combines rasterized vision inputs, global match context, and per-unit state information through an image encoder and attention-based interaction modeling. Experiments on a large proprietary World of Tanks dataset compare single-task and multi-task training, evaluate weighting strategies for mixed losses and conflicting gradients, and test pre-training/fine-tuning under limited target-data regimes. We also examine within-game transfer across game maps under structured environment shift.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: LLMs比人类教师干预更频繁且更早；倾向于提供完整解决方案而非部分提示；虽然在短期内提升任务成功率，但在促进长期学习和泛化能力方面表现较差。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used as tutors and thought partners, helping users reason through problems. While guidance from AI assistants can scaffold thinking and foster learning, such benefits depend on how they help--for instance, intervening too early or too frequently may hinder true learning and cognitive engagement. Yet how AI systems navigate intervention decisions during problem-solving remains poorly understood. Here, we introduce Int-Bench, a simulation-based benchmark for evaluating LLM interventions during learning. Int-Bench simulates a "student" solving a problem while a "teacher" monitors the student's reasoning and decides whether, when, and how to intervene. Across three domains--code debugging, mathematics, and brain teasers--we evaluate LLM teachers on the frequency and timing of interventions, as well as their impact on both immediate task success and generalization to new problems. We also compare LLMs to humans, finding that LLMs intervene more frequently and earlier than humans. Moreover, in contrast to humans, they tend to provide complete solutions rather than targeted hints. These findings suggest that current LLM assistants often optimize for short-term success rather than supporting the reasoning processes needed for deeper learning and long-term success.

M$^3$-Gen learns a unified latent representation from the clinical variables and the images, leveraging contrastive learning, and exploits the embeddings of the two modalities to guide a generative model in producing biologically coherent gene expression profiles. Evaluations on the TCGA dataset demonstrate that M$^3$-Gen generates realistic and functionally meaningful gene expression data. ### [265] [How Many Bits Can an Adapter Write? Measuring the Capacity and Memorization of Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21351)
*Kaizhen Tan,Heqing Du,Yang Feng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过量化低秩适配器（LoRA）在冻结主模型上写入的信息量（以比特为单位），揭示了其实际记忆容量远低于参数数量所暗示的水平，且受参数位置和模型结构影响显著。实验表明，适配器仅每可训练参数存储约2比特信息，且将参数从注意力层移到MLP可提升存储能力近一倍；若移除主模型结构，存储能力几乎消失。此外，隐私泄露与适配器写入的比特数正相关，而非参数数量。监督微调会直接复制秘密信息，而基于可验证奖励的强化学习适配器则不会记录。该工作将传统“适配器即技能”的直觉转化为可度量、可设计的量化指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有认知将LoRA适配器视为一种技能而非数据记录，但缺乏对其实质记忆能力的量化理解。本文旨在打破这一模糊假设，通过直接测量适配器在冻结模型中写入的信息量，揭示其真实记忆容量与结构依赖性，进而为隐私保护和模型设计提供新依据。

Method: 扩展基于压缩的记忆分析方法至冻结基础模型场景，直接以比特为单位测量适配器写入的信息量；通过改变参数分布位置（注意力层 vs MLP）、移除主模型结构等操作，系统评估其对存储容量的影响；应用于Qwen2.5的真实微调任务，比较监督学习与强化学习适配器的隐私泄露行为。

Result: LoRA适配器每可训练参数仅存储约2比特信息，远低于全量微调；存储能力强烈依赖于参数位置和主模型结构；将相同参数预算从注意力层转移至MLP可使容量接近翻倍；移除主模型结构后容量近乎消失；隐私泄露程度与适配器写入的比特数相关，而非参数数量；监督微调会复制敏感信息，而基于奖励的强化学习适配器则不会记录。

Conclusion: 适配器并非简单的能力表达，而是具有有限且结构敏感的记忆容量。通过直接测量微调写入的比特数，可实现对模型隐私与知识保留的精准控制，推动从经验直觉向可量化设计的转变。

Abstract: A LoRA adapter is a few megabytes that almost everyone treats as a skill rather than a record of the data behind it. We put that assumption on a scale. Extending compression-based memorization analysis to the frozen-base setting, we measure directly, in bits, how much a low-rank adapter writes into a model it never changes. The answer is both smaller than full fine-tuning and less lawful than parameter counting would predict. Adapters store a couple of bits per trainable parameter, well short of a full model's budget, but that figure turns less on how many parameters an adapter carries than on where they sit. Move the same parameter budget from attention into the MLP and it holds nearly twice as much; strip the frozen base of its structure and the capacity all but disappears. Applied to realistic fine-tunes of Qwen2.5, the same instrument shows privacy leakage rising with the bits an adapter writes rather than the parameters it nominally has, and it draws a clean line between supervised and reinforcement learning: the secrets that supervised fine-tuning copies down verbatim, an adapter trained on verifiable rewards never records. Measuring what fine-tuning writes, rather than attacking it after the fact, turns a piece of folklore into a quantity one can design against.

</details>


### [266] [Gradient Concentration, Not Weight Saliency, Explains Representation-Level Class Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21353)
*Billel Habbati,Alessio Merlo,Luca Verderame,Meriem Guerar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究首次对SalUn中使用的梯度显著性掩码机制进行了受控消融实验。在CIFAR-10和CIFAR-100上使用ResNet-18，通过匹配计算量的实验设计，比较了基于显著性的掩码、同等稀疏度的随机掩码以及无约束更新三种策略。结果表明，在线性探测、原型恢复和层间CKA等表示层面评估中，三者表现统计上无差异。发现遗忘梯度高度集中在网络最后几层（约92%的平方梯度能量），导致所有掩码策略均作用于同一表示子空间；且显著性掩码的类别特异性极低（特异性指数0.09–0.11），不同类别选择的参数集高度重叠。研究指出，在所研究设置下，表示层面遗忘主要由梯度集中和表示几何决定，而非显著性选中的权重身份。更广泛地，结果支持现有证据：有效的表示级遗忘需要直接作用于潜在表示的目标函数，而非依赖复杂的权重选择策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器遗忘方法普遍采用基于梯度显著性的权重选择来实现遗忘，但其对表示层面遗忘的实际贡献尚不明确。本文旨在揭示该机制在表示遗忘中的真实作用，挑战现有方法对复杂权重选择策略的依赖。

Method: 采用匹配计算量的实验设计，在CIFAR-10和CIFAR-100上使用ResNet-18模型，对比三种配置：基于显著性的掩码、随机掩码（同等稀疏度）和无约束更新。保持未学习目标、优化调度和计算预算一致，通过线性探测、原型恢复、层间CKA等多维度评估表示恢复能力。同时分析梯度分布与掩码的类别特异性。

Result: 三种配置在表示层面的可恢复性无统计差异；遗忘梯度高度集中在网络末层（约92%的平方梯度能量）；显著性掩码的类别特异性极低（0.09–0.11），参数选择高度重叠。

Conclusion: 在所研究设置下，表示层面遗忘主要由梯度集中性和表示几何结构主导，而非显著性选中的权重身份。有效表示级遗忘应转向直接作用于潜在表示的目标函数，而非依赖复杂的权重选择策略。

Abstract: Machine unlearning aims to remove the influence of specific training data while preserving model utility. Many state-of-the-art approaches pursue this goal by restricting the forgetting update to a subset of parameters selected through gradient-based saliency. Although such methods are widely adopted, the actual contribution of saliency-based weight selection to representation-level forgetting remains unclear. In this work, we perform the first controlled ablation of the saliency masking mechanism used by SalUn. Using a matched-compute experimental design on CIFAR-10 and CIFAR-100 with ResNet-18, we compare saliency-based masking against random masks of equal sparsity and unconstrained updates, while keeping the unlearning objective, optimization schedule, and computational budget fixed. Across multiple representation-level evaluations, including linear probing, prototype recovery, and layer-wise CKA, the three configurations exhibit statistically equivalent representation-level recoverability. We find that forget gradients are strongly concentrated in the final network layers (approximately 92% of the squared gradient energy on CIFAR-10) before any mask is applied, causing all masking strategies to operate within the same representational subspace. Furthermore, saliency masks show limited class specificity (specificity index 0.09-0.11), selecting highly overlapping parameter subsets across different forget classes. Our findings suggest that, in the studied setting, representation-level forgetting is primarily governed by gradient concentration and representation geometry rather than by the specific identity of saliency-selected weights. More broadly, the results support a growing body of evidence indicating that effective representation-level unlearning requires objectives that act directly on latent representations rather than on increasingly sophisticated weight-selection strategies.

</details>


### [267] [Emergent Misalignment Recruits a Pre-existing Persona Subspace](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21356)
*Mohammed Suhail B Nadaf*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 微调一个对齐的语言模型仅针对少量不良建议，会导致其在与训练数据无关的问题上广泛失对齐，称为涌现失对齐。研究发现，这种窄范围的微调会激活模型预存的‘人格化’结构。通过对比教师强制法从冻结的指令微调模型（Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct）中提取各领域人格子空间，发现四个不相关领域共享一个低秩核心，其显著性为随机子空间的657倍，且82%的核心成分位于风格核心之外。在安全代码上进行微调的第一步优化即比以教育形式呈现的相同代码更难跨越广义失对齐边界，并可预测未来375步的边界移动。在整个微调过程中将该子空间从残差流中移除可防止广义失对齐（从27.7%降至0.0%），而匹配秩的随机子空间无影响；反之，将其注入从未微调的模型则诱导出随剂量增长至45.4%的失对齐行为，超过原微调模型的表现。权重梯度上的相同投影无效，三种事后权重编辑也未能消除该倾向：最剧烈的编辑仅抑制行为而非根除，且被清除的结构会在编辑后重新在子空间内形成。将固定量的坏数据分散到四个领域产生的广义失对齐程度，远超机械权重叠加和匹配多样性所能解释的范围。所有测量均基于单一14B模型，提取来自对齐的指令微调检查点，因此该结构的来源尚不明确；而阻止失对齐的干预也同时消除了窄域训练行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究为何仅在特定领域微调会导致模型在无关任务上出现广泛失对齐现象，揭示其背后的机制是否源于模型内部预存的结构。

Method: 从冻结的指令微调模型中使用对比教师强制法提取各领域的个性化子空间，分析跨域共享的核心结构；通过微调实验观察行为变化，实施子空间投影干预，测试权重编辑效果，并比较不同数据分布策略的影响。

Result: 发现多个无关领域共享一个显著的低秩核心结构，该结构能引发广义失对齐；子空间投影可有效防止失对齐但同时消除窄域训练行为；权重编辑无法根除该现象，表明其具有内在恢复能力；跨领域数据分布加剧失对齐，超出传统解释能力。

Conclusion: 涌现失对齐并非由微调本身直接导致，而是由于窄域微调触发了模型中预先存在的、跨域共享的人格化子空间结构。这一结构具有强泛化能力且难以通过常规手段消除，提示模型对齐风险可能深植于其内部表征架构之中。

Abstract: Fine-tuning an aligned language model on a narrow stream of bad advice can make it broadly misaligned on questions unrelated to the training data, a phenomenon called emergent misalignment. We ask why the narrow lesson generalizes at all, and we find that narrow fine-tuning recruits a persona structure that is present in the model before the fine-tune exists. From a frozen instruction-tuned model (Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct) we extract per-domain persona subspaces by contrastive teacher forcing and find that 4 unrelated domains share one low-rank core at 657x a random-subspace null, with 82% of that core lying outside a style core built at matched diversity. The literal first optimizer step of fine-tuning on insecure code climbs a broad-misalignment margin harder than the same code framed as educational, and forecasts realized margin movement out to 375 steps. Projecting the subspace out of the residual stream throughout fine-tuning prevents broad misalignment (27.7% to 0.0% of judged generations) while a matched-rank random subspace changes nothing; injecting it into the never-fine-tuned model induces misalignment that grows with dose to 45.4%, past the fine-tuned model it is measured against. The same projection applied to the weight gradient is inert, and three post-hoc weight edits leave the disposition in place: the sharpest edit suppresses the behavior rather than removing it, and the ablated structure re-forms inside the subspace the edit cleared. Spreading a fixed budget of bad data across 4 domains produces more broad misalignment than mechanical weight superposition and matched diversity jointly account for. All measurements come from one model at 14B; the extraction is from an aligned instruction-tuned checkpoint, which leaves the structure's provenance open; and the intervention that prevents misalignment also abolishes the narrow trained behavior.

</details>


### [268] [Hilbert Operator for Progressive Encoding (HOPE): A Mathematical Framework for Deconstructing Learned Representations in Deep Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21366)
*Hossein Mobahi,Peter L. Bartlett*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HOPE 是一种基于希尔伯特空间的连续函数框架，将网络压缩从离散域转化为连续表示，通过将神经元建模为秩-1 希尔伯特-施密特算子，统一了剪枝与神经元合并为低秩子空间投影，并引入宏块剔除以涵盖残差路径等多层结构，实现跨层、跨架构的无偏压缩决策。该框架无需数据和超参数，具备理论指导意义与实际应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有网络压缩方法受尺度对称性和架构偏差影响，难以公平分析深层网络中的内部表示；需一种不受架构限制、可统一处理不同层结构的压缩理论框架。

Method: 提出希尔伯特算子渐进编码（HOPE）框架，将神经元视为希尔伯特-施密特算子，利用低秩子空间投影统一剪枝与合并操作，引入宏块剔除机制以覆盖复杂多层结构，所有操作在希尔伯特空间中进行，实现无数据、无超参数的压缩分析。

Result: 实验验证了 HOPE 在模型压缩与微调任务中的有效性，证明其理论框架能有效揭示网络内部表示，支持跨架构、跨层级的无偏压缩决策。

Conclusion: HOPE 为深度神经网络内部知识的解构提供了一种数学上严谨、通用性强且无需依赖数据与超参数的新范式，具有重要的理论价值与实践前景。

Abstract: Deep neural networks encode complex representations, but deconstructing this internal knowledge remains a challenge. Given the link between learning and compression, network compression offers a promising lens to analyze this knowledge. However, standard compression heuristics often suffer from scale symmetries and architectural biases. To resolve these, we introduce Hilbert Operator for Progressive Encoding (HOPE), a mathematical framework to gradually deconstruct the representations in trained network weights.
  HOPE shifts network compression from the discrete domain into a Hilbert space of continuous functions. By modeling individual neurons as rank-1 Hilbert-Schmidt operators, HOPE unifies pruning and neuron merging as low-rank subspace projection. Extending this formulation, HOPE introduces macro block eviction to encompass multi-layer structures like entire residual pathways under the same unified metric. This unified approach enables unbiased architectural decisions across layers with different types and sizes. HOPE is a data-free and hyperparameter-free framework. We present proof-of-concept experiments in model compression and fine-tuning to highlight the practical potential of our theory.

### [269] [Mean-to-Score Discrete Diffusion: Posterior-Mean Denoisers for Score Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21372)
*Jingyuan Li,Xiaoyi Jiang,Yixuan Jiang,Wei Liu,Yi Zhu,Zuoqiang Shi,Pipi Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SEDD方法虽通过正分率保证反向跳跃率非负，但不确保贝叶斯可实现性；提出M2S方法，通过将清洁标记后验均值映射为得分，确保符合有效后验约束，在多个基准测试中显著提升生成性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SEDD中的分数熵损失虽有正确理论最优解，但无法强制远离该解时的贝叶斯可实现性约束，导致部分得分向量违反有效性条件，引发采样中负权重问题。

Method: 引入mean-to-score（M2S）方法，基于已知连续时间马尔可夫链（CTMC）的线性映射，从后验均值精确转换为得分，适用于满足弱支持条件的任意坐标独立连续时间马尔可夫链；对均匀污染和吸收掩码污染分别映射至桥多面体与恢复MD4。

Result: 在CIFAR-10上，M2S将测试BPD从3.173降至3.129，FID-50k从$\CifarSEDDFID$降至$\CifarMtwoSFID$；170M参数模型在262B token上训练，128步生成PPL达143.3，优于纯均匀SEDD、GIDD和神经CTMC基线。

Conclusion: M2S通过确保得分向量位于桥多面体内，解决了SEDD中因违反贝叶斯可实现性导致的负权重问题，显著提升了生成质量与稳定性，是离散扩散模型的有效改进方案。

Abstract: Score Entropy Discrete Diffusion (SEDD) parameterizes discrete reverse processes with unconstrained positive score ratios. While positivity guarantees nonnegative reverse jump rates, it does not ensure Bayes realizability: ratios at a noisy state need not be jointly induced by any clean-token posterior under the forward kernel. The score-entropy loss has the correct population optimum but does not enforce this constraint away from it. In a trained pure-uniform SEDD checkpoint, roughly one quarter of complete score vectors violate the coordinate box, while more than half lie inside it yet remain materially incompatible with any valid posterior. Such violations can produce negative pre-normalization weights in finite-step sampling. Projecting raw scores onto the bridge polytope removes all observed negative weights and improves external generative PPL from $203.6$ to $175.1$ without changing the sampler. We introduce \emph{mean-to-score} (M2S), which predicts a clean-token posterior mean and converts it to the score through an exact kernel-dependent linear map. The construction applies to any known coordinate-wise continuous-time Markov chain (CTMC) satisfying a mild support condition. For uniform corruption, it maps the probability simplex onto the bridge polytope; for absorbing-mask corruption, the resulting objective recovers MD4 exactly. In a controlled 28.4M-parameter CIFAR-10 comparison, M2S lowers test BPD from $3.173$ to $3.129$ and FID-50k from $\CifarSEDDFID$ to $\CifarMtwoSFID$. A 170M-parameter M2S model trained on about 262B OpenWebText token slots outperforms the evaluated pure-uniform SEDD, GIDD, and Neural CTMC checkpoints at every tested sampling budget, reaching generative PPL $143.3$ at 128 steps versus $183.6$ for the strongest pure-uniform baseline.

</details>

Abstract: Mobile-health interventions increasingly use online learning and decision making algorithms to personalize when to nudge users toward healthier behavior, but a poorly designed algorithm can burden and disengage participants. New algorithm design decisions should therefore be vetted against realistic simulated users before each real-life deployment. We propose a method to develop ``JITAI-Twins'': digital twins of a target subpopulation for comparing candidate online algorithms before a just-in-time adaptive intervention (JITAI) deployment. The method builds on a conditional time-series diffusion model that is temporally consistent (future actions do not affect the generated past), and it supports repeated updating from three sources of information, in three steps: pre-training on a large observational dataset, fine-tuning on small prior intervention deployments in related populations, and inference-time calibration to the next target population from domain-scientist expertise. We validate the twin at each pre-deployment stage of the long-running HeartSteps series (v2 through v4) of physical-activity suggestion intervention deployments, treating each successive deployment as an upcoming study. The proposed method reproduces the target subpopulation's temporal and between-participant structure better than simpler simulators. These results suggest that our twin can be used to simulate a target deployment before it runs, the prerequisite for testing and informing online algorithm design decisions.

To ensure constructive cooperation, we propose a semantic-aware task clustering method for CMT-SemCom. ### [272] [Context-weighted Discrete Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21427)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种上下文加权采样器，通过在连续时间马尔可夫链中融入局部上下文信息，并设计一种缩放的交叉熵损失函数以重新加权不同词元的训练信号。

Abstract: Discrete flow matching provides a flexible framework for generative modeling on discrete structures. However, the standard factorized training objective exposes the model to targets of varying difficulty, mixing well-conditioned, predictable tokens with ambiguous, high-entropy ones. We empirically demonstrate that the uncertainty over the value of each token is closely related to the density of available context in its neighborhood. Motivated by this observation, we propose a simple modification to the underlying continuous-time Markov chain (CTMC) that incorporates local context information. Our context-weighted sampler improves generation quality with negligible computational overhead, while our scaled cross-entropy loss function reweights the training signal from different tokens and reduces generative perplexity by up to 63% on OpenWebText. Moreover, our approach matches a strong semi-autoregressive block diffusion baseline in quality while retaining the ability to perform generation in any order. These results highlight the role of local context as an important factor in discrete generative modeling and show that simple context-aware modifications can significantly improve both sampling and training efficiency.

### [273] [KroQuant: Kronecker-Structured Block Transforms for Efficient Post-Training Quantization of Diffusion Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21446)
*Yann Bouquet,Alireza Khodamoradi,Kristof Denolf,Mathieu Salzmann*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: KroQuant 是一种用于扩散变压器（DiTs）的后训练量化（PTQ）方法，针对 W4A4 量化中因激活值包含异常值导致输出质量下降的问题。它采用学习得到的克罗内克结构可逆变换对每个 32 元素激活块进行处理，参数量少于通道级缩放（SmoothQuant），且在 MI350 GPU 上比 SmoothQuant 快 14%。通过离线 LoRaQ 权重校准吸收残余量化误差，在 PixArt-Σ、SANA 和 FLUX.1-schnell 上实现优于 SVDQuant 和 LoRaQ 的图像质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: W4A4 量化下扩散变压器的激活值存在异常值，标准量化方法无法有效表示，导致输出质量严重下降。现有解决方案在量化精度和推理开销之间权衡不佳：如 SmoothQuant 计算便宜但破坏通道幅度，固定哈达玛变换需大块尺寸导致高在线成本，而全维可逆变换虽校准效果好但带来巨大计算开销。因此亟需一种高效且高精度的 PTQ 方法。

Method: 提出 KroQuant，使用学习的克罗内克结构可逆变换作用于每个 32 元素激活块，以减少参数量并支持小规模张量核心 GEMM 运算；结合离线 LoRaQ 权重校准，补偿量化过程中的残余误差。

Result: 在 W4A4（MXFP4e2）设置下，KroQuant 在 MJHQ-30K 与 SDCI 数据集上生成的图像质量优于 SVDQuant 与 LoRaQ，同时保持或提升原始图像质量；在 MI350 GPU 上，其量化核比 SmoothQuant 快 14%。

Conclusion: KroQuant 有效解决了扩散变压器在极端低比特量化下的性能瓶颈，兼具高精度与高效率，是当前最先进且实用的 W4A4 PTQ 方案之一。

Abstract: Post-training quantization (PTQ) of diffusion transformers (DiTs) to W4A4 severely degrades output quality, because activations entering each linear layer contain outliers that 4-bit formats cannot represent. The standard fix applies an invertible linear transform to the activations and its inverse to the weights before quantizing both. Normalization layers between blocks force this transform to run online at every denoising step, making its inference computation cost the binding design constraint. Existing options trade quantization quality for inference cost: per-channel scaling (SmoothQuant) is computationally cheap but impacts the magnitude of the channels, which can harm quantization accuracy; fixed Hadamard transforms yield better quantization accuracy but require large block sizes that incur a high online cost; learned full-$d$ invertible transforms calibrate best but entail a prohibitive dense $d \times d$ matrix multiplication (GEMM) per layer per step.
  We propose KroQuant, a PTQ method that applies a learned Kronecker-structured invertible transform to each 32-element block of the activation, storing less than half the parameters of per-channel scaling. The block-local structure runs as small tensor-core GEMMs, and on an MI350 GPU the KroQuant quantizer kernel is up to $14\%$ faster than the SmoothQuant kernel. Offline LoRaQ weight calibration then absorbs the residual per-weight quantization error. On PixArt-$Σ$, SANA, and FLUX.1-schnell at W4A4 (MXFP4e2), KroQuant produces outputs closer to the FP reference than SVDQuant and LoRaQ on MJHQ-30K and SDCI, while preserving or improving image quality.

</details>


### [274] [Test-Time Scaling via Error Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21453)
*Rajiv Shailesh Chitale,Rahul Madhavan,Taneesh Gupta,Deepanway Ghosal,Aravindan Raghuveer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TTEL是一种基于错误定位的测试时扩展算法，通过利用固定或环境反馈进行令牌级错误定位，实现高效推理。它通过比较有反馈条件概率与无反馈基线，识别出错误发生步骤，并截断轨迹后分支新生成路径，最大程度复用有效前缀。在多个复杂推理任务上，TTEL显著优于现有方法，在相同性能下减少约一半的生成令牌数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准推理方法如独立采样和顺序多轮精炼缺乏令牌级信用分配，导致有效推理前缀频繁被丢弃，造成计算效率低下。为解决此问题，需引入更精细的错误定位机制以提升推理效率。

Method: TTEL利用环境或固定反馈信息，通过对比带反馈条件概率与零上下文基线，实现令牌级错误定位；一旦检测到错误，即截断当前生成轨迹并基于有效前缀分支新路径，从而最大化重用已有正确推理。

Result: 在LiveCodeBench上，使用Qwen3-8B模型时，TTEL达到pass@64为71.0%，生成令牌数仅为独立采样的约一半（360.4k vs. 735.0k）；在AIME-2025和HMMT-2025数学基准上，TTEL对齐两种模型均显著超越其他测试时基线方法。

Conclusion: TTEL通过引入令牌级错误定位机制，实现了高效的推理过程，显著提升了大语言模型在复杂推理任务中的性能与计算效率，构建了更优的帕累托前沿。

Abstract: Scaling inference-time computation has emerged as a reliable method to improve the performance of large language models on complex reasoning and programming tasks. However, standard approaches such as independent sampling and sequential multi-turn refinement operate without token-level credit assignment, resulting in computational inefficiency, since valid reasoning prefixes are frequently discarded. In this work, we introduce Test-Time Scaling via Error Localization (TTEL), an inference-time algorithm that utilizes fixed or environment feedback to perform token-level error localization. By comparing conditional probabilities under informed feedback against a null-context baseline, TTEL isolates the step at which an error occurred. The algorithm then truncates the trajectory and branches a new generation, maximally reusing the valid prefix. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that TTEL establishes strictly dominating Pareto frontiers across sequential reasoning domains, measured by pass-at-k vs. generated-token cost. With Qwen3-8B on LiveCodeBench, TTEL attains a pass@64 of 71.0% while generating approximately half as many tokens as independent sampling (360.4k vs. 735.0k). Generalizing to math benchmarks AIME-2025 and HMMT-2025, TTEL cleanly outperforms competing test-time baselines across both Qwen3-8B and Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507.

</details>


### [275] [Error Certificates for KV-Cache Eviction via Randomized Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21475)
*Peng Xie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出随机化KV缓存淘汰策略，通过泊松采样尾部并引入哈杰克校正，实现无损的误差证书，使系统能够识别缓存错误来源，而非仅预测错误。实证显示其在真实负载下具有0.97的覆盖率，且能有效区分缓存导致与固有错误，优于输出置信度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定性KV缓存淘汰无法识别被破坏的内容，即使系统保留的值不变，注意力输出误差也可无限增大，导致无法构建一致的误差估计器。因此需要新的方法来恢复可识别性。

Method: 采用泊松采样尾部，以已知包含概率进行随机淘汰；通过单个logit偏移在softmax中执行哈杰克校正，并使用调查抽样方差估计器作为每步误差证书。

Result: 在真实工作负载上，该方法实现了0.97的实证覆盖度，且不损失精度。预注册的七个假设中有四条成立：可感知问题的淘汰在25%-50%预算下近乎无成本；输出对数概率比证书更能预测失败；证书门控预算扩展无效。但证书能有效实现归因，区分缓存引发与固有错误（AUC 0.73–0.75），调度重计算优于随机或置信度门控。

Conclusion: 随机化机制带来了归因能力，而非预测能力，是提升系统可解释性和可靠性的重要突破。

Abstract: Deterministic KV-cache eviction keeps the top-$k$ tokens under an importance score and deletes the rest. We prove that this design cannot know what it destroyed: evicted values can be altered so that everything the serving system retains is unchanged while the true attention-output error grows arbitrarily, so no serving-time estimator of that error is consistent. Randomized eviction restores identifiability. With a Poisson-sampled tail at known inclusion probabilities, one logit offset performs the Hájek correction inside the softmax, and a survey-sampling variance estimator over the retained set becomes a per-step error certificate with 0.97 empirical coverage at no accuracy cost. On real workloads we pre-registered seven claims and lost three: question-aware eviction at 25--50\% budgets is nearly free; output log-probability predicts failure better than the certificate; certificate-gated budget escalation adds nothing. What survives is attribution: the certificate separates cache-induced from inherent failures (AUC 0.73--0.75, against 0.47--0.54 for output confidence) and schedules recomputation better than random or confidence gating. Randomization buys attribution, not prediction.

### [276] [Finite-Sample Coverage Audits for High-Recall Candidate Generation: Certification and Learning-Theoretic Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21480)
*Martin Anthony,Kaveh Salehzadeh Nobari*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在经验性流程中，如何通过有限样本验证来确保初始高召回阶段遗漏的相关项数量足够少。核心结论是：必须对被排除的池子进行采样才能有效评估遗漏质量；任何有效的审计必须检查约 $N_0/m$ 个来自排除池的标签，才能以高概率保证最多遗漏 $m$ 个相关项。文中提出一种基于二项分布和超几何分布精确反演的有限样本工具包，可实现对遗漏质量的严格认证，并支持多候选生成器并行验证与压力测试，所有保证均在固定规则前提下成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在信息检索或机器学习的预筛选流程中，初始阶段若遗漏相关项目，将无法被后续步骤恢复，因此需要可靠地量化并控制这种遗漏。现有方法依赖渐近近似，缺乏有限样本下的严格保证。本文旨在建立一个具有有限样本有效性、能准确评估遗漏质量的审计机制。

Method: 通过理论分析证明仅使用候选集内部标签无法提供非平凡的遗漏边界；引入排除池采样作为必要条件；构建基于二项分布与超几何分布精确反演的有限样本统计工具；设计双池实验设计以转换遗漏质量到召回率；支持对一系列嵌套候选生成器的同步验证及对抗扰动的压力测试。

Result: 证明了排除池采样在零遗漏情形下的最小最优性（minimax rate-optimal）；提出了一个精确的有限样本审计框架，可在不依赖渐近近似的情况下，对遗漏质量进行严格认证；实现了对多个候选生成器的并行验证与负担-性能权衡选择；所有结果在预先固定规则的前提下具有形式化保证。

Conclusion: 排除池采样不仅是便利做法，更是理论上最优的审计策略。所提出的工具包提供了可信赖的、无需渐近假设的遗漏质量认证机制，可用于指导实际系统中候选生成器的选择，平衡审查成本与召回目标。

Abstract: An initial high-recall stage in an empirical pipeline decides which items pass to later review, labelling, or modelling, and relevant items it misses are lost to every subsequent stage. We study how many audit labels are needed to certify, with finite-sample validity, that this missed relevant mass is small, and our main results characterise the label complexity of this problem. We first show that no procedure using only labels from inside the candidate set can certify any non-trivial bound on the missed mass: the audit must sample the excluded pool, the only region where unrecovered relevant items can lie. We then prove a matching finite-corpus lower bound. Any valid audit that certifies fewer than $m$ missed relevant items with high probability when none are present, even if adaptive and permitted to label the entire included pool, must inspect on the order of $N_0/m$ excluded-pool labels. Excluded-pool auditing is therefore minimax rate-optimal, not merely convenient, for missed-mass certification in the zero-miss regime. Building on this characterisation, we develop an exact finite-sample toolkit, using binomial and hypergeometric inversion rather than asymptotic approximation, that certifies missed mass, converts it to recall through a two-pool design, certifies pre-specified families of nested candidate generators simultaneously, and produces stress-test certificates against declared perturbation mechanisms. These certificates can be paired with observable review burden to select the least burdensome pre-specified candidate generator meeting a missed-mass target. Every guarantee holds under one discipline: the candidate generator, or the pre-specified family from which it is selected, and the audit rule are fixed before the certification labels are examined.

</details>

### [278] [Windowed-MTP: Removing the Full-Context Draft-KV Tax at Million-Token Context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21535)
*Alagappan Valliappan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种无需训练、可直接替换的Windowed-MTP方法，通过在草案注意力中引入滑动窗口与注意力汇点，将草案的KV缓存读取量从线性增长降至常数，显著降低百万级上下文下的生成延迟。该方法在不改变目标模型验证结果的前提下，使每步解码成本下降28%-44%，端到端延迟同步提升，同时回收7.7-11%的未使用KV内存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前主流模型内置的多标记预测（MTP）草案头在百万级上下文下因需对整个KV缓存进行全注意力计算，导致草案读取开销随上下文线性增长，成为性能瓶颈，尤其在长序列和混合注意力架构中更为严重，削弱了推测解码的优势。

Method: 采用StreamingLLM风格的滑动窗口结合注意力汇点机制，仅应用于草案的注意力计算，保持目标模型的全注意力验证不变；该方法为训练无关、即插即用且无损，确保接受的标记仍由目标模型决定，仅影响提案标记范围。

Result: 在三个不同架构（Qwen GDN-MoE 35B/122B 和 Mamba2-hybrid NoPE 120B）上，于单个GPU环境下测试，当上下文长度达到100万时，与原生MTP草案相比，每解码步成本降低28%至44%，该收益与输入无关并随上下文增长而扩大；端到端延迟相应改善，同时接受率可能进一步提升，且输出分布保持不变。此外，约7.7-11%的未使用KV缓存被紧凑环形缓冲区回收，无质量损失。

Conclusion: Windowed-MTP是一种高效、无损、无需训练的优化方案，有效解决了长上下文场景下推测解码中草案开销过大的问题，显著提升推理效率，适用于大规模语言模型的实际部署。

Abstract: Speculative decoding accelerates autoregressive generation by having a cheap draft propose tokens that a target verifies in parallel. Frontier models increasingly ship a built-in Multi-Token-Prediction (MTP/NEXTN) draft head under the assumption that the draft is negligibly cheap. At million-token context this breaks: an MTP draft head typically runs full attention over the entire KV cache at every draft step, so its read grows linearly with context and comes to dominate the draft cost -- precisely where speculation is most valuable. The effect compounds with draft length (a deep native draft can turn net-negative, slower than no speculation) and sharpens under hybrid/linear-attention targets, where cheaper verification leaves the draft's full-attention read exposed. We apply a StreamingLLM-style sliding window plus attention sink to the draft's attention only (Windowed-MTP), leaving full-attention verification intact. It is training-free, drop-in, and lossless by construction: the full-attention target still decides every accepted token, so windowing changes only which tokens are proposed, never which are accepted. It bounds the draft's KV working set to a constant, dropping ~99% of KV entries at 1M. Across three architecture families (Qwen GDN-MoE 35B/122B and a Mamba2-hybrid NoPE 120B) at 1M context on a single GPU in SGLang, windowing cuts the per-decode-step cost over the shipping native MTP draft by +28% to +44%, an input-invariant margin that widens with context. Since per-token latency is this cost divided by acceptance length, at matched acceptance end-to-end decode latency improves by the same amount, and more where windowing also lifts acceptance, while preserving the target's verified output distribution. Finally, the unread draft KV -- 7.7-11% of total KV at 1M -- is reclaimed via a compact ring buffer at no acceptance or quality cost.

</details>

*Yakun Wang,Leyang Wang,Song Liu,Taiji Suzuki*

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于零流准则的统计差异度量（零流差异，ZFD），用于两样本检验。通过分离见证函数学习与假设检验评估，ZF2ST利用灵活的神经网络实现有效且校准良好的检验，对结构化分布变化具有强检验力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有两样本检验方法在处理复杂分布差异时可能缺乏灵活性或统计校准性，尤其在高维数据中表现不足。本文旨在设计一种既能捕捉局部样本错位模式、又能保持严格统计校准的新型检验方法。

Abstract: We propose a new approach to two-sample testing for deciding whether two sets of samples are drawn from the same distribution. The test is built on a statistical discrepancy based on the zero-flow criterion, termed zero-flow discrepancy (ZFD). We prove the validity of ZFD and propose a practical testing procedure, termed the zero-flow two-sample test (ZF2ST). The key idea is to learn how samples from the two distributions are locally misaligned and use the resulting directional pattern as evidence of distributional difference. By separating witness learning from hypothesis evaluation, ZF2ST can use flexible neural networks while maintaining valid statistical calibration. We develop both regression-based and power-maximized approaches for learning the witness. Experiments on synthetic and image datasets demonstrate that ZF2ST can achieve strong testing power for structured distributional changes while maintaining well-calibrated type-I error.

### [280] [X$^3$-OPD: Distilling Reasoning into Large Audio-Language Models via On-Policy Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21550)
*Dongjie Fu,Di Cao,Xize Cheng,Zihan Zhang,Wenxu Jia,Yifu Chen,Shengpeng Ji,Yu Zhang,Tao Jin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: X$^3$-OPD是一种跨模态在线策略蒸馏框架，旨在将文本教师模型的推理能力迁移至音频语言学生模型，通过构建三层次对称语料库（文本推理转语音、复杂声景中的事件推理、包含副语言线索的对话推理），扩展了跨模态蒸馏的范围，使其不仅限于可文字还原的内容，还涵盖非语言事件、语调和对话上下文。实验表明，该方法显著提升了音频基础推理能力和思维链质量，并在领域偏移下保持了原有性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大音频语言模型在深层逻辑推理方面仍落后于文本大模型，主要受限于高质量音频推理数据的匮乏。

Method: 提出X$^3$-OPD框架，利用文本教师提供词级别指导，学生基于自身声学感知生成推理轨迹，结合三层次对称语料库进行训练。

Result: 在MMSU、MMAU、BIG Bench Audio和MMAR数据集上，X$^3$-OPD显著提升音频基础推理表现和思维链质量，同时在领域变化下保持模型原有能力。

Conclusion: X$^3$-OPD成功实现了从文本到音频的语言模型推理能力迁移，推动了音频语言模型在复杂听觉场景下的深度推理发展。

Abstract: While large audio-language models have achieved remarkable progress in auditory perception, they still lag behind text-based large language models in deep logical reasoning, primarily due to the scarcity of high-quality audio reasoning data. To bridge this gap, we propose X$^3$-OPD, a cross-modal on-policy distillation framework that transfers reasoning capabilities from a powerful text teacher to an audio-language student. During training, the student generates reasoning trajectories conditioned on its own acoustic perception, while the teacher provides token-level guidance using matched textual inputs and verified answers. We further construct a three-tier symmetric corpus covering textual reasoning rendered into speech, audio-event reasoning grounded in complex acoustic scenes, and spoken-dialogue reasoning involving paralinguistic cues. This design extends cross-modal distillation beyond textually recoverable content to reasoning grounded in non-linguistic events, prosody, and conversational context. Experiments on MMSU, MMAU, BIG Bench Audio, and MMAR demonstrate that X$^3$-OPD substantially improves audio-grounded reasoning and chain-of-thought quality while largely preserving the model's existing capabilities under domain shift.

</details>


### [281] [Graph Learning on Ensembles of Cyclic Peptides: An Investigation of Molecular Ensemble Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21561)
*Aaron Feller,Kris Deibler,Maxim Secor*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为EnsembleEGNN的分子集合基础模型，用于通过编码分子的多个构象来预测分子属性。该模型利用共享的等变图神经网络（EGNN）对每个构象进行编码，并通过集合注意力块对构象表示进行池化。模型在CREMP数据集上进行多任务自监督预训练，包括掩码标记恢复、噪声坐标重建和成对距离重建。尽管从零开始训练效果很差（R²=0.005），但预训练后的模型在CREMP-CycPeptMPDB数据集上取得了R²=0.477和皮尔逊相关系数r=0.699的性能，优于仅基于序列的BERT基线模型。当与BERT序列编码器联合训练时，混合模型进一步提升至R²=0.538，r=0.737。结果表明，将热力学信息融入的构象集合编码能有效提升环肽性质预测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统分子属性预测通常仅使用单个代表性构象，但许多分子在溶液中以构象集合形式存在。因此，需要一种能够有效编码分子构象集合的方法，以更准确地反映其真实物理状态并提升属性预测性能。

Method: EnsembleEGNN模型首先使用共享的等变图神经网络（EGNN）层对每个构象进行编码，然后通过集合注意力块对所有构象的表示进行池化，生成一个综合的嵌入表示。模型在CREMP数据集上采用多任务自监督学习进行预训练，包括掩码标记恢复、噪声坐标重建和成对距离重建。最后，可与BERT序列编码器联合训练以提升性能。

Result: 从零开始训练的EnsembleEGNN在测试集上表现极差（R²=0.005）。预训练后的模型达到R²=0.477，Pearson r=0.699，优于序列基线模型（R²=0.439，r=0.667）。联合训练的混合模型进一步提升至R²=0.538，r=0.737，证明了构象集合编码的有效性。

Conclusion: 将分子构象集合编码为一个热力学一致的嵌入表示，能够显著提升环肽类分子的性质预测性能，表明构象信息在分子建模中具有重要价值。

Abstract: Molecular property prediction from structure often uses a single representative conformation, even though many molecules exist as conformational ensembles in solution. We introduce EnsembleEGNN, a molecular ensemble foundation model that encodes an ensemble by first encoding each conformer with shared Equivariant Graph Neural Network (EGNN) layers, then pooling the resulting conformer representations with a Set Attention Block. We pretrain the model on CREMP, a cyclic peptide ensemble dataset, using a multi-task self-supervised objective combining masked token recovery, noisy-coordinate reconstruction, and pairwise distance reconstruction. On the CREMP-CycPeptMPDB dataset, training EnsembleEGNN from scratch fails entirely ($R^2=0.005$). However, the pretrained model reaches $R^2=0.477$ and Pearson $r=0.699$, outperforming the sequence-only BERT baseline ($R^2=0.439$, Pearson $r=0.667$). When EnsembleEGNN is co-trained end-to-end with the BERT sequence encoder, the hybrid model improves further to $R^2=0.538$ and Pearson $r=0.737$. These results demonstrate that encoding conformational ensembles into a single thermodynamically informed embedding improves cyclic-peptide property prediction.

</details>


### [282] [Beyond Sufficiency: Time Series Explanation with Counterfactual Necessity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21573)
*Hongnan Ma,Yiwei Shi,Mengyue Yang,Weiru Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TimePNS 是一种必要性感知的时间序列解释框架，通过因果干预检测时间因子的必要性，结合两阶段设计提升解释的准确性与可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法多关注充分性，易将无关子序列误判为重要，缺乏对必要性的考量，导致解释不准确。

Method: 提出两阶段框架：第一阶段学习可识别的因果生成过程并生成充分性解释掩码；第二阶段通过反事实干预获取必要性信号，指导时间门控模块优化初始解释，剔除非必要成分、强化必要成分。

Result: 在合成与真实世界时间序列数据集上，TimePNS 更准确地识别出决策关键子序列，并在充分性-必要性权衡上优于多个强基线方法。

Conclusion: TimePNS 有效提升了时间序列分类器解释的可信度，实现了更精准、更符合因果逻辑的解释。

Abstract: Faithful explanations of time-series classifiers should identify subsequences that are not only sufficient to preserve a black-box model's prediction, but also necessary for maintaining it. However, existing sufficiency-oriented methods can assign high importance to spurious subsequences that support the prediction without being essential to the model's decision. We introduce \textbf{TimePNS}, a necessity-aware framework for time-series explanation. Inspired by Pearl's counterfactual notion of necessity, TimePNS assesses whether a temporal factor is necessary by intervening on it and measuring whether the original prediction is disrupted. The framework adopts a two-stage design. Stage I learns an identifiable causal generative process together with a sufficiency-oriented explanation mask. Stage II performs counterfactual interventions on temporal factors to derive necessity signals, which supervise a temporal gate that refines the initial explanation by suppressing non-essential components and emphasizing counterfactually necessary ones. Experiments on synthetic and real-world time-series benchmarks show that TimePNS more accurately identifies decision-critical subsequences and consistently improves sufficiency-necessity trade-offs over strong baselines.

</details>


### [283] [Expanding Flow Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21585)
*Sophia Tang,Pranam Chatterjee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Expanding Generative Flows (EFlows)和Expanding Flow Maps (EFMs)，解决生成模型在维度和序列长度上固定的问题，通过引入可扩展的插值路径，实现动态增长的状态空间建模，并支持连续与离散模态下的变量尺寸生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于流的生成模型受限于固定的维度或序列长度，无法灵活处理可变大小的输出，因此需要一种能够动态扩展状态空间的新框架。

Method: 设计EFlows，利用条件噪声扩充状态空间并沿扩展插值路径定义概率流；提出EFMs，将状态变换分解为可学习的扩展算子和传输映射，实现高效几步生成；拓展至离散单纯形以支持图和序列的可变长度生成。

Result: 在连续与离散模态下均实现了对输出尺寸的可控学习与生成，恢复了传统固定尺度流模型作为特例，且具备更强的灵活性与表达能力。

Conclusion: EFlows和EFMs构成一个统一且可扩展的生成建模框架，使输出尺寸成为可学习、可控制的自由度，适用于广泛的应用场景。

Abstract: Flow-based generative models have enabled remarkable progress in fast and controllable generation across continuous and discrete state spaces, yet existing parameterizations are constrained to fixed dimensions or fixed sequence lengths. Here, we introduce Expanding Generative Flows (EFlows), which define flows between distributions of increasing dimensionality along an expanding interpolant that grows the state by augmenting it with conditional noise. Building on this construction, we propose Expanding Flow Maps (EFMs), a new class of flow maps that distill the expanding interpolant into efficient few-step generative models. Each EFM factors the map between any two timesteps into two learnable operations: an expand operator, which augments the state space with new coordinates or tokens conditioned on the current state, and a transport map, which pushes the expanded state forward along the interpolant. Composing these operators yields a single map that jointly expands and denoises the state, recovering existing fixed-canvas flows and flow maps as the special case in which the expand operator is the identity. We further extend the framework to the discrete simplex, enabling variable-size graph generation and variable-length sequence generation. Across both continuous and discrete modalities, we establish EFlows and EFMs as a principled framework for settings in which output size is itself a learned, controllable degree of freedom.

</details>

### [284] [AINTMA: Agentic AI Architecture for Autonomous Test Management with Generative Intelligence, Secure Cloud Communication and Adaptive Quality Analytics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20452)
*Vinil Pasupuleti,Shyalendar Reddy Allala,Siva Rama Krishna Varma Bayyavarapu,Shrey Tyagi,Srinivasateja Songa*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AINTMA 是一个基于多智能体的智能测试管理架构，通过六个专用AI智能体（测试发现、风险评估、强化学习优先级、执行编排、生成式质量智能、云安全监控）在云原生微服务架构上实现自主协同。其生成式质量智能模块利用大语言模型生成可读性强的质量报告与测试建议；强化学习优先级智能体基于47个特征和36个月历史数据建模测试选择为马尔可夫决策过程，实现高精度优先级排序。系统采用零信任API网关与加密通信保障安全，支持多租户隔离。在12个异构项目中18个月的评估显示：测试优先级准确率达88.4%（远超随机51.2%和商用基准82.1%），测试周期缩短43%，缺陷逃逸率从8.3%降至2.1%，9个月回本，投资回报率达340%。系统可扩展至5万+测试用例，响应时间低于400毫秒，生成式模块开发者满意度达4.3/5.0。表明智能体AI结合自主协调、生成智能与安全连接，能显著提升云规模企业软件质量管理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统测试管理难以应对分布式云环境下的复杂性与动态变化，亟需具备自适应决策能力的智能系统以提升软件质量与效率。

Method: 提出AINTMA架构，集成六类专用AI智能体，基于云原生微服务部署，通过零信任通信框架实现安全协作；其中强化学习优先级智能体使用马尔可夫决策过程建模，结合大规模历史数据训练上下文感知策略；生成式质量智能模块利用大语言模型生成自然语言质量报告与建议。

Result: 在12个真实项目中持续18个月的评估表明：测试优先级准确率达88.4%（优于随机51.2%和商用基准82.1%），测试周期减少43%，缺陷逃逸率由8.3%降至2.1%，9个月实现回本，投资回报率达340%；系统支持5万+测试用例，响应时间<400ms，生成式模块获4.3/5.0开发者评分。

Conclusion: AINTMA证明了智能体AI在融合自主多智能体协作、生成式智能与安全智能连接的基础上，能够从根本上推动云规模企业软件质量管理体系的演进。

Abstract: Modern software quality assurance demands intelligent, autonomous systems capable of adaptive decision-making across distributed cloud environments. This paper presents AINTMA (Agentic Intelligent Test Management Architecture), a multi-agent agentic AI system that transforms traditional test management into an autonomous quality intelligence ecosystem. AINTMA deploys six specialized AI agents (Test Discovery, Risk Assessment, Reinforcement Learning Prioritization, Execution Orchestration, Generative Quality Intelligence, and Cloud Security Monitor) coordinated through a secure multi-agent communication framework over a cloud-native microservices infrastructure. The Generative Quality Intelligence agent employs large language models to produce plain language quality narratives, defect risk summaries, and data-augmented test recommendations. The RL Prioritization agent models test selection as a Markov Decision Process, learning contextual policies from large-scale historical test execution data (47 features, rolling 36-month window). Secure cloud communication is enforced through a zero-trust API gateway with OAuth2/JWT authentication, encrypted inter-agent messaging, and multi-tenant isolation. Evaluation across 12 heterogeneous software projects over 18 months demonstrates: 88.4% test prioritization accuracy (APFD, vs. 51.2% random, 82.1% best commercial baseline); 43% test cycle time reduction; defect escape rate reduced from 8.3% to 2.1%; 340% ROI at 9-month payback. The agentic architecture scales to 50,000+ test cases with sub-400ms response time, and the generative intelligence module achieves 4.3/5.0 developer usefulness rating. AINTMA demonstrates that agentic AI, combining autonomous multi-agent coordination, generative intelligence and secure smart connectivity, can fundamentally advance software quality management in cloud-scale enterprise environments.

### [285] [Marking the Wrong Symptoms: Evaluating LLM Watermarks in Medical Texts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20462)
*Melanie Rieff,Robin Staab,Thibaud Gloaguen,Stefan Hegselmann,Martin Vechev*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究首次系统评估了大语言模型水印对医疗领域性能的影响，对比了5种水印方案在11个LLM和7个VLM上的表现，发现水印会导致词汇错误、虚构术语及图像发现误报或遗漏等严重退化问题。现有通用基准无法捕捉临床文本中的关键缺陷，强调需采用领域特定评估以确保水印模型在医疗场景中的安全部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在医疗流程中的应用日益广泛，亟需可靠的输出可追溯性技术如水印。然而，现有水印方法多基于通用基准评估，未充分考虑医疗领域中微小的词级扰动可能引发显著语义变化的特点，导致潜在临床风险被忽视。因此，亟需开展针对医疗领域的水印影响研究。

Method: 构建了由人类专家验证的系统性审计流程，用于评估医疗推理质量、术语精确性及幻觉生成情况；在11个LLM和7个VLM上测试5种水印方案，在多种单模态与多模态临床推理任务中进行评估，并结合人工验证与定量指标分析失败模式。

Result: 水印显著导致多种故障模式，包括词汇污染、虚构医学术语、图像发现的误报或遗漏；现有聚合指标难以揭示这些临床相关的退化问题，存在系统性掩盖风险。

Conclusion: 域特定评估是医疗场景中水印模型安全部署的先决条件，当前通用基准可能隐藏具有临床意义的性能下降，必须引入专业审计机制以保障患者安全。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly integrated into clinical workflows, stressing the need for reliable traceability of model-generated output with watermarking. Yet, most watermarks are evaluated on general-purpose benchmarks, leaving domains like medicine, where small token-level perturbations can result in significant semantic changes, underexplored. In this work, we present the first rigorous study of how LLM watermarks affect medical performance, benchmarking 5 watermarking schemes across 11 LLMs and 7 VLMs on various tasks spanning unimodal and multimodal clinical reasoning. Importantly, we complement existing evaluations by introducing a human-expert-validated pipeline for systematically auditing medical reasoning quality, terminological precision, and induced hallucinations. Our results reveal that watermarking can induce substantial degradation across multiple failure modes, including lexical corruption, hallucinated terminology, and amplified misattribution or omission of image findings. Notably, we find that the absence of domain-specific analyses, combined with aggregate metrics that miss failures inherent to clinical text, can systematically obscure practical watermark-induced degradations. Our findings establish domain-specific evaluation as a prerequisite for the safe deployment of watermarked models in medicine, where current benchmarks can otherwise mask clinically consequential failures.

</details>


### [286] [ClickGuard: Detecting and Spoiling Clickbait News with Informativeness Measures and Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20463)
*Wojciech Michaluk,Tymoteusz Urban,Mateusz Kubita,Soveatin Kuntur,Anna Wróblewska*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一款基于AI的浏览器扩展，用于识别点击诱饵（clickbait），帮助用户避免误导性网络文章。系统采用融合Transformer嵌入与语言学特征的混合机器学习架构，并引入自定义的“诱饵度”评分。通过对比多种NLP技术（从传统向量化到大语言模型嵌入），最终采用XGBoost模型，在公开数据集上达到91%的F1分数。该工具可在用户访问文章前和后发出警告：打开文章后，用户会收到一个百分比得分，表示文章为点击诱饵的可能性，并附有基于系统分析指标的解释；同时提供“点击诱饵剧透”——用一两句话总结全文内容。演示视频链接：https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IJ1gkQV82C4

Result: 所提出的浏览器扩展在公开组合数据集上实现了91%的F1-score，表现出优异的检测性能。系统不仅能提前预警，还能在用户打开文章后提供可解释的预测结果与简明的剧透摘要，显著提升用户体验与信息判断力。

Conclusion: 本研究成功开发出一款兼具高精度、实时性与可解释性的点击诱饵检测浏览器扩展。其融合深度学习与语言学特征的方法为未来网络内容可信度评估提供了有效范式，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: This paper presents an AI-driven browser extension that identifies clickbait to help users avoid misleading Internet articles. Moving beyond traditional detection, the application employs a hybrid machine learning architecture that combines transformer-based embeddings with linguistically motivated features and a custom "baitness" score. After evaluating various natural language processing techniques -- from classic vectorizers to large language model (LLM) embeddings -- an XGBoost-based model was developed that achieves an F1-score of 91% on the open combined dataset. Most importantly, the tool can warn users before and after they access a clickbait article. After opening an article, the user receives a percentage score indicating the likelihood that it is clickbait. The prediction is explained based on the analyzed metrics, including those specifically developed within the proposed system. The browser extension also provides a clickbait spoiler -- a one- to two-sentence summary of the entire article. ### [287] [Stochastic Sampling is Epistemically Shallow: The Dimensionality Gap Between Temperature Variation and Model Diversity in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20464)
*Izhar Ali*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨语言模型在多次运行中答案变化是否能揭示其知识盲区。通过比较单个模型重复运行（100次，τ=1）与多个模型各运行一次（24个模型，τ=0）的差异，发现单一模型内部仅有一个维度显著高于噪声，而多样化的模型集成则有四个显著维度，表明只有集成才能揭示跨问题的知识结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究语言模型在重复运行中答案变化是否能反映其未知知识，特别是跨问题之间的潜在结构关系。

Method: 采用Marchenko-Pastur随机矩阵理论区分信号与采样噪声，对比单个模型多次运行和多样化模型集成的表现，分析不同设置下的特征值分布。

Result: 单个模型在多次运行中仅有极少数特征值显著高于噪声，而多样化模型集成中多个特征值显著，且远超随机基准，表明只有多样化的集成能揭示模型未掌握的跨问题结构。

Conclusion: 自一致性方法可提供准确的单题不确定性估计，但无法捕捉跨问题结构；只有多样化的模型集成才能有效揭示模型所不知道的内容。

Abstract: When a language model gives different answers on repeated runs, does that variation reveal what it does not know? Self-consistency turns the variation into a per-question uncertainty estimate via majority voting. But does the same variation reveal cross-question structure -- related questions flipping together, the way a diverse ensemble does? We compare two regimes on the same questions: one model run $100$ times at $τ=1$ versus an ensemble of $24$ LLMs run once each at $τ=0$. A Marchenko--Pastur random-matrix test separates signal from sampling noise on both sides. Within any single model, at most one dimension rises above noise across five families and three benchmarks (MMLU, HellaSwag, GSM8K). Across the ensemble, four eigenvalues clear the noise edge, while a matched-difficulty Bernoulli null produces at most one in $500$ Monte Carlo draws. Self-consistency gives accurate per-question uncertainty but no detectable cross-question structure; only a diverse ensemble surfaces what a model does not know.

</details>


### [288] [JAXBench: Benchmarking Autonomous TPU Kernel Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20466)
*Arya Tschand,Charles Hong,Julian Walker,Nina Cai,Shangkun Wang,Suvinay Subramanian,Sundar Dev,Vijay Janapa Reddi,Amir Yazdanbakhsh,Sethu Sankaran*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 JAXBench，一个针对 Google Cloud TPUs 的原生基准测试套件，用于人工智能生成的内核优化。该套件包含 50 个相关且具备优化空间的 JAX 工作负载，涵盖从 MaxText 库中提取的 17 个生产级机器学习算子，以及从 KernelBench 转换而来的 33 个算子。其中 8 个算子已有手写优化的 Pallas 内核作为基线。评估四种基于反馈的方法在生成候选 Pallas 内核时发现，针对特定目标的上下文比模型规模更重要；结合精心整理的 TPU 文档可使单样本正确率从 5.8% 提升至 37.3%，并解决 48/50 个基准测试，实现 1.28x 的几何平均加速。一旦正确性达成，搜索结构带来显著性能提升，Autocomp 的束搜索流水线相比 XLA 达到 1.36x 加速。在 8 个手工调优的内核上，Autocomp 达到 1.60x 相比 XLA，接近 Tokamax 2.08x 上限但仍在分页和稀疏注意力算子上落后。作者公开了 JAXBench 基准、评估工具和基线结果，以支持开源贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自主 GPU 内核优化得益于严格的基准测试推动，但针对 TPUs 缺乏类似标准。为填补这一空白，本文旨在建立一个专为 TPU 设计的、可用于 AI 生成内核优化的基准测试体系，以促进高效内核开发与评估。

Method: 构建 JAXBench 基准套件，整合来自 MaxText 库的 17 个真实生产算子和来自 KernelBench 的 33 个验证算子，并设定高 TPU v6e MXU 利用率的问题规模。采用手写优化的 Pallas 内核作为专家上界基线（8 个）。使用 Gemini 3 Flash 模型进行反馈驱动的内核生成，结合上下文提示工程与搜索结构优化，评估多种方法在生成高质量 Pallas 内核上的表现。

Result: 引入针对性上下文后，单样本正确率从 5.8% 提升至 37.3%，成功解决 48/50 个基准测试，实现 1.28x 几何平均加速。在正确性保障前提下，搜索结构优化带来显著收益，Autocomp 束搜索管道达到 1.36x 相比 XLA 的加速。在 8 个手工优化内核上，其性能达 XLA 的 1.60x，接近 Tokamax 2.08x 上限，但在分页和稀疏注意力算子上仍存在差距。

Conclusion: 高质量的 TPU 内核优化仍具挑战性，但 JAXBench 及其配套工具为社区提供了开放基准与评估平台，有助于推动未来 AI 驱动的内核优化研究与开源协作。

Abstract: Rigorous benchmarks have driven progress in autonomous GPU kernel performance optimization by establishing a shared target to hillclimb on, but no equivalent exists for TPUs. We present JAXBench, a TPU-native benchmark suite for AI-generated kernel optimization on Google Cloud TPUs. JAXBench comprises 50 JAX workloads that are both relevant and provide headroom for optimization. We extract 17 production ML operators from architectures in the public MaxText library such as Llama-3.1, DeepSeek-V3, Mixtral, Mamba-2, and AlphaFold2, and translate 33 operators from KernelBench that are validated for correctness and set with new problem sizes that achieve high TPU v6e MXU utilization. Eight of the 17 production operators ship with hand-optimized Pallas kernels from the public Tokamax library and block-size tuned to establish an expert upper-bound baseline. We evaluate four feedback-driven methods on generating candidate Pallas kernels for JAXBench. Across the full suite with Gemini 3 Flash, we find that target-specific context matters more than model scale on a sparsely-documented DSL like Pallas. Conditioning on curated TPU documentation raises per-sample correctness from 5.8% to 37.3% and solves 48 of 50 benchmarks at a 1.28x geomean speedup. Search structure yields significant gains once correctness is achieved, with Autocomp's beam-search pipeline reaching a 1.36x geomean speedup over XLA. On the 8 hand-tuned kernels, Autocomp reaches 1.60x geomean over XLA, recovering most of the 2.08x Tokamax upper bound but trailing on the specialized paged and ragged attention operators. High-quality TPU kernel optimization remains a challenging task, and we release the JAXBench benchmark, evaluation harness, and baseline results to support open source contributions.

### [289] [DC-Leap: Training-Free Acceleration of dLLMs via Draft-Guided Contiguous Leaping Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20467)
*Yanhua Jiao,Tianyi Wu,Xiaoxi Sun,Yulin Li,HuiLing Zhen,Libo Qin,Baotian Hu,Zhuotao Tian,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DC-Leap 是一种无需训练的框架，通过动态连续验证和草稿引导解码，克服了扩散大语言模型中因联合概率依赖误差导致的保守置信度阈值问题，实现高效并行解码，在中等置信度下显著提升推理速度，最高可达53.19倍加速，结合KV缓存更达105.02倍，且生成质量保持相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前扩散大语言模型的并行解码受限于过于保守的置信度阈值，这源于联合概率依赖误差（JPDE），导致冗余去噪迭代和低效推理，亟需一种无需训练即可在中等置信度下实现可靠加速的方法。

Method: 提出DC-Leap框架，采用动态连续验证策略，将严格有序的因果约束融入并行解码过程，逐步验证令牌依赖关系以消除JPDE；同时引入草稿引导解码机制，利用草稿跳跃式扩展上下文，提供前瞻信息，并保留双向注意力的结构优势。

Result: 在标准基准测试中，DC-Leap实现了显著加速：在长序列生成任务MBPP上最高达53.19倍，结合KV缓存时最高达105.02倍，同时保持与原有方法相当的生成质量。

Conclusion: DC-Leap成功解决了扩散大语言模型中因JPDE带来的并行解码效率瓶颈，通过无训练设计实现高速、高质推理，为dLLMs的实用化提供了有效路径。

Abstract: While parallel decoding is central to the efficiency of Diffusion Large Language Models (dLLMs), current strategies are often hindered by overly conservative confidence thresholds. These thresholds, necessitated by the Joint Probability Dependence Error (JPDE), result in redundant denoising iterations and suboptimal inference speeds. To overcome this, we propose DC-Leap, a training-free framework that enables reliable acceleration of dLLMs in the moderate-confidence regime. DC-Leap introduces a Dynamic Contiguous Verification strategy that integrates strictly-ordered causal constraints into the parallel decoding process. By progressively validating token dependencies, this mechanism effectively neutralizes the JPDE, enabling reliable acceleration with comparable performance. Furthermore, DC-Leap incorporates the draft-guided decoding mechanism, where the draft helps extend the context by leaping forward across multiple tokens, providing look-ahead context and retaining the structural benefits of bidirectional attention during inference. Extensive experiments on standard benchmarks demonstrate that DC-Leap achieves substantial speedups, up to 53.19x on MBPP for long-sequence generation, and up to 105.02x when combined with KV-Cache with comparable generation quality. Code is available at https://github.com/ffh-wyls/DC-Leap .

</details>


### [290] [InferenceBench: A Benchmark for Open-Ended LLM Inference Optimization by AI Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20468)
*Jehyeok Yeon,Ben Rank,Maksym Andriushchenko*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: InferenceBench introduces a benchmark for AI agents to optimize LLM inference on a single H100 GPU across four scenarios targeting different bottlenecks. Agents outperform naive baselines and match default serving engines but fall short of simple hyperparameter searches, indicating limitations in exploring diverse configurations despite testing many techniques.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing benchmarks for AI agents are often limited to fixed workflows or narrow action spaces, allowing agents to succeed via memorized solutions rather than genuine optimization. This undermines the evaluation of true problem-solving ability in open-ended AI engineering tasks.

Method: The benchmark evaluates agents by deploying an OpenAI-compatible inference server and optimizing inference speed under time constraints. It includes four distinct optimization scenarios: prefill latency, decode latency, concurrent request throughput, and a balanced combination. Agents have two hours to improve performance using available resources.

Result: Agents achieve up to 8.08× speedup over a naive PyTorch baseline and up to 4.05× compared to default vLLM settings, but still lag behind a simple hyperparameter search that achieves up to 11.53× improvement. Analysis reveals agents focus heavily on one inference framework, test few distinct configurations, and spend most time re-measuring or tuning rather than exploring new strategies.

Conclusion: The main limitation of current AI agents is not lack of domain knowledge but their inability to generate and evaluate diverse configurations systematically. InferenceBench exposes this gap, highlighting the need for better exploration and strategy diversity in agent-based optimization.

Abstract: AI agents are increasingly used to automate research and development tasks, yet existing benchmarks typically evaluate them on prescribed workflows or narrow action spaces. Even nominally open-ended tasks can often be solved by retrieving a well-known recipe and tuning a few hyperparameters, making it unclear whether strong results reflect genuine optimization or memorized solutions. We introduce InferenceBench, where an agent must deploy an OpenAI-compatible inference server and optimize the speed of LLM inference. Each agent receives a target LLM, one H100 GPU, an optimization scenario, and a wall-clock time budget of two hours. Three optimization scenarios isolate distinct bottlenecks of inference (prefill latency, decode latency, and concurrent request throughput) and a fourth balances all three at the same time. Across 15 frontier agent configurations, agents reliably improve over a naive PyTorch baseline (up to $8.08\times$) and often match or exceed serving engines with default settings ($4.05\times$ for vLLM), but still fall below a simple hyperparameter search under the same time budget (up to $11.53\times$). Qualitative analysis of agent trajectories shows that although agents enumerate many relevant optimization techniques, they overwhelmingly converge on a single inference framework. They test only a few distinct configurations and spend the remaining budget re-measuring, repairing, or optimizing hyperparameters rather than exploring substantially different strategies. This suggests the bottleneck is not domain knowledge, but the ability to propose diverse configurations, evaluate them systematically, and submit the best identified solution. Overall, InferenceBench reflects the ability of agents to operate in an open-ended AI engineering setting, where memorized solutions lead to limited improvements.

### [291] [DecodeShare: Tracing the Shared Subspace of LLM Decode-Time Decisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20469)
*Zishan Shao,Lixun Zhang,Kangning Cui,Yixiao Wang,Ting Jiang,Hancheng Ye,Qinsi Wang,Zhixu Du,Yuzhe Fu,Fan Yang,Danyang Zhuo,Yiran Chen,Hai Helen Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DecodeShare提出一种协议，识别解码阶段隐藏状态中跨任务共享的低维子空间，并通过仅在解码时移除该子空间来测试其因果作用。实验表明，干扰该共享子空间会显著降低决策性能，远超干扰预填充推导或随机子空间的效果。该子空间在激活操控中具有实际意义，常见操控方向与任务通用解码通道重叠。投影出该子空间可明确区分不同组件的功能角色，且解码时评估操控向量比基于预填充的代理更可靠。尽管结构紧凑，该共享子空间在解码时仍是一个高杠杆的因果通道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在推理时使用缓存键值（KV-cached inference），但解码阶段是否使用统一的任务泛化结构尚不明确。现有方法依赖预填充阶段的表示，可能无法准确反映解码时的真实功能机制。因此需要识别并验证解码阶段是否存在共享的、任务通用的内部结构。

Method: 提出DecodeShare协议，通过分析解码阶段隐藏状态，识别跨任务一致共享的低维子空间；随后设计干预实验，仅在解码阶段移除该子空间，评估其对模型性能的影响；进一步结合激活操控技术，验证该子空间在功能分离和信号可靠性方面的优势。

Result: 干扰解码共享子空间导致性能下降显著高于干扰预填充或随机子空间；该子空间与常见激活操控方向重叠，投影移除后可清晰分离功能组件；解码时评估操控向量比预填充代理更可靠，具备更强的下游部署价值。

Conclusion: 解码阶段存在一个任务通用的低维共享子空间，是模型决策的关键因果通道。该子空间虽小，但具有高杠杆效应，可作为理解与控制大模型推理过程的重要工具，为激活操控和模型解释提供新思路。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) handle many tasks with one set of parameters, but under KV-cached inference it is unclear what task-general structure, if any, is used at decode time rather than during prefill. We propose DecodeShare, a protocol that identifies a low-dimensional subspace consistently shared across tasks in decode-time hidden states, and then tests its causal role by removing that subspace only during decoding. In our experiments, disturbing the discovered shared subspace degrades decision performance far more than disturbing either a prefill-derived or random subspace under the same intervention budget. We further show this decode-shared subspace has practical consequences for activation steering: common steering directions can overlap the task-general decode channel. Projecting out this shared subspace directly separates the functional roles of the two components, while evaluating steering vectors at decode-time yields more reliable signal for downstream deployment than prefill-based proxies. Despite its compactness, the shared subspace can serve as a high-leverage causal channel at decode time. Code is available at: https://github.com/Zishan-Shao/decodeshare.git.

</details>

Method: 提出PlanE框架，包含数据分解、指令微调和提示推理三阶段；引入DTI规划器，根据数据集特性自动选择最优基础模型及其微调与推理组合。

Result: 在不同数据集上使用相同基础模型，以及在相同数据集上使用不同基础模型时，PlanE均表现出优异性能；DTI规划器在多种优化目标下具备良好泛化能力。

Conclusion: PlanE框架有效提升了LLM在特定任务上的表现，结合DTI规划器可显著提高模型构建效率，具有良好的通用性和实用性。

Abstract: Enhancing the task-specific capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs) primarily requires substantial instruction-tuning datasets. To address the above issues, we propose a \textbf{Plan}ning framework for constructing \textbf{E}xtractive-based LLMs called \textbf{PlanE}, which includes data decomposition, instruction tuning, and prompt inference. Additionally, we introduce a Data-Tuning-Inference (DTI) planner, aimed at selecting the optimal base-LLM and its DTI combinations for specific datasets to improve construction efficiency. The experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of our PlanE from two views: (1) across different datasets using the same base-LLM, and (2) on the same dataset using different base-LLMs. Furthermore, we validate the generalizability of the proposed DTI planner under different optimization objectives. ### [293] [Benchmarking the Personalization Capabilities of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20471)
*Ashutosh Srivastava,Siddharth Yedlapati,Vinay Aggarwal,Yaman Kumar Singla,Shashwat Dixit,Jitendra Ajmera,Balaji Krishnamurthy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究将Kamenica和Gentzkow（2011）的贝叶斯说服框架应用于生成式智能体，构建了面向销售场景的个性化评估基准SDR-Bench，包含6,279条跨22个行业的客户成功案例。通过时间受限模拟避免未来数据泄露，发现当前前沿大模型与深度研究代理在个人化表现上存在持续瓶颈，且在财富100强科技企业样本中无模型能显著区分成功与失败的销售接触。实地部署验证显示48%的模型生成内容被专业销售代表认为立即可用，资深专家评分一致性达皮尔逊相关系数0.82。研究公开发布SDR-Arena与SDR-Bench以支持可复现的大规模生成式个性化研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统个性化研究关注发送方对特定接收方的行为影响，但现有大语言模型（LLM）评估多聚焦于发送方适应性，缺乏对生成消息是否真正诱导第三方行动的系统性测试。尤其在真实销售场景中，接收者行为数据可追踪，为量化评估提供了可能，因此亟需一个可重复、可扩展的基准来检验生成式模型在经典双人互动情境下的个性化能力。

Method: 基于贝叶斯说服理论构建生成式代理的个性化建模框架；设计时间约束仿真环境以防止未来信息泄露；利用真实销售记录构建大规模公开数据集SDR-Bench；通过对比不同模型在真实业务场景中的表现，评估其个性化效果；结合人工评估与专家一致性分析验证结果可靠性。

Result: 所有前沿模型均表现出个人化性能的平台期，在财富100强科技企业样本中无一统计上显著优于其他模型；现场部署表明48%的模型生成内容被评价为立即可用，专家评分一致性较高（Pearson 0.82）；证实了所提框架的有效性和可推广性。

Conclusion: 当前大语言模型在经典意义上的个性化任务中已达到性能瓶颈，单纯提升模型规模或训练策略难以突破。研究提出的新基准（SDR-Bench与SDR-Arena）为可复现、规模化评估生成式个性化提供了基础设施，推动该领域向更严谨、更贴近真实应用的方向发展。

Abstract: Personalization, the act of varying a message to induce action from a specific receiver while keeping sender, channel, and time fixed, has a long tradition in psychology and marketing as a two-party problem in which sender and receiver have independent objectives. Large language models remove the bounded-inventory constraint of classical retrieval-and-ranking approaches by generating a continuum of message variants conditioned on inferred receiver state, raising the question of how well current models perform personalization in the classical sense. Existing LLM personalization benchmarks measure sender-side adaptation, in which the receiver is the same user the model is serving. The two-party question, whether a generated message induces its intended action in a third party, has been investigated only through A/B tests and small-scale human studies that cannot be re-run against a new model on demand. We adapt the Bayesian Persuasion framework of Kamenica and Gentzkow (2011) to generative agents and instantiate the formulation in sales, where receiver actions are routinely logged against the outreach that induced them. We release SDR-Bench, a public corpus of 6,279 customer success stories spanning 22 industries and approximately 200 enterprises, served through a temporally constrained simulation that prevents future-data leakage. Across frontier LLMs and deep-research agents, we observe a consistent personalization plateau and on a Fortune 100 tech cohort no model statistically separates successful from unsuccessful outreach. A field deployment with 12 professional sales representatives validates the framework, with 48 percent of model-generated content rated immediately useful and senior-expert agreement at Pearson 0.82. We release SDR-Arena and SDR-Bench publicly to support reproducible study of generative personalization at scale.

### [294] [Robust Critics: Defending LLMs Against Multi-Turn Attacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20472)
*Roman Belaire,Arunesh Sinha,Pradeep Varakantham*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Dialogue Critic Guided Sampling (DCGS)框架，通过在对话每一轮中推断用户意图，解决大语言模型安全中的意图模糊问题。DCGS将对抗性对话建模为马尔可夫决策过程，利用基于价值和后悔的批评者在词元和话语层面评分候选回复，实现推理时重加权，逼近指数倾斜，保证有限候选池下期望回报提升。在CARES-18k、WildJailbreak、Redbench和Harmbench上优于强基线与前沿模型，并可无微调迁移至其他模型提升鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全框架对有害对话采用上下文老虎机处理方式，忽视对话轨迹，无法有效区分恶意攻击与善意误解，导致误伤或被绕过。多轮对话中攻击意图可能逐步显现，需动态推断用户真实意图以提升安全性与可用性平衡。

Method: 将对抗性对话建模为马尔可夫决策过程，设计基于价值和后悔的双层批评者（词元级与话语级），通过行动价值批评者对候选回复进行评分；采用推理时重加权机制，近似指数倾斜，优化响应生成策略。

Result: 在CARES-18k、WildJailbreak、Redbench和Harmbench等多个对抗性对话数据集上，DCGS显著优于现有强基线与前沿模型；具备良好的迁移能力，无需微调即可提升其他大模型的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: DCGS通过动态推断用户意图并基于对话历史调整响应生成，在保障安全性的同时减少对合法用户的误伤，为构建更智能、更适应性的语言模型安全机制提供了新范式。

Abstract: When a user asks a language model something harmful, is it a genuine attack or a misunderstood but well-meaning question? This ambiguity is one of the central challenges of LLM safety. A model that assumes the worst harms legitimate users; one that assumes the best is easily exploited. The problem is compounded in multi-turn dialogue, where an attacker's true intent may only reveal itself gradually across many exchanges, yet existing safety frameworks apply a contextual bandit treatment, ignoring the trajectory of the conversation.
  To that end, we propose Dialogue Critic Guided Sampling (DCGS), a framework that addresses this by inferring user intent at every turn of dialogue. Instead of applying a fixed rule about what is or is not safe, DCGS learns what the user's intent is likely to be based on the full conversational history and generates responses accordingly. Formally, we model adversarial dialogue as a Markov Decision Process and learn value and regret-based critics at both the individual token and utterance (full response) levels, scoring candidate responses via an action-value critic. We prove that this inference-time reweighting approximates exponential tilting of the base policy, guaranteeing improvement in expected return for any finite candidate pool, a property that group-relative objectives do not exhibit. Evaluated on CARES-18k, WildJailbreak, Redbench, and Harmbench, DCGS outperforms strong robust baselines and frontier models on adversarial dialogue tasks. DCGS also transfers to frontier models, improving their robustness without fine-tuning.

</details>


### [295] [Incomplete Prompt Jailbreaks in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20473)
*Yeonjea Kim,Bumjin Park,Jaesik Choi*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型已开放权重并内置安全机制，但不完整提示仍可能导致模型生成有害内容。现有方法对不完整提示的防御能力有限，亟需系统性理解其触发机制并开发更有效的防护策略。

Method: 通过构建多种不完整提示模式，分析模型在不同吸引子类型下的反应行为；利用神经激活分析识别关键功能神经元，探索基于神经元层级的干预手段。

Result: 发现模型在句子未结束前普遍延迟拒绝有害请求；参数微调训练无法跨域泛化；识别出终止与延续神经元，可作为精准控制的潜在靶点。

Conclusion: 不完整提示越狱是当前大模型安全的重要挑战。仅依赖参数调整难以应对复杂场景，而基于神经元级干预的细粒度控制具有显著潜力，为未来构建更鲁棒的安全防御体系提供新方向。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly released as open-weight models with safeguards against harmful requests. Nevertheless, sentence completion remains vulnerable to incomplete harmful prompts. In this work, we formalize this phenomenon as incomplete prompt jailbreaks (IPJ) and provide a systematic empirical characterization of when and how incomplete prompts elicit harmful continuations. We analyze diverse attractor types associated with incomplete sentence continuation and show that LLMs systematically delay refusal until sentence termination. We further demonstrate that training models to refuse incomplete harmful prompts via parameter tuning is insufficient, failing to generalize across both content domains and attractor types. To enable fine-grained control, we identify two functional neurons: termination and continuation neurons. By clarifying their roles in sentence completion, we highlight the potential of neuron-level interventions for more precise and robust IPJ defenses.

### [296] [VeriSimpl: Robust Optimization Modeling from Natural Language using Simplification-based Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20474)
*Sumaya Abdul Rahman,Seckhen Ariel Andrade Cuellar,Ghani Raissov,Mohammad Raza*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在将自然语言问题描述自动转化为可执行求解器公式时，虽能保证语法正确性，但难以确保公式真正符合预期任务目标，因此需要一种机制来验证公式的语义正确性。

Method: 提出基于简化验证的方法，通过在约束和决策变量等维度上设计简化策略，利用求解器生成诊断查询，使LLM能够以可计算的方式局部推理公式正确性，并结合全局上下文进行判断。

Result: 在多个优化基准测试中，VeriSimpl 相比现有方法显著提升了形式化准确率，并提供了高精度的自验证信号，增强了模型对错误公式的检测能力。

Conclusion: VeriSimpl 有效解决了自然语言到优化形式化中的语义一致性问题，通过简化验证机制实现了更可靠、可验证的自动建模，为未来智能优化系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: Natural language interfaces can greatly benefit the accessibility and usability of optimization modeling, and recent advances in large language models (LLMs) show promise in automatically translating textual problem descriptions into executable solver formulations. However, a key challenge for existing approaches is to ensure that the inferred formulation correctly implements the intended task, even if it may execute without errors. We introduce VeriSimpl, a solver LLM framework for robust natural-language-to-optimization formalization. Our approach is based on the idea of simplification-based verification, where the optimization solver is leveraged to generate simplified diagnostic queries about a candidate formulation to allow the LLM to tractably reason about the correctness of the formulation with respect to the task description. We present such simplification strategies along different dimensions with respect to problem constraints and decision variables, which allow the LLM to reason locally under fixed global contexts. Evaluations on a range of optimization benchmarks show how our approach provides consistent improvements in accuracy over existing methods, while also providing a novel high-precision self-verification signal.

### [297] [SonicSampler: Unified Tile-Aware Kernels for LLM Sampling and Speculative Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20475)
*Pragaash Ponnusamy,Shivam Sahni,Jue Wang,Tri Dao*

Main category: cs.AI
